MIDST Challenge at SaTML 2025: Membership Inference over Diffusion-models-based Synthetic Tabular data
Authors: Masoumeh Shafieinejad, Xi He, Mahshid Alinoori, John Jewell, Sana Ayromlou, Wei Pang, Veronica Chatrath, Garui Sharma, Deval Pandya
First: 2026-03-19T17:42:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T17:42:46+00:00
Comments: 4 page, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Synthetic data is often perceived as a silver-bullet solution to data anonymization and privacy-preserving data publishing. Drawn from generative models like diffusion models, synthetic data is expected to preserve the statistical properties of the original dataset while remaining resilient to privacy attacks. Recent developments of diffusion models have been effective on a wide range of data types, but their privacy resilience, particularly for tabular formats, remains largely unexplored. MIDST challenge sought a quantitative evaluation of the privacy gain of synthetic tabular data generated by diffusion models, with a specific focus on its resistance to membership inference attacks (MIAs). Given the heterogeneity and complexity of tabular data, multiple target models were explored for MIAs, including diffusion models for single tables of mixed data types and multi-relational tables with interconnected constraints. MIDST inspired the development of novel black-box and white-box MIAs tailored to these target diffusion models as a key outcome, enabling a comprehensive evaluation of their privacy efficacy. The MIDST GitHub repository is available at https://github.com/VectorInstitute/MIDST
中文标题/摘要
标题：2025年SaTML的MIDST挑战：基于扩散模型的合成表格数据的成员推断
合成数据常被视为数据匿名化和隐私保护数据发布的灵丹妙药。合成数据源自生成模型，如扩散模型，预计能够保留原始数据集的统计特性，同时对隐私攻击保持韧性。最近扩散模型的发展在多种数据类型上取得了有效成果，但其隐私韧性，特别是在表格格式方面，仍然 largely 未被探索。MIDST挑战旨在定量评估由扩散模型生成的合成表格数据的隐私增益，特别关注其对成员推断攻击（MIA）的抵抗力。鉴于表格数据的异质性和复杂性，探索了多种目标模型用于MIA，包括针对混合数据类型的单表扩散模型和具有相互约束的多关系表。MIDST激发了针对这些目标扩散模型开发新型黑箱和白箱MIA，作为关键成果，使其隐私有效性得以全面评估。MIDST GitHub库可在 https://github.com/VectorInstitute/MIDST 获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of ensuring privacy in synthetic data generated by diffusion models, which are increasingly used for data anonymization. The study evaluates the privacy resilience of synthetic tabular data against membership inference attacks (MIAs) by exploring various target models, including those for single and multi-relational tables. Key findings indicate that novel MIAs, both black-box and white-box, were developed specifically for these diffusion models, providing a comprehensive assessment of their effectiveness in preserving privacy.
本研究的动机在于评估由扩散模型生成的合成表格数据在抵御成员推断攻击方面的隐私韧性。研究采用定量方法评估这些攻击的多种目标模型的有效性，包括单表和多关系表。主要发现是开发了专门针对扩散模型的新型黑箱和白箱成员推断攻击，这为合成表格数据的隐私有效性提供了全面评估。
WebWeaver: Breaking Topology Confidentiality in LLM Multi-Agent Systems with Stealthy Context-Based Inference
Authors: Zixun Xiong, Gaoyi Wu, Lingfeng Yao, Miao Pan, Xiaojiang Du, Hao Wang
First: 2026-03-11T16:04:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T17:37:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Communication topology is a critical factor in the utility and safety of LLM-based multi-agent systems (LLM-MAS), making it a high-value intellectual property (IP) whose confidentiality remains insufficiently studied. Existing topology inference attempts rely on impractical assumptions, including control over the administrative agent and direct identity queries via jailbreaks, which are easily defeated by basic keyword-based defenses. As a result, prior analyses fail to capture the real-world threat of such attacks. To bridge this realism gap, we propose \textit{WebWeaver}, an attack framework that infers the complete LLM-MAS topology by compromising only a single arbitrary agent instead of the administrative agent. Unlike prior approaches, WebWeaver relies solely on agent contexts rather than agent IDs, enabling significantly stealthier inference. WebWeaver further introduces a new covert jailbreak-based mechanism and a novel fully jailbreak-free diffusion design to handle cases where jailbreaks fail. Additionally, we address a key challenge in diffusion-based inference by proposing a masking strategy that preserves known topology during diffusion, with theoretical guarantees of correctness. Extensive experiments show that WebWeaver substantially outperforms state-of-the-art (SOTA) baselines, achieving about 60\% higher inference accuracy under active defenses with negligible overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WebWeaver：在LLM多智能体系统中通过隐秘的基于上下文的推断打破拓扑保密性
通信拓扑是基于LLM的多智能体系统（LLM-MAS）效用和安全性的关键因素，使其成为一种高价值的知识产权（IP），其保密性仍然研究不足。现有的拓扑推断尝试依赖于不切实际的假设，包括对管理代理的控制和通过越狱进行的直接身份查询，这些都容易被基本的基于关键词的防御所击败。因此，之前的分析未能捕捉到此类攻击的现实威胁。为了弥补这一现实差距，我们提出了\textit{WebWeaver}，一个攻击框架，通过仅妥协一个任意代理而不是管理代理来推断完整的LLM-MAS拓扑。与之前的方法不同，WebWeaver仅依赖于代理上下文而非代理ID，从而实现显著更隐秘的推断。WebWeaver进一步引入了一种新的隐秘越狱机制和一种新颖的完全无越狱扩散设计，以处理越狱失败的情况。此外，我们通过提出一种在扩散过程中保持已知拓扑的掩蔽策略，解决了基于扩散推断的一个关键挑战，并提供了正确性的理论保证。大量实验表明，WebWeaver在主动防御下的推断准确率比最先进的基线高出约60\%，且开销微乎其微。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the insufficient study of communication topology confidentiality in LLM-based multi-agent systems (LLM-MAS), which is crucial for their utility and safety. The authors propose WebWeaver, an attack framework that infers the complete topology by compromising only a single arbitrary agent, rather than relying on impractical assumptions like controlling the administrative agent. Experimental results demonstrate that WebWeaver significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods, achieving approximately 60% higher inference accuracy under active defenses with minimal overhead.
本研究的动机在于解决LLM多智能体系统中通信拓扑保密性不足的问题，这对其效用和安全性至关重要。作者提出了一种名为WebWeaver的新攻击框架，通过仅攻陷一个任意代理来推断完整的拓扑，而不是依赖于控制管理代理的非现实假设。实验结果表明，WebWeaver在现有方法中表现显著优越，在主动防御下实现了约60%的推断准确率提升，同时保持了极小的开销。
On Optimizing Multimodal Jailbreaks for Spoken Language Models
Authors: Aravind Krishnan, Karolina Stańczak, Dietrich Klakow
First: 2026-03-19T16:48:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T16:48:28+00:00
Comments: Under Review at INTERSPEECH 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As Spoken Language Models (SLMs) integrate speech and text modalities, they inherit the safety vulnerabilities of their LLM backbone and an expanded attack surface. SLMs have been previously shown to be susceptible to jailbreaking, where adversarial prompts induce harmful responses. Yet existing attacks largely remain unimodal, optimizing either text or audio in isolation. We explore gradient-based multimodal jailbreaks by introducing JAMA (Joint Audio-text Multimodal Attack), a joint multimodal optimization framework combining Greedy Coordinate Gradient (GCG) for text and Projected Gradient Descent (PGD) for audio, to simultaneously perturb both modalities. Evaluations across four state-of-the-art SLMs and four audio types demonstrate that JAMA surpasses unimodal jailbreak rate by 1.5x to 10x. We analyze the operational dynamics of this joint attack and show that a sequential approximation method makes it 4x to 6x faster. Our findings suggest that unimodal safety is insufficient for robust SLMs. The code and data are available at https://repos.lsv.uni-saarland.de/akrishnan/multimodal-jailbreak-slm
中文标题/摘要
标题：优化多模态越狱针对语音语言模型
随着语音语言模型（SLMs）整合语音和文本模态，它们继承了其大型语言模型（LLM）基础的安全漏洞和扩展的攻击面。研究表明，SLMs 易受越狱攻击，恶意提示会引发有害响应。然而，现有攻击大多是单模态的，分别优化文本或音频。我们通过引入 JAMA（联合音频-文本多模态攻击）探索基于梯度的多模态越狱，这是一种结合贪婪坐标梯度（GCG）用于文本和投影梯度下降（PGD）用于音频的联合多模态优化框架，以同时扰动两种模态。对四种最先进的 SLM 和四种音频类型的评估表明，JAMA 的越狱成功率比单模态高 1.5 倍到 10 倍。我们分析了这种联合攻击的操作动态，并表明顺序近似方法使其速度提高了 4 倍到 6 倍。我们的研究结果表明，单模态安全性不足以保证 SLM 的稳健性。代码和数据可在 https://repos.lsv.uni-saarland.de/akrishnan/multimodal-jailbreak-slm 获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the safety vulnerabilities of Spoken Language Models (SLMs), which are susceptible to jailbreaking attacks that exploit their integration of speech and text modalities. The authors introduce JAMA (Joint Audio-text Multimodal Attack), a novel framework that employs a combination of Greedy Coordinate Gradient for text and Projected Gradient Descent for audio to optimize attacks across both modalities simultaneously. Experimental results indicate that JAMA significantly outperforms unimodal approaches, achieving a jailbreak rate that is 1.5x to 10x higher, while also demonstrating a sequential approximation method that enhances attack speed by 4x to 6x, highlighting the inadequacy of unimodal safety measures for robust SLMs.
本研究的动机在于解决口语语言模型（SLMs）的安全漏洞，这些模型容易受到利用语音和文本模态的越狱攻击。作者提出了JAMA（联合音频-文本多模态攻击），这是一种新颖的框架，结合了文本的贪婪坐标梯度和音频的投影梯度下降，以同时优化两种模态的攻击。实验结果表明，JAMA显著提高了越狱成功率，相比单模态攻击提高了1.5到10倍，而序列近似方法使攻击速度提高了4到6倍，表明单模态安全措施不足以确保SLMs的稳健性。
FedTrident: Resilient Road Condition Classification Against Poisoning Attacks in Federated Learning
Authors: Sheng Liu, Panos Papadimitratos
First: 2026-03-19T16:26:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T16:26:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
FL has emerged as a transformative paradigm for ITS, notably camera-based Road Condition Classification (RCC). However, by enabling collaboration, FL-based RCC exposes the system to adversarial participants launching Targeted Label-Flipping Attacks (TLFAs). Malicious clients (vehicles) can relabel their local training data (e.g., from an actual uneven road to a wrong smooth road), consequently compromising global model predictions and jeopardizing transportation safety. Existing countermeasures against such poisoning attacks fail to maintain resilient model performance near the necessary attack-free levels in various attack scenarios due to: 1) not tailoring poisoned local model detection to TLFAs, 2) not excluding malicious vehicular clients based on historical behavior, and 3) not remedying the already-corrupted global model after exclusion. To close this research gap, we propose FedTrident, which introduces: 1) neuron-wise analysis for local model misbehavior detection (notably including attack goal identification, critical feature extraction, and GMM-based model clustering and filtering); 2) adaptive client rating for client exclusion according to the local model detection results in each FL round; and 3) machine unlearning for corrupted global model remediation once malicious clients are excluded during FL. Extensive evaluation across diverse FL-RCC models, tasks, and configurations demonstrates that FedTrident can effectively thwart TLFAs, achieving performance comparable to that in attack-free scenarios and outperforming eight baseline countermeasures by 9.49% and 4.47% for the two most critical metrics. Moreover, FedTrident is resilient to various malicious client rates, data heterogeneity levels, complicated multi-task, and dynamic attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FedTrident：针对联邦学习中毒攻击的鲁棒道路状况分类
联邦学习（FL）已成为智能交通系统（ITS）的变革性范式，特别是在基于摄像头的道路状况分类（RCC）中。然而，通过促进协作，基于FL的RCC使系统暴露于发起定向标签翻转攻击（TLFAs）的对抗参与者。恶意客户端（车辆）可以重新标记其本地训练数据（例如，将实际不平坦的道路标记为错误的平坦道路），从而损害全球模型预测并危及交通安全。现有针对这种中毒攻击的对策未能在各种攻击场景中保持接近必要的无攻击水平的鲁棒模型性能，原因包括：1）未针对TLFAs定制中毒本地模型检测，2）未根据历史行为排除恶意车辆客户端，3）未在排除后修复已损坏的全球模型。为填补这一研究空白，我们提出了FedTrident，提出了：1）用于本地模型异常行为检测的神经元级分析（特别包括攻击目标识别、关键特征提取和基于GMM的模型聚类与过滤）；2）根据每轮FL的本地模型检测结果进行客户端排除的自适应客户端评分；3）在FL中排除恶意客户端后，对损坏的全球模型进行机器遗忘。对多种FL-RCC模型、任务和配置的广泛评估表明，FedTrident能够有效抵御TLFAs，其性能可与无攻击场景相媲美，并在两个最关键的指标上超越八个基线对策，分别提高9.49%和4.47%。此外，FedTrident对各种恶意客户端比例、数据异质性水平、复杂的多任务和动态攻击具有鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the vulnerabilities of federated learning-based road condition classification systems to targeted label-flipping attacks, which can compromise transportation safety. The authors propose a method called FedTrident, which includes neuron-wise analysis for detecting local model misbehavior, adaptive client rating for excluding malicious clients, and machine unlearning to remediate corrupted global models. Experimental results show that FedTrident effectively mitigates targeted label-flipping attacks, achieving performance levels comparable to attack-free scenarios and surpassing eight baseline countermeasures by 9.49% and 4.47% for the two most critical metrics, while also demonstrating resilience against various attack conditions.
本研究的动机在于解决基于联邦学习的道路状况分类系统在面对目标标签翻转攻击时的脆弱性，这种攻击可能危及交通安全。作者提出了一种名为FedTrident的方法，包括神经元级分析以检测本地模型的不当行为、自适应客户评级以排除恶意客户，以及机器遗忘以修复全球模型。实验结果表明，FedTrident有效减轻了目标标签翻转攻击，达到了与无攻击场景相似的性能水平，并在关键指标上超越了八个基线对策，分别提高了9.49%和4.47%，同时在各种攻击条件和数据异质性下保持了韧性。
Functional Subspace Watermarking for Large Language Models
Authors: Zikang Ding, Junhao Li, Suling Wu, Junchi Yao, Hongbo Liu, Lijie Hu
First: 2026-03-19T11:44:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T11:44:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model watermarking utilizes internal representations to protect the ownership of large language models (LLMs). However, these features inevitably undergo complex distortions during realistic model modifications such as fine-tuning, quantization, or knowledge distillation, making reliable extraction extremely challenging. Despite extensive research on model-side watermarking, existing methods still lack sufficient robustness against parameter-level perturbations. To address this gap, we propose \texttt{\textbf{Functional Subspace Watermarking (FSW)}}, a framework that anchors ownership signals into a low-dimensional functional backbone. Specifically, we first solve a generalized eigenvalue problem to extract a stable functional subspace for watermark injection, while introducing an adaptive spectral truncation strategy to achieve an optimal balance between robustness and model utility. Furthermore, a vector consistency constraint is incorporated to ensure that watermark injection does not compromise the original semantic performance. Extensive experiments across various LLM architectures and datasets demonstrate that our method achieves superior detection accuracy and statistical verifiability under multiple model attacks, maintaining robustness that outperforms existing state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型的功能子空间水印
模型水印利用内部表示来保护大型语言模型（LLMs）的所有权。然而，这些特征在现实模型修改（如微调、量化或知识蒸馏）过程中不可避免地经历复杂的扭曲，使得可靠提取极具挑战性。尽管在模型侧水印方面进行了广泛研究，但现有方法在参数级扰动下仍缺乏足够的鲁棒性。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了\texttt{\textbf{功能子空间水印（FSW）}}，一个将所有权信号锚定到低维功能骨架的框架。具体而言，我们首先解决一个广义特征值问题，以提取用于水印注入的稳定功能子空间，同时引入自适应谱截断策略，以实现鲁棒性与模型实用性之间的最佳平衡。此外，加入了向量一致性约束，以确保水印注入不会损害原始语义性能。在各种LLM架构和数据集上的广泛实验表明，我们的方法在多种模型攻击下实现了优越的检测准确性和统计可验证性，保持了超越现有最先进（SOTA）方法的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enhance the robustness of model watermarking for large language models (LLMs), which face challenges in reliably extracting ownership signals due to distortions from modifications like fine-tuning and quantization. The authors propose a novel approach called Functional Subspace Watermarking (FSW), which involves solving a generalized eigenvalue problem to create a stable functional subspace for watermark injection, complemented by an adaptive spectral truncation strategy to balance robustness and model utility. Experimental results show that FSW significantly improves detection accuracy and statistical verifiability against various model attacks, outperforming existing state-of-the-art methods in maintaining robustness.
本研究旨在解决大型语言模型（LLMs）所有权保护中的挑战，尤其是模型水印技术在微调和量化等修改过程中面临的失真问题。作者提出了一种新的框架，称为功能子空间水印（FSW），该框架通过解决广义特征值问题来创建一个稳定的功能子空间用于水印注入，并采用自适应谱截断策略以平衡鲁棒性和模型效用。实验结果表明，FSW在不同LLM架构和数据集上相比现有方法具有更高的检测准确性和统计可验证性，并在多种模型攻击下展现出更强的鲁棒性。
SIA: A Synthesize-Inject-Align Framework for Knowledge-Grounded and Secure E-commerce Search LLMs with Industrial Deployment
Authors: Zhouwei Zhai, Mengxiang Chen, Anmeng Zhang
First: 2026-03-17T05:41:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T08:59:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models offer transformative potential for e-commerce search by enabling intent-aware recommendations. However, their industrial deployment is hindered by two critical challenges: (1) knowledge hallucination due to insufficient encoding of dynamic, fine-grained product knowledge, and (2) security vulnerabilities under jailbreak attacks that threaten compliance. To address these issues, we propose SIA--a Synthesize-Inject-Align framework for building knowledgeable and secure e-commerce search LLMs. Our approach first synthesizes high-quality natural language corpus by combining structured knowledge graphs with unstructured behavioral logs, augmented with reasoning chains and safety-aware data. We then introduce a parameter-efficient pre-training strategy based on Depth Up-Scaling to inject domain knowledge while preserving general capabilities. Finally, a dual-path alignment method via multi-task instruction tuning and adversarial training strengthens both task performance and safety robustness. The framework has been deployed at JD.com, China's largest self-operated e-commerce platform, where A/B tests across five core search scenarios demonstrate significant improvements in key business metrics, validating its industrial effectiveness and scalability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SIA：一个用于知识驱动和安全电子商务搜索LLM的合成-注入-对齐框架，具有工业部署
大型语言模型通过实现意图感知推荐，为电子商务搜索提供了变革性潜力。然而，它们的工业部署受到两个关键挑战的阻碍：（1）由于动态、细粒度产品知识编码不足而导致的知识幻觉，以及（2）在越狱攻击下的安全漏洞，威胁合规性。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了SIA——一个用于构建知识丰富和安全的电子商务搜索LLM的合成-注入-对齐框架。我们的方法首先通过将结构化知识图与非结构化行为日志相结合，合成高质量的自然语言语料库，并增强推理链和安全意识数据。然后，我们引入了一种基于深度上升的参数高效预训练策略，以在保留通用能力的同时注入领域知识。最后，通过多任务指令调优和对抗训练的双路径对齐方法，增强了任务性能和安全鲁棒性。该框架已在中国最大的自营电子商务平台京东部署，在五个核心搜索场景中的A/B测试显示关键业务指标显著改善，验证了其工业有效性和可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enhance the deployment of large language models for e-commerce search, addressing challenges such as knowledge hallucination and security vulnerabilities. The authors propose the SIA framework, which synthesizes a high-quality natural language corpus from structured knowledge graphs and unstructured behavioral logs, and employs a parameter-efficient pre-training strategy to inject domain knowledge. Key experimental findings from A/B tests at JD.com indicate significant improvements in key business metrics across five core search scenarios, demonstrating the framework's effectiveness and scalability in an industrial setting.
本研究的动机是通过解决知识幻觉和安全漏洞来增强大型语言模型在电子商务搜索中的应用。作者提出了合成-注入-对齐（SIA）框架，该框架通过结合结构化知识图谱和非结构化行为日志来合成高质量的自然语言语料库，并采用参数高效的预训练策略来注入领域知识。对京东进行的A/B测试结果显示，在五个核心搜索场景中关键业务指标显著改善，验证了该框架在工业环境中的有效性和可扩展性。
Attack by Unlearning: Unlearning-Induced Adversarial Attacks on Graph Neural Networks
Authors: Jiahao Zhang, Yilong Wang, Suhang Wang
First: 2026-03-19T07:30:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T07:30:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph neural networks (GNNs) are widely used for learning from graph-structured data in domains such as social networks, recommender systems, and financial platforms. To comply with privacy regulations like the GDPR, CCPA, and PIPEDA, approximate graph unlearning, which aims to remove the influence of specific data points from trained models without full retraining, has become an increasingly important component of trustworthy graph learning. However, approximate unlearning often incurs subtle performance degradation, which may incur negative and unintended side effects. In this work, we show that such degradations can be amplified into adversarial attacks. We introduce the notion of \textbf{unlearning corruption attacks}, where an adversary injects carefully chosen nodes into the training graph and later requests their deletion. Because deletion requests are legally mandated and cannot be denied, this attack surface is both unavoidable and stealthy: the model performs normally during training, but accuracy collapses only after unlearning is applied. Technically, we formulate this attack as a bi-level optimization problem: to overcome the challenges of black-box unlearning and label scarcity, we approximate the unlearning process via gradient-based updates and employ a surrogate model to generate pseudo-labels for the optimization. Extensive experiments across benchmarks and unlearning algorithms demonstrate that small, carefully designed unlearning requests can induce significant accuracy degradation, raising urgent concerns about the robustness of GNN unlearning under real-world regulatory demands. The source code will be released upon paper acceptance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过反学习进行攻击：基于反学习的图神经网络对抗攻击
图神经网络（GNN）广泛用于从社交网络、推荐系统和金融平台等图结构数据中学习。为了遵守GDPR、CCPA和PIPEDA等隐私法规，近似图反学习旨在在不进行完全重训练的情况下，消除特定数据点对训练模型的影响，已成为可信图学习中越来越重要的组成部分。然而，近似反学习往往会导致微妙的性能下降，这可能会带来负面和意想不到的副作用。在本研究中，我们展示了这种下降可以被放大为对抗攻击。我们引入了“反学习腐败攻击”的概念，其中对手将精心选择的节点注入训练图中，并随后请求删除它们。由于删除请求是法律强制的，无法拒绝，因此这一攻击面既不可避免又隐蔽：模型在训练期间表现正常，但在应用反学习后准确性会崩溃。从技术上讲，我们将此攻击形式化为一个双层优化问题：为了克服黑箱反学习和标签稀缺的挑战，我们通过基于梯度的更新近似反学习过程，并采用代理模型生成伪标签以进行优化。针对基准和反学习算法的广泛实验表明，小而精心设计的反学习请求可以导致显著的准确性下降，提出了关于GNN反学习在现实世界监管要求下的鲁棒性的重要担忧。源代码将在论文接受后发布。

The authors propose a novel attack method termed unlearning corruption attacks, where adversaries strategically inject nodes into the training graph and subsequently request their deletion, exploiting the legal obligation to comply with such requests. Experimental results reveal that these unlearning requests, even when small and carefully designed, can cause significant accuracy degradation in GNNs, highlighting serious concerns regarding the robustness of unlearning processes in compliance with real-world regulations.

CausalVAD: De-confounding End-to-End Autonomous Driving via Causal Intervention
Authors: Jiacheng Tang, Zhiyuan Zhou, Zhuolin He, Jia Zhang, Kai Zhang, Jian Pu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-19T07:21:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T07:21:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Planning-oriented end-to-end driving models show great promise, yet they fundamentally learn statistical correlations instead of true causal relationships. This vulnerability leads to causal confusion, where models exploit dataset biases as shortcuts, critically harming their reliability and safety in complex scenarios. To address this, we introduce CausalVAD, a de-confounding training framework that leverages causal intervention. At its core, we design the sparse causal intervention scheme (SCIS), a lightweight, plug-and-play module to instantiate the backdoor adjustment theory in neural networks. SCIS constructs a dictionary of prototypes representing latent driving contexts. It then uses this dictionary to intervene on the model's sparse vectorized queries. This step actively eliminates spurious associations induced by confounders, thereby eliminating spurious factors from the representations for downstream tasks. Extensive experiments on benchmarks like nuScenes show CausalVAD achieves state-of-the-art planning accuracy and safety. Furthermore, our method demonstrates superior robustness against both data bias and noisy scenarios configured to induce causal confusion.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CausalVAD：通过因果干预去混淆的端到端自主驾驶
以规划为导向的端到端驾驶模型展现出巨大的潜力，但它们从根本上学习的是统计相关性而非真实的因果关系。这一脆弱性导致了因果混淆，模型利用数据集偏差作为捷径，严重损害了其在复杂场景中的可靠性和安全性。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了CausalVAD，一个利用因果干预的去混淆训练框架。其核心是设计稀疏因果干预方案（SCIS），这是一个轻量级的即插即用模块，用于在神经网络中实例化后门调整理论。SCIS构建了一个原型字典，代表潜在的驾驶上下文。然后，它使用这个字典对模型的稀疏向量查询进行干预。这一步主动消除由混淆因素引起的虚假关联，从而消除下游任务表示中的虚假因素。在nuScenes等基准上的大量实验表明，CausalVAD实现了最先进的规划准确性和安全性。此外，我们的方法在抵御数据偏差和噪声场景引起的因果混淆方面表现出更强的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to improve the reliability and safety of end-to-end autonomous driving models, which often rely on statistical correlations rather than true causal relationships, leading to causal confusion. The authors propose CausalVAD, a de-confounding training framework that employs a sparse causal intervention scheme (SCIS) to implement backdoor adjustment theory in neural networks. Experimental results on benchmarks such as nuScenes indicate that CausalVAD achieves state-of-the-art planning accuracy and safety while also demonstrating enhanced robustness against data bias and noisy scenarios that can induce causal confusion.
本研究的动机在于提高端到端自动驾驶模型的可靠性和安全性，这些模型往往依赖统计相关性而非真实因果关系，从而导致因果混淆。作者提出了CausalVAD，这是一种去混淆训练框架，采用稀疏因果干预方案（SCIS）在神经网络中应用因果干预。对nuScenes等基准的实验结果表明，CausalVAD在规划准确性和安全性方面达到了最先进的水平，同时在应对数据偏差和设计用于诱导因果混淆的场景方面表现出更强的鲁棒性。
Beyond Passive Aggregation: Active Auditing and Topology-Aware Defense in Decentralized Federated Learning
Authors: Sheng Pan, Niansheng Tang
First: 2026-03-19T06:46:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T06:46:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decentralized Federated Learning (DFL) remains highly vulnerable to adaptive backdoor attacks designed to bypass traditional passive defense metrics. To address this limitation, we shift the defensive paradigm toward a novel active, interventional auditing framework. First, we establish a dynamical model to characterize the spatiotemporal diffusion of adversarial updates across complex graph topologies. Second, we introduce a suite of proactive auditing metrics, stochastic entropy anomaly, randomized smoothing Kullback-Leibler divergence, and activation kurtosis. These metrics utilize private probes to stress-test local models, effectively exposing latent backdoors that remain invisible to conventional static detection. Furthermore, we implement a topology-aware defense placement strategy to maximize global aggregation resilience. We provide theoretical property for the system's convergence under co-evolving attack and defense dynamics. Numeric empirical evaluations across diverse architectures demonstrate that our active framework is highly competitive with state-of-the-art defenses in mitigating stealthy, adaptive backdoors while preserving primary task utility.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越被动聚合：去中心化联邦学习中的主动审计与拓扑感知防御
去中心化联邦学习（DFL）仍然高度脆弱于旨在绕过传统被动防御指标的自适应后门攻击。为了解决这一局限性，我们将防御范式转向一种新颖的主动干预审计框架。首先，我们建立了一个动态模型，以表征对抗性更新在复杂图拓扑中的时空扩散。其次，我们引入了一套主动审计指标，包括随机熵异常、随机平滑的Kullback-Leibler散度和激活峰度。这些指标利用私有探针对本地模型进行压力测试，有效揭示传统静态检测无法察觉的潜在后门。此外，我们实施了一种拓扑感知的防御部署策略，以最大化全局聚合的韧性。我们提供了系统在共同演化攻击和防御动态下收敛的理论性质。针对多种架构的数值实证评估表明，我们的主动框架在减轻隐秘的自适应后门方面与最先进的防御方案高度竞争，同时保持主要任务的效用。

The research addresses the vulnerability of Decentralized Federated Learning (DFL) to adaptive backdoor attacks that can evade traditional defenses. The authors propose an active auditing framework that includes a dynamical model to analyze the spread of adversarial updates in complex graph topologies and introduce new proactive auditing metrics to detect hidden backdoors. Experimental results show that this active approach significantly enhances resilience against stealthy attacks while maintaining the utility of the primary task, outperforming existing state-of-the-art defenses.

AJAR: Adaptive Jailbreak Architecture for Red-teaming
Authors: Yipu Dou, Wang Yang
First: 2026-01-16T03:30:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T05:58:01+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 3 figures. Code and data available at https://github.com/douyipu/ajar
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) safety evaluation is moving from content moderation to action security as modern systems gain persistent state, tool access, and autonomous control loops. Existing jailbreak frameworks still leave a gap between adaptive multi-turn attacks and agentic runtimes: attack algorithms are usually packaged as monolithic scripts, while agent harnesses rarely expose explicit abstractions for rollback, tool simulation, or strategy switching. We present AJAR, a red-teaming framework that exposes multi-turn jailbreak algorithms as callable MCP services and lets an Auditor Agent orchestrate them inside a tool-aware runtime built on Petri. AJAR integrates three representative attacks, namely Crescendo, ActorAttack, and X-Teaming, under a shared service interface for planning, prompt generation, optimization, evaluation, and context control. On 200 HarmBench validation behaviors, AJAR improves X-Teaming from 65.0% to 76.0% attack success rate (ASR), reaches 80% cumulative success one turn earlier than the native implementation, and reproduces Crescendo more effectively than PyRIT (91.0% vs. 87.5% ASR). Behavior-level analysis shows that these gains are concentrated in hard categories and frequently depend on rollback-enabled transcript repair. We further show that tool access reshapes rather than uniformly enlarges the attack surface: ActorAttack rises from 51.0% to 56.0% ASR with tools, whereas Crescendo drops from 91.0% to 78.0% and X-Teaming from 76.0% to 55.5%, with the sharpest declines appearing in categories that rely on long semantic buildup. These results position AJAR as a practical foundation for evaluating multi-turn jailbreaks under realistic agent constraints. Code and data are available at https://github.com/douyipu/ajar.

大型语言模型（LLM）的安全评估正从内容审核转向行动安全，因为现代系统获得了持久状态、工具访问和自主控制循环。现有的越狱框架仍然在适应性多轮攻击和代理运行时之间存在差距：攻击算法通常被打包为单一脚本，而代理工具很少提供回滚、工具模拟或策略切换的明确抽象。我们提出了AJAR，一个红队框架，它将多轮越狱算法暴露为可调用的MCP服务，并让审计代理在基于Petri构建的工具感知运行时中协调它们。AJAR集成了三种代表性攻击，即Crescendo、ActorAttack和X-Teaming，提供共享服务接口用于规划、提示生成、优化、评估和上下文控制。在200个HarmBench验证行为上，AJAR将X-Teaming的攻击成功率（ASR）从65.0%提高到76.0%，比原生实现提前一轮达到80%的累积成功率，并且比PyRIT更有效地重现Crescendo（91.0%对87.5% ASR）。行为级分析表明，这些增益集中在困难类别，并且通常依赖于启用回滚的转录修复。我们进一步表明，工具访问重塑而非均匀扩大攻击面：ActorAttack在使用工具时从51.0%上升到56.0% ASR，而Crescendo从91.0%下降到78.0%，X-Teaming从76.0%下降到55.5%，在依赖于长语义构建的类别中出现最明显的下降。这些结果将AJAR定位为在现实代理约束下评估多轮越狱的实用基础。代码和数据可在https://github.com/douyipu/ajar获取。

The authors developed AJAR, a red-teaming framework that presents multi-turn jailbreak algorithms as callable MCP services, allowing an Auditor Agent to manage them within a tool-aware runtime based on Petri nets. Experimental results demonstrate that AJAR significantly improves the attack success rate of X-Teaming from 65.0% to 76.0%, achieves 80% cumulative success one turn earlier than the native implementation, and outperforms PyRIT in reproducing Crescendo with a 91.0% attack success rate, while also revealing that tool access affects the attack surface variably across different attack types.

Membership Inference Attack against Large Language Model-based Recommendation Systems: A New Distillation-based Paradigm
Authors: Li Cuihong, Huang Xiaowen, Yin Chuanhuan, Sang Jitao
First: 2025-09-16T09:36:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T05:41:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Membership Inference Attack (MIA) aims to determine whether a specific data sample was included in the training dataset of a target model. Traditional MIA approaches rely on shadow models to mimic target model behavior, but their effectiveness diminishes for Large Language Model (LLM)-based recommendation systems due to the scale and complexity of training data. This paper introduces a novel knowledge distillation-based MIA paradigm tailored for LLM-based recommendation systems. Our method constructs a reference model via distillation, applying distinct strategies for member and non-member data to enhance discriminative capabilities. The paradigm extracts fused features (e.g., confidence, entropy, loss, and hidden layer vectors) from the reference model to train an attack model, overcoming limitations of individual features. Extensive experiments on extended datasets (Last.FM, MovieLens, Book-Crossing, Delicious) and diverse LLMs (T5, GPT-2, LLaMA3) demonstrate that our approach significantly outperforms shadow model-based MIAs and individual-feature baselines. The results show its practicality for privacy attacks in LLM-driven recommender systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对基于大型语言模型的推荐系统的成员推断攻击：一种新的基于蒸馏的范式
成员推断攻击（MIA）旨在确定特定数据样本是否包含在目标模型的训练数据集中。传统的MIA方法依赖于影子模型来模拟目标模型的行为，但由于训练数据的规模和复杂性，这些方法在基于大型语言模型（LLM）的推荐系统中的有效性降低。本文介绍了一种新颖的基于知识蒸馏的MIA范式，专为基于LLM的推荐系统量身定制。我们的方法通过蒸馏构建参考模型，针对成员和非成员数据应用不同策略以增强区分能力。该范式从参考模型中提取融合特征（例如，置信度、熵、损失和隐藏层向量）来训练攻击模型，克服单一特征的局限性。在扩展数据集（Last.FM、MovieLens、Book-Crossing、Delicious）和多种LLM（T5、GPT-2、LLaMA3）上进行的广泛实验表明，我们的方法显著优于基于影子模型的MIA和单一特征基线。结果表明其在LLM驱动的推荐系统中的隐私攻击的实用性。

A Model Consistency-Based Countermeasure to GAN-Based Data Poisoning Attack in Federated Learning
Authors: Wei Sun, Bo Gao, Ke Xiong, Yuwei Wang, Pingyi Fan, Khaled Ben Letaief
First: 2024-05-19T04:23:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T04:19:58+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 16 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In federated learning (FL), although the original intention of available but not visible data is to allay data privacy concerns, it potentially brings new security threats, particularly poisoning attacks that target such not visible local data. Intuitively, such data poisoning attacks have great potential in stealthily degrading global FL outcomes, and are expected to be even stealthier if being enhanced by generative models like generative adversarial networks (GANs). However, existing defense methods have not been thoroughly challenged in this regard and generally fail to be aware of a local generation of seemingly legitimate poisoned data. With a growing concern on potentially stealthier attacks, in this paper, a cost-effective defense mechanism named Model Consistency-Based Defense (MCD) is proposed, which offers a comprehensive examination of available local models across multiple feature dimensions, providing an indirect yet effective means of identifying hidden data poisoning attackers. To push the limit of MCD against stealthier attacks, we propose a new GAN-based data poisoning attack model named VagueGAN and an unsupervised variant of it, which can be flexibly deployed to generate seemingly legitimate but noisy poisoned data. The consistency of GAN outputs revealed by VagueGAN helps strengthen MCD to work against stealthier GAN-based attacks as well as other mainstream ones. Extensive experiments on multiple open datasets (MNIST, Fashion-MNIST, CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and Mini-Imagenet) indicate that our attack method better balances the trade-off between attack effectiveness and stealthiness with low complexity. More importantly, our defense mechanism is shown to be more competent in identifying a variety of poisoned data, particularly stealthier GAN-poisoned ones.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模型一致性的对抗GAN数据中毒攻击的联邦学习对策
在联邦学习（FL）中，虽然可用但不可见数据的初衷是缓解数据隐私问题，但它可能带来新的安全威胁，特别是针对这些不可见本地数据的中毒攻击。直观上，这种数据中毒攻击在悄悄降低全球FL结果方面具有很大潜力，并且如果通过生成对抗网络（GAN）等生成模型增强，预计会更加隐蔽。然而，现有的防御方法在这方面尚未受到彻底挑战，通常未能意识到本地生成的看似合法的中毒数据。随着对潜在更隐蔽攻击的关注增加，本文提出了一种名为基于模型一致性的防御机制（MCD），该机制对多个特征维度的可用本地模型进行了全面检查，提供了一种间接但有效的手段来识别隐藏的数据中毒攻击者。为了推动MCD在面对更隐蔽攻击时的极限，我们提出了一种新的基于GAN的数据中毒攻击模型，名为VagueGAN及其无监督变体，可以灵活部署以生成看似合法但噪声较大的中毒数据。VagueGAN揭示的GAN输出一致性有助于增强MCD对抗更隐蔽的基于GAN的攻击以及其他主流攻击的能力。在多个开放数据集（MNIST、Fashion-MNIST、CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100和Mini-Imagenet）上的大量实验表明，我们的攻击方法在攻击有效性和隐蔽性之间更好地平衡了低复杂性。更重要的是，我们的防御机制在识别各种中毒数据方面表现得更为出色，特别是更隐蔽的GAN中毒数据。

The motivation behind this research is to address the security threats posed by data poisoning attacks in federated learning, particularly those enhanced by generative adversarial networks (GANs). The authors propose a defense mechanism called Model Consistency-Based Defense (MCD), which evaluates local models across multiple feature dimensions to identify hidden data poisoning attacks. Experimental results on various datasets, including MNIST and CIFAR-10, demonstrate that the proposed MCD effectively detects a range of poisoned data, especially those generated by the new VagueGAN model, while maintaining a balance between attack effectiveness and stealthiness.
本研究的动机是解决联邦学习中数据中毒攻击带来的安全威胁，特别是那些由生成对抗网络（GAN）增强的攻击。作者提出了一种名为模型一致性防御（MCD）的防御机制，该机制通过评估多个特征维度的本地模型来检测隐藏的数据中毒。实验结果表明，新提出的基于GAN的攻击模型VagueGAN能够有效生成看似合法的中毒数据，而MCD在识别各种类型的中毒数据方面表现出更强的能力，尤其是那些更隐蔽的基于GAN的中毒数据，实验数据集包括MNIST和CIFAR-10等。
Prompt Control-Flow Integrity: A Priority-Aware Runtime Defense Against Prompt Injection in LLM Systems
Authors: Md Takrim Ul Alam, Akif Islam, Mohd Ruhul Ameen, Abu Saleh Musa Miah, Jungpil Shin
First: 2026-03-19T02:50:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-19T02:50:15+00:00
Comments: 4 Figures, 3 Tables, Submitted to the International Conference on Power, Electronics, Communications, Computing, and Intelligent Infrastructure 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) deployed behind APIs and retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) stacks are vulnerable to prompt injection attacks that may override system policies, subvert intended behavior, and induce unsafe outputs. Existing defenses often treat prompts as flat strings and rely on ad hoc filtering or static jailbreak detection. This paper proposes Prompt Control-Flow Integrity (PCFI), a priority-aware runtime defense that models each request as a structured composition of system, developer, user, and retrieved-document segments. PCFI applies a three-stage middleware pipeline, lexical heuristics, role-switch detection, and hierarchical policy enforcement, before forwarding requests to the backend LLM. We implement PCFI as a FastAPI-based gateway for deployed LLM APIs and evaluate it on a custom benchmark of synthetic and semi-realistic prompt-injection workloads. On the evaluated benchmark suite, PCFI intercepts all attack-labeled requests, maintains a 0% False Positive Rate, and introduces a median processing overhead of only 0.04 ms. These results suggest that provenance- and priority-aware prompt enforcement is a practical and lightweight defense for deployed LLM systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：提示控制流完整性：针对大型语言模型系统中提示注入的优先级感知运行时防御
部署在API和检索增强生成（RAG）堆栈后的大型语言模型（LLMs）易受提示注入攻击，这可能会覆盖系统政策、颠覆预期行为并引发不安全输出。现有防御通常将提示视为平面字符串，并依赖于临时过滤或静态越狱检测。本文提出了提示控制流完整性（PCFI），这是一种优先级感知的运行时防御，模型将每个请求视为系统、开发者、用户和检索文档段的结构化组合。PCFI应用三阶段中间件管道、词汇启发式、角色切换检测和分层政策执行，然后将请求转发到后端LLM。我们将PCFI实现为基于FastAPI的网关，用于部署的LLM API，并在自定义基准的合成和半现实提示注入工作负载上进行评估。在评估的基准套件中，PCFI拦截所有标记为攻击的请求，保持0%的误报率，并引入仅0.04毫秒的中位处理开销。这些结果表明，基于来源和优先级的提示执行是部署的LLM系统的实用且轻量级的防御。

Auditing Black-Box LLM APIs with a Rank-Based Uniformity Test
Authors: Xiaoyuan Zhu, Yaowen Ye, Tianyi Qiu, Hanlin Zhu, Sijun Tan, Ajraf Mannan, Jonathan Michala, Raluca Ada Popa, Willie Neiswanger
First: 2025-06-08T03:00:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T23:06:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As API access becomes a primary interface to large language models (LLMs), users often interact with black-box systems that offer little transparency into the deployed model. To reduce costs or maliciously alter model behaviors, API providers may discreetly serve quantized or fine-tuned variants, which can degrade performance and compromise safety. Detecting such substitutions is difficult, as users lack access to model weights and, in most cases, even output logits. To tackle this problem, we propose a rank-based uniformity test that can verify the behavioral equality of a black-box LLM to a locally deployed authentic model. Our method is accurate, query-efficient, and avoids detectable query patterns, making it robust to adversarial providers that reroute or mix responses upon the detection of testing attempts. We evaluate the approach across diverse threat scenarios, including quantization, harmful fine-tuning, jailbreak prompts, and full model substitution, showing that it consistently achieves superior statistical power over prior methods under constrained query budgets.

Revisiting Locally Differentially Private Protocols: Towards Better Trade-offs in Privacy, Utility, and Attack Resistance
Authors: Héber H. Arcolezi, Sébastien Gambs
First: 2025-03-03T12:41:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T20:47:49+00:00
Comments: Paper accepted at ICDE 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Local Differential Privacy (LDP) offers strong privacy protection, especially in settings in which the server collecting the data is untrusted. However, designing LDP mechanisms that achieve an optimal trade-off between privacy, utility and robustness to adversarial inference and integrity attacks remains challenging. In this work, we introduce a general multi-objective optimization framework for refining LDP protocols, enabling the joint optimization of privacy and utility under various adversarial settings. While our framework is flexible to accommodate multiple privacy and security attacks as well as utility metrics, in this paper, we specifically optimize for Attacker Success Rate (ASR) under \emph{data reconstruction attack} as a concrete measure of privacy leakage and Mean Squared Error (MSE) as a measure of utility. Complementarily, we evaluate integrity-oriented threats through data poisoning attacks, providing an additional adversarial perspective. More precisely, we systematically revisit these trade-offs by analyzing eight state-of-the-art LDP frequency estimation protocols and proposing refined counterparts that leverage tailored optimization techniques. Experimental results demonstrate that our proposed adaptive mechanisms consistently outperform their non-adaptive counterparts, achieving substantial reductions in ASR while preserving utility, and pushing closer to the ASR-MSE Pareto frontier. By bridging the gap between theoretical guarantees and real-world vulnerabilities, our framework enables modular and context-aware deployment of LDP mechanisms with tunable privacy-utility-attackability trade-offs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新审视局部差分隐私协议：朝着隐私、效用和攻击抵抗之间更好的权衡
局部差分隐私（LDP）提供了强大的隐私保护，特别是在收集数据的服务器不可信的情况下。然而，设计能够在隐私、效用和对抗推理及完整性攻击的鲁棒性之间实现最佳权衡的LDP机制仍然具有挑战性。在本研究中，我们引入了一个通用的多目标优化框架，用于优化LDP协议，使得在各种对抗环境下能够联合优化隐私和效用。虽然我们的框架灵活地适应多种隐私和安全攻击以及效用指标，但在本文中，我们特别针对数据重构攻击下的攻击者成功率（ASR）作为隐私泄露的具体度量，以及均方误差（MSE）作为效用的度量进行优化。此外，我们通过数据中毒攻击评估面向完整性的威胁，提供额外的对抗视角。更准确地说，我们通过分析八种最先进的LDP频率估计协议，系统地重新审视这些权衡，并提出利用定制优化技术的改进版本。实验结果表明，我们提出的自适应机制在保持效用的同时，ASR显著降低，且始终优于其非自适应对应物，向ASR-MSE帕累托前沿更进一步。通过弥合理论保证与现实世界脆弱性之间的差距，我们的框架实现了LDP机制的模块化和上下文感知部署，具有可调的隐私-效用-攻击性权衡。

The authors propose a multi-objective optimization framework that allows for the joint optimization of privacy and utility, specifically focusing on the Attacker Success Rate (ASR) in data reconstruction attacks and Mean Squared Error (MSE) for utility assessment. Experimental results indicate that the adaptive mechanisms developed in this study significantly reduce ASR while maintaining utility, outperforming non-adaptive methods and approaching the optimal ASR-MSE trade-off.
本研究的动机在于改善局部差分隐私（LDP）协议中隐私、效用和攻击抵抗之间的权衡，特别是在数据由不可信服务器收集的情况下。作者提出了一种多目标优化框架，允许在隐私和效用指标之间进行联合优化，特别关注数据重构攻击下的攻击者成功率（ASR）和效用评估的均方误差（MSE）。实验结果表明，所提出的自适应机制在保持效用的同时显著降低了ASR，优于非自适应协议，并朝着ASR-MSE帕累托前沿迈进，从而增强了LDP机制在各种对抗威胁下的实际部署能力。
OPUS-VFL: Incentivizing Optimal Privacy-Utility Tradeoffs in Vertical Federated Learning
Authors: Sindhuja Madabushi, Ahmad Faraz Khan, Haider Ali, Jin-Hee Cho
First: 2025-04-22T16:00:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T20:16:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vertical Federated Learning (VFL) enables organizations with disjoint feature spaces but shared user bases to collaboratively train models without sharing raw data. However, existing VFL systems face critical limitations: they often lack effective incentive mechanisms, struggle to balance privacy-utility tradeoffs, and fail to accommodate clients with heterogeneous resource capabilities. These challenges hinder meaningful participation, degrade model performance, and limit practical deployment. To address these issues, we propose OPUS-VFL, an Optimal Privacy-Utility tradeoff Strategy for VFL. OPUS-VFL introduces a novel, privacy-aware incentive mechanism that rewards clients based on a principled combination of model contribution, privacy preservation, and resource investment. It employs a lightweight leave-one-out (LOO) strategy to quantify feature importance per client, and integrates an adaptive differential privacy mechanism that enables clients to dynamically calibrate noise levels to optimize their individual utility. Our framework is designed to be scalable, budget-balanced, and robust to inference and poisoning attacks. Extensive experiments on benchmark datasets (MNIST, CIFAR-10, and CIFAR-100) demonstrate that OPUS-VFL significantly outperforms state-of-the-art VFL baselines in both efficiency and robustness. It reduces label inference attack success rates by up to 20%, increases feature inference reconstruction error (MSE) by over 30%, and achieves up to 25% higher incentives for clients that contribute meaningfully while respecting privacy and cost constraints. These results highlight the practicality and innovation of OPUS-VFL as a secure, fair, and performance-driven solution for real-world VFL.
中文标题/摘要

垂直联邦学习（VFL）使得具有不相交特征空间但共享用户基础的组织能够在不共享原始数据的情况下协作训练模型。然而，现有的VFL系统面临关键限制：它们往往缺乏有效的激励机制，难以平衡隐私与效用的权衡，并且无法适应具有异构资源能力的客户。这些挑战阻碍了有意义的参与，降低了模型性能，并限制了实际部署。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了OPUS-VFL，一种针对VFL的最佳隐私-效用权衡策略。OPUS-VFL引入了一种新颖的、关注隐私的激励机制，根据模型贡献、隐私保护和资源投资的原则组合来奖励客户。它采用轻量级的留一法（LOO）策略来量化每个客户的特征重要性，并集成了一种自适应差分隐私机制，使客户能够动态调整噪声水平以优化其个体效用。我们的框架旨在可扩展、预算平衡，并对推断和中毒攻击具有鲁棒性。在基准数据集（MNIST、CIFAR-10和CIFAR-100）上的大量实验表明，OPUS-VFL在效率和鲁棒性方面显著优于最先进的VFL基线。它将标签推断攻击成功率降低了多达20%，特征推断重建误差（MSE）增加了超过30%，并为在尊重隐私和成本约束的同时做出有意义贡献的客户提供了高达25%的更高激励。这些结果突显了OPUS-VFL作为一种安全、公平和以性能为驱动的现实世界VFL解决方案的实用性和创新性。

Privacy-Preserving Machine Learning for IoT: A Cross-Paradigm Survey and Future Roadmap
Authors: Zakia Zaman, Praveen Gauravaram, Mahbub Hassan, Sanjay Jha, Wen Hu
First: 2026-03-13T20:19:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T18:14:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid proliferation of the Internet of Things has intensified demand for robust privacy-preserving machine learning mechanisms to safeguard sensitive data generated by large-scale, heterogeneous, and resource-constrained devices. Unlike centralized environments, IoT ecosystems are inherently decentralized, bandwidth-limited, and latency-sensitive, exposing privacy risks across sensing, communication, and distributed training pipelines. These characteristics render conventional anonymization and centralized protection strategies insufficient for practical deployments. This survey presents a comprehensive IoT-centric, cross-paradigm analysis of privacy-preserving machine learning. We introduce a structured taxonomy spanning perturbation-based mechanisms such as differential privacy, distributed paradigms such as federated learning, cryptographic approaches including homomorphic encryption and secure multiparty computation, and generative synthesis techniques based on generative adversarial networks. For each paradigm, we examine formal privacy guarantees, computational and communication complexity, scalability under heterogeneous device participation, and resilience against threats including membership inference, model inversion, gradient leakage, and adversarial manipulation. We further analyze deployment constraints in wireless IoT environments, highlighting trade-offs between privacy, communication overhead, model convergence, and system efficiency within next-generation mobile architectures. We also consolidate evaluation methodologies, summarize representative datasets and open-source frameworks, and identify open challenges including hybrid privacy integration, energy-aware learning, privacy-preserving large language models, and quantum-resilient machine learning.

This survey employs a cross-paradigm analysis to categorize various privacy-preserving methods, including perturbation-based mechanisms, distributed learning approaches, cryptographic techniques, and generative synthesis methods. Key findings indicate that traditional privacy strategies are inadequate for IoT environments, and the study highlights the importance of addressing deployment challenges such as privacy guarantees, computational complexity, and resilience against various threats while balancing privacy with system efficiency and communication overhead.
物联网的快速普及使得对有效的隐私保护机器学习技术的需求日益迫切，以保护来自多样化和资源有限设备的敏感数据。该调查采用跨范式分析的方法，对各种隐私保护机制进行分类，包括差分隐私、联邦学习、同态加密和生成对抗网络。主要发现揭示了这些方法的正式隐私保证、计算复杂性和可扩展性问题，以及它们对诸如成员推断和模型反演等威胁的脆弱性，同时还解决了无线物联网环境中的部署挑战以及隐私、通信开销和系统效率之间的权衡。
From Chat Control to Robot Control: Implications of the Chat Control Proposal for Human-Robot Interaction
Authors: Neziha Akalin, Alberto Giaretta
First: 2026-01-05T15:27:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T15:33:24+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper explores how a recent European Union proposal, the so-called Chat Control, which creates regulatory incentives for providers to implement content detection and communication scanning, could transform the foundations of human-robot interaction (HRI). As robots increasingly act as interpersonal communication channels in care, education, and telepresence, they convey not only speech but also gesture, emotion, and contextual cues. We argue that extending digital surveillance laws to such embodied systems would entail continuous monitoring, embedding observation into the very design of everyday robots. This regulation blurs the line between protection and control, turning companions into potential informants. At the same time, monitoring mechanisms that undermine end-to-end encryption function as de facto backdoors, expanding the attack surface and allowing adversaries to exploit legally induced monitoring infrastructures. This creates a paradox of safety through insecurity: systems introduced to protect users may instead compromise their privacy, autonomy, and trust. This work does not aim to predict the future, but to raise awareness and help prevent certain futures from materialising.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从聊天控制到机器人控制：聊天控制提案对人机交互的影响
本文探讨了最近欧盟提案，即所谓的聊天控制，该提案为提供者实施内容检测和通信扫描创造了监管激励，可能会改变人机交互（HRI）的基础。随着机器人在护理、教育和远程存在中越来越多地充当人际沟通渠道，它们不仅传达语言，还传达手势、情感和上下文线索。我们认为，将数字监控法律扩展到这些具身系统将意味着持续监控，将观察嵌入日常机器人的设计中。这项监管模糊了保护与控制之间的界限，使伴侣变成潜在的告密者。同时，破坏端到端加密的监控机制实际上充当了后门，扩大了攻击面，使对手能够利用法律引发的监控基础设施。这创造了通过不安全性实现安全的悖论：旨在保护用户的系统可能反而会损害他们的隐私、自主权和信任。该工作并不旨在预测未来，而是提高意识，帮助防止某些未来的实现。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this paper is to investigate the implications of the European Union's Chat Control proposal on human-robot interaction, particularly as robots become integral in communication across various sectors. The authors analyze how regulatory incentives for content detection and communication scanning could lead to continuous monitoring of robots, fundamentally altering their design and function. The key findings indicate that such regulations could transform robots from companions into informants, compromising user privacy and autonomy while creating vulnerabilities that could be exploited by adversaries, thus highlighting a paradox where intended safety measures may actually increase insecurity.
本论文的动机在于探讨欧盟的聊天控制提案对人机交互的影响，特别是随着机器人在各个领域的沟通中变得日益重要。作者分析了该提案如何鼓励内容检测和通信扫描，可能导致对机器人的持续监控，从而根本改变它们在日常生活中的设计和功能。主要发现表明，这种监管措施可能模糊用户保护与控制之间的界限，潜在地将机器人从伴侣转变为告密者，同时引入可能通过削弱加密和增加监控风险来危害用户隐私和信任的脆弱性。
Beware Untrusted Simulators -- Reward-Free Backdoor Attacks in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ethan Rathbun, Wo Wei Lin, Alina Oprea, Christopher Amato
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-04T22:17:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T14:45:34+00:00
Comments: 10 pages main body, ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Simulated environments are a key piece in the success of Reinforcement Learning (RL), allowing practitioners and researchers to train decision making agents without running expensive experiments on real hardware. Simulators remain a security blind spot, however, enabling adversarial developers to alter the dynamics of their released simulators for malicious purposes. Therefore, in this work we highlight a novel threat, demonstrating how simulator dynamics can be exploited to stealthily implant action-level backdoors into RL agents. The backdoor then allows an adversary to reliably activate targeted actions in an agent upon observing a predefined ``trigger'', leading to potentially dangerous consequences. Traditional backdoor attacks are limited in their strong threat models, assuming the adversary has near full control over an agent's training pipeline, enabling them to both alter and observe agent's rewards. As these assumptions are infeasible to implement within a simulator, we propose a new attack ``Daze'' which is able to reliably and stealthily implant backdoors into RL agents trained for real world tasks without altering or even observing their rewards. We provide formal proof of Daze's effectiveness in guaranteeing attack success across general RL tasks along with extensive empirical evaluations on both discrete and continuous action space domains. We additionally provide the first example of RL backdoor attacks transferring to real, robotic hardware. These developments motivate further research into securing all components of the RL training pipeline to prevent malicious attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：警惕不可信的模拟器——强化学习中的无奖励后门攻击
模拟环境是强化学习（RL）成功的关键部分，使从业者和研究人员能够在不进行昂贵的真实硬件实验的情况下训练决策代理。然而，模拟器仍然是一个安全盲点，使对手开发者能够出于恶意目的改变其发布的模拟器的动态。因此，在这项工作中，我们强调了一种新威胁，展示了如何利用模拟器动态隐秘地将动作级后门植入RL代理中。后门允许对手在观察到预定义的“触发”后可靠地激活代理中的目标动作，导致潜在的危险后果。传统的后门攻击在其强威胁模型中受到限制，假设对手几乎完全控制代理的训练流程，使其能够同时改变和观察代理的奖励。由于这些假设在模拟器中不可行，我们提出了一种新的攻击“Daze”，能够在不改变或甚至观察代理奖励的情况下，可靠且隐秘地将后门植入为真实世界任务训练的RL代理中。我们提供了Daze在保证攻击成功方面的正式证明，适用于一般RL任务，并在离散和连续动作空间领域进行了广泛的实证评估。此外，我们还提供了RL后门攻击转移到真实机器人硬件的第一个例子。这些发展激励了对保护RL训练流程所有组件的进一步研究，以防止恶意攻击。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the vulnerability of simulated environments in Reinforcement Learning (RL), which can be manipulated by adversaries to implant backdoors in RL agents. The authors introduce a novel attack method called 'Daze', which stealthily embeds action-level backdoors into RL agents without requiring control over the training pipeline or observing rewards. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of Daze across various RL tasks, including its successful transfer to real robotic hardware, highlighting the need for enhanced security measures in RL training processes.
本研究的动机是解决用于训练强化学习（RL）代理的模拟环境中的安全漏洞，这些漏洞可能被对手利用来植入后门。作者提出了一种名为“Daze”的新攻击方法，该方法在不需要改变或观察奖励的情况下，悄然将动作级后门嵌入RL代理中。实验结果表明，Daze在各种RL任务中有效，并成功转移到真实的机器人硬件上，突显了在RL训练管道中加强安全措施的紧迫性。
Multilingual LLMs Struggle to Link Orthography and Semantics in Bilingual Word Processing
Authors: Eshaan Tanwar, Gayatri Oke, Tanmoy Chakraborty
First: 2025-01-15T20:22:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T14:38:19+00:00
Comments: Code available at: https://github.com/EshaanT/Bilingual_processing_LLMs
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Bilingual lexical processing is shaped by the complex interplay of phonological, orthographic, and semantic features of two languages within an integrated mental lexicon. In humans, this is evident in the ease with which cognate words - words similar in both orthographic form and meaning (e.g., blind, meaning "sightless" in both English and German) - are processed, compared to the challenges posed by interlingual homographs, which share orthographic form but differ in meaning (e.g., gift, meaning "present" in English but "poison" in German). We investigate how multilingual Large Language Models (LLMs) handle such phenomena, focusing on English-Spanish, English-French, and English-German cognates, non-cognate, and interlingual homographs. Specifically, we evaluate their ability to disambiguate meanings and make semantic judgments, both when these word types are presented in isolation or within sentence contexts. Our findings reveal that while certain LLMs demonstrate strong performance in recognizing cognates and non-cognates in isolation, they exhibit significant difficulty in disambiguating interlingual homographs, often performing below random baselines. This suggests LLMs tend to rely heavily on orthographic similarities rather than semantic understanding when interpreting interlingual homographs. Further, we find LLMs exhibit difficulty in retrieving word meanings, with performance in isolative disambiguation tasks having no correlation with semantic understanding. Finally, we study how the LLM processes interlingual homographs in incongruent sentences. We find models to opt for different strategies in understanding English and non-English homographs, highlighting a lack of a unified approach to handling cross-lingual ambiguities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多语言大型语言模型在双语词处理中的正字法与语义链接的困难
双语词汇处理受到两种语言的音韵、正字法和语义特征之间复杂相互作用的影响。在人类中，这在同源词的处理上表现得尤为明显——同源词在正字法形式和意义上相似（例如，blind，在英语和德语中均意为“失明”），相比之下，跨语言同形异义词则带来了挑战，它们在正字法形式上相同但意义不同（例如，gift，在英语中意为“礼物”，而在德语中意为“毒药”）。我们研究多语言大型语言模型（LLMs）如何处理这些现象，重点关注英语-西班牙语、英语-法语和英语-德语的同源词、非同源词和跨语言同形异义词。具体而言，我们评估它们在孤立呈现或句子上下文中对这些词类型进行意义消歧和语义判断的能力。我们的研究发现，尽管某些LLMs在识别孤立的同源词和非同源词方面表现出色，但在消歧跨语言同形异义词时却表现出显著困难，通常低于随机基线。这表明LLMs在解释跨语言同形异义词时往往过于依赖正字法相似性，而非语义理解。此外，我们发现LLMs在检索词义时存在困难，孤立消歧任务的表现与语义理解之间没有相关性。最后，我们研究LLM在不一致句子中处理跨语言同形异义词的方式。我们发现模型在理解英语和非英语同形异义词时选择不同的策略，突显出处理跨语言歧义时缺乏统一的方法。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates how multilingual Large Language Models (LLMs) process bilingual lexical items, motivated by the complexities of phonological, orthographic, and semantic features in human language processing. The study evaluates LLMs' abilities to disambiguate meanings and make semantic judgments regarding cognates, non-cognates, and interlingual homographs in both isolation and sentence contexts. Key findings indicate that while LLMs perform well with cognates and non-cognates, they struggle significantly with interlingual homographs, often relying on orthographic similarities rather than semantic understanding, and show no correlation between performance in disambiguation tasks and semantic comprehension.

Rethinking Gradient-based Adversarial Attacks on Point Cloud Classification
Authors: Jun Chen, Xinke Li, Mingyue Xu, Chongshou Li, Truiani Li
Venue: ICME 2026
First: 2025-05-28T00:55:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T13:36:28+00:00
Comments: ICME 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Gradient-based adversarial attacks are widely used to evaluate the robustness of 3D point cloud classifiers, yet they often rely on uniform update rules that neglect point-wise heterogeneity, leading to perceptible perturbations. We propose two complementary strategies to improve both the effectiveness and imperceptibility of the attack. \textbf{WAAttack} employs weighted gradients to dynamically adjust per-point perturbation magnitudes and uses an adaptive step size strategy to regulate the global perturbation scale. \textbf{SubAttack} partitions the point cloud into subsets and, at each iteration, perturbs only those combinations with high adversarial efficacy and low perceptual saliency. Together, these methods offer a principled refinement of gradient-based attacks for 3D point clouds. Extensive experiments show that our approach consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods in generating highly imperceptible adversarial examples. The code is available at https://github.com/chenjun0326/WA_SubAttack.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新思考基于梯度的点云分类对抗攻击

Experimental results demonstrate that these methods significantly outperform existing state-of-the-art techniques in generating adversarial examples that are less perceptible to human observers.
本研究解决了基于梯度的对抗攻击在3D点云分类器上的局限性，这些攻击由于统一的更新规则而产生明显的扰动，忽视了点之间的差异。作者提出了两种策略：WAAttack，利用加权梯度和自适应步长来增强扰动控制；SubAttack，根据对抗有效性和感知显著性选择性地扰动点云的子集。实验结果表明，这些方法显著改善了与现有最先进技术相比，生成不可察觉的对抗样本的能力。
Parameter-Efficient Modality-Balanced Symmetric Fusion for Multimodal Remote Sensing Semantic Segmentation
Authors: Haocheng Li, Juepeng Zheng, Shuangxi Miao, Ruibo Lu, Guosheng Cai, Haohuan Fu, Jianxi Huang
First: 2026-03-18T13:23:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T13:23:58+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multimodal remote sensing semantic segmentation enhances scene interpretation by exploiting complementary physical cues from heterogeneous data. Although pretrained Vision Foundation Models (VFMs) provide strong general-purpose representations, adapting them to multimodal tasks often incurs substantial computational overhead and is prone to modality imbalance, where the contribution of auxiliary modalities is suppressed during optimization. To address these challenges, we propose MoBaNet, a parameter-efficient and modality-balanced symmetric fusion framework. Built upon a largely frozen VFM backbone, MoBaNet adopts a symmetric dual-stream architecture to preserve generalizable representations while minimizing the number of trainable parameters. Specifically, we design a Cross-modal Prompt-Injected Adapter (CPIA) to enable deep semantic interaction by generating shared prompts and injecting them into bottleneck adapters under the frozen backbone. To obtain compact and discriminative multimodal representations for decoding, we further introduce a Difference-Guided Gated Fusion Module (DGFM), which adaptively fuses paired stage features by explicitly leveraging cross-modal discrepancy to guide feature selection. Furthermore, we propose a Modality-Conditional Random Masking (MCRM) strategy to mitigate modality imbalance by masking one modality only during training and imposing hard-pixel auxiliary supervision on modality-specific branches. Extensive experiments on the ISPRS Vaihingen and Potsdam benchmarks demonstrate that MoBaNet achieves state-of-the-art performance with significantly fewer trainable parameters than full fine-tuning, validating its effectiveness for robust and balanced multimodal fusion. The source code in this work is available at https://github.com/sauryeo/MoBaNet.
中文标题/摘要
标题：参数高效的模态平衡对称融合用于多模态遥感语义分割
多模态遥感语义分割通过利用异构数据的互补物理线索增强场景解释。尽管预训练的视觉基础模型（VFM）提供了强大的通用表示，但将其适应于多模态任务通常会产生大量计算开销，并且容易出现模态不平衡，在优化过程中辅助模态的贡献被抑制。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了MoBaNet，一个参数高效且模态平衡的对称融合框架。MoBaNet建立在一个大部分冻结的VFM骨干网络之上，采用对称双流架构以保留可泛化的表示，同时最小化可训练参数的数量。具体而言，我们设计了一个跨模态提示注入适配器（CPIA），通过生成共享提示并将其注入冻结骨干下的瓶颈适配器来实现深层语义交互。为了获得紧凑且具有区分性的多模态表示以进行解码，我们进一步引入了差异引导门控融合模块（DGFM），该模块通过明确利用跨模态差异来指导特征选择，自适应地融合配对阶段特征。此外，我们提出了一种模态条件随机掩蔽（MCRM）策略，通过在训练期间仅掩蔽一种模态并对模态特定分支施加硬像素辅助监督来减轻模态不平衡。在ISPRS Vaihingen和波茨坦基准上的大量实验表明，MoBaNet在可训练参数显著少于完全微调的情况下实现了最先进的性能，验证了其在稳健和平衡的多模态融合中的有效性。本工作的源代码可在https://github.com/sauryeo/MoBaNet获取。

The authors propose MoBaNet, a parameter-efficient and modality-balanced symmetric fusion framework that utilizes a largely frozen VFM backbone and a dual-stream architecture to maintain generalizable representations while reducing trainable parameters. Key experimental results show that MoBaNet achieves state-of-the-art performance on the ISPRS Vaihingen and Potsdam benchmarks with significantly fewer trainable parameters compared to full fine-tuning, demonstrating its effectiveness in robust and balanced multimodal fusion.

STEP: Detecting Audio Backdoor Attacks via Stability-based Trigger Exposure Profiling
Authors: Kun Wang, Meng Chen, Junhao Wang, Yuli Wu, Li Lu, Chong Zhang, Peng Cheng, Jiaheng Zhang, Kui Ren
First: 2026-03-18T12:14:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T12:14:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the widespread deployment of deep-learning-based speech models in security-critical applications, backdoor attacks have emerged as a serious threat: an adversary who poisons a small fraction of training data can implant a hidden trigger that controls the model's output while preserving normal behavior on clean inputs. Existing inference-time defenses are not well suited to the audio domain, as they either rely on trigger over-robustness assumptions that fail on transformation-based and semantic triggers, or depend on properties specific to image or text modalities. In this paper, we propose STEP (Stability-based Trigger Exposure Profiling), a black-box, retraining-free backdoor detector that operates under hard-label-only access. Its core idea is to exploit a characteristic dual anomaly of backdoor triggers: anomalous label stability under semantic-breaking perturbations, and anomalous label fragility under semantic-preserving perturbations. STEP profiles each test sample with two complementary perturbation branches that target these two properties respectively, scores the resulting stability features with one-class anomaly detectors trained on benign references, and fuses the two scores via unsupervised weighting. Extensive experiments across seven backdoor attacks show that STEP achieves an average AUROC of 97.92% and EER of 4.54%, substantially outperforming state-of-the-art baselines, and generalizes across model architectures, speech tasks, an open-set verification scenario, and over-the-air physical-world settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：STEP：通过基于稳定性的触发器暴露分析检测音频后门攻击
随着基于深度学习的语音模型在安全关键应用中的广泛部署，后门攻击已成为一个严重威胁：对训练数据的小部分进行污染的对手可以植入一个隐藏的触发器，控制模型的输出，同时在干净输入上保持正常行为。现有的推理时防御措施不适合音频领域，因为它们要么依赖于在基于变换和语义触发器上失效的触发器过度鲁棒性假设，要么依赖于特定于图像或文本模态的属性。本文提出了STEP（基于稳定性的触发器暴露分析），这是一种黑箱、无重训练的后门检测器，仅在硬标签访问下操作。其核心思想是利用后门触发器的特征双重异常：在语义破坏扰动下的异常标签稳定性，以及在语义保持扰动下的异常标签脆弱性。STEP通过两个互补的扰动分支对每个测试样本进行分析，分别针对这两个属性，使用在良性参考上训练的一类异常检测器对结果稳定性特征进行评分，并通过无监督加权融合这两个评分。针对七种后门攻击的广泛实验表明，STEP的平均AUROC达到97.92%，EER为4.54%，显著优于最先进的基线，并在模型架构、语音任务、开放集验证场景和物理世界设置中具有良好的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is the increasing threat of backdoor attacks on deep-learning-based speech models, particularly in security-sensitive applications. The authors propose a novel detection method called STEP (Stability-based Trigger Exposure Profiling), which is a black-box, retraining-free approach that utilizes hard-label-only access. The key experimental findings demonstrate that STEP effectively identifies backdoor triggers by analyzing label stability and fragility under different perturbations, achieving an average AUROC of 97.92% and an EER of 4.54%, significantly outperforming existing methods across various attack scenarios and model architectures.
本研究的动机在于应对深度学习语音模型中日益严重的后门攻击威胁，这些攻击可能危及安全关键应用。作者提出了一种新颖的检测方法，称为STEP（基于稳定性的触发器暴露分析），该方法无需重新训练，仅依赖硬标签访问。该方法利用后门触发器的双重异常特性，通过分析在不同扰动下的标签稳定性和脆弱性，实现在七种后门攻击中平均AUROC达到97.92%，EER为4.54%，显著优于现有的最先进防御，并在各种模型架构和现实场景中表现出鲁棒性。
VeriGrey: Greybox Agent Validation
Authors: Yuntong Zhang, Sungmin Kang, Ruijie Meng, Marcel Böhme, Abhik Roychoudhury
First: 2026-03-18T12:00:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T12:00:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic AI has been a topic of great interest recently. A Large Language Model (LLM) agent involves one or more LLMs in the back-end. In the front end, it conducts autonomous decision-making by combining the LLM outputs with results obtained by invoking several external tools. The autonomous interactions with the external environment introduce critical security risks. In this paper, we present a grey-box approach to explore diverse behaviors and uncover security risks in LLM agents. Our approach VeriGrey uses the sequence of tools invoked as a feedback function to drive the testing process. This helps uncover infrequent but dangerous tool invocations that cause unexpected agent behavior. As mutation operators in the testing process, we mutate prompts to design pernicious injection prompts. This is carefully accomplished by linking the task of the agent to an injection task, so that the injection task becomes a necessary step of completing the agent functionality. Comparing our approach with a black-box baseline on the well-known AgentDojo benchmark, VeriGrey achieves 33% additional efficacy in finding indirect prompt injection vulnerabilities with a GPT-4.1 back-end. We also conduct real-world case studies with the widely used coding agent Gemini CLI, and the well-known OpenClaw personal assistant. VeriGrey finds prompts inducing several attack scenarios that could not be identified by black-box approaches. In OpenClaw, by constructing a conversation agent which employs mutational fuzz testing as needed, VeriGrey is able to discover malicious skill variants from 10 malicious skills (with 10/10= 100% success rate on the Kimi-K2.5 LLM backend, and 9/10= 90% success rate on Opus 4.6 LLM backend). This demonstrates the value of a dynamic approach like VeriGrey to test agents, and to eventually lead to an agent assurance framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VeriGrey: 灰盒代理验证
代理人工智能最近引起了极大关注。大型语言模型（LLM）代理涉及一个或多个后端LLM。在前端，它通过将LLM输出与调用多个外部工具获得的结果结合，进行自主决策。与外部环境的自主交互引入了关键的安全风险。 在本文中，我们提出了一种灰盒方法，以探索LLM代理的多样行为并揭示安全风险。我们的方法VeriGrey使用调用工具的序列作为反馈函数来驱动测试过程。这有助于揭示导致意外代理行为的不频繁但危险的工具调用。作为测试过程中的变异操作符，我们变异提示以设计恶意注入提示。这是通过将代理的任务与注入任务关联来仔细完成的，从而使注入任务成为完成代理功能的必要步骤。与著名的AgentDojo基准上的黑盒基线相比，VeriGrey在使用GPT-4.1后端时，在发现间接提示注入漏洞方面实现了33%的额外有效性。 我们还对广泛使用的编码代理Gemini CLI和著名的OpenClaw个人助手进行了真实案例研究。VeriGrey发现了几种攻击场景的提示，这些场景无法通过黑盒方法识别。在OpenClaw中，通过构建一个根据需要采用变异模糊测试的对话代理，VeriGrey能够从10个恶意技能中发现恶意技能变体（在Kimi-K2.5 LLM后端的成功率为10/10=100%，在Opus 4.6 LLM后端的成功率为9/10=90%）。这证明了像VeriGrey这样的动态方法在测试代理方面的价值，并最终导致代理保证框架的建立。

Impact of Data Duplication on Deep Neural Network-Based Image Classifiers: Robust vs. Standard Models
Authors: Alireza Aghabagherloo, Aydin Abadi, Sumanta Sarkar, Vishnu Asutosh Dasu, Bart Preneel
First: 2025-04-01T10:48:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T11:51:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The accuracy and robustness of machine learning models against adversarial attacks are significantly influenced by factors such as training data quality, model architecture, the training process, and the deployment environment. In recent years, duplicated data in training sets, especially in language models, has attracted considerable attention. It has been shown that deduplication enhances both training performance and model accuracy in language models. While the importance of data quality in training image classifier Deep Neural Networks (DNNs) is widely recognized, the impact of duplicated images in the training set on model generalization and performance has received little attention. In this paper, we address this gap and provide a comprehensive study on the effect of duplicates in image classification. Our analysis indicates that the presence of duplicated images in the training set not only negatively affects the efficiency of model training but also may result in lower accuracy of the image classifier. This negative impact of duplication on accuracy is particularly evident when duplicated data is non-uniform across classes or when duplication, whether uniform or non-uniform, occurs in the training set of an adversarially trained model. Even when duplicated samples are selected in a uniform way, increasing the amount of duplication does not lead to a significant improvement in accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据重复对基于深度神经网络的图像分类器的影响：鲁棒模型与标准模型
机器学习模型在对抗攻击下的准确性和鲁棒性受到训练数据质量、模型架构、训练过程和部署环境等因素的显著影响。近年来，训练集中的重复数据，尤其是在语言模型中，受到了相当大的关注。研究表明，去重可以提高语言模型的训练性能和模型准确性。尽管在训练图像分类器深度神经网络（DNNs）时数据质量的重要性得到了广泛认可，但训练集中重复图像对模型泛化和性能的影响却鲜有关注。 本文旨在填补这一空白，全面研究图像分类中重复数据的影响。我们的分析表明，训练集中重复图像的存在不仅对模型训练效率产生负面影响，还可能导致图像分类器的准确性降低。当重复数据在类别间不均匀分布时，或者在对抗训练模型的训练集中发生重复时，这种对准确性的负面影响尤为明显。即使以均匀方式选择重复样本，增加重复量也不会显著提高准确性。

rSDNet: Unified Robust Neural Learning against Label Noise and Adversarial Attacks
Authors: Suryasis Jana, Abhik Ghosh
First: 2026-03-18T11:47:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T11:47:46+00:00
Comments: Pre-print; under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural networks are central to modern artificial intelligence, yet their training remains highly sensitive to data contamination. Standard neural classifiers are trained by minimizing the categorical cross-entropy loss, corresponding to maximum likelihood estimation under a multinomial model. While statistically efficient under ideal conditions, this approach is highly vulnerable to contaminated observations including label noises corrupting supervision in the output space, and adversarial perturbations inducing worst-case deviations in the input space. In this paper, we propose a unified and statistically grounded framework for robust neural classification that addresses both forms of contamination within a single learning objective. We formulate neural network training as a minimum-divergence estimation problem and introduce rSDNet, a robust learning algorithm based on the general class of $S$-divergences. The resulting training objective inherits robustness properties from classical statistical estimation, automatically down-weighting aberrant observations through model probabilities. We establish essential population-level properties of rSDNet, including Fisher consistency, classification calibration implying Bayes optimality, and robustness guarantees under uniform label noise and infinitesimal feature contamination. Experiments on three benchmark image classification datasets show that rSDNet improves robustness to label corruption and adversarial attacks while maintaining competitive accuracy on clean data, Our results highlight minimum-divergence learning as a principled and effective framework for robust neural classification under heterogeneous data contamination.
中文标题/摘要
标题：rSDNet：针对标签噪声和对抗攻击的统一鲁棒神经学习
神经网络是现代人工智能的核心，但其训练对数据污染高度敏感。标准神经分类器通过最小化分类交叉熵损失进行训练，对应于多项式模型下的最大似然估计。在理想条件下，这种方法在统计上是有效的，但对污染观察（包括输出空间中损坏监督的标签噪声和输入空间中引起最坏情况偏差的对抗扰动）高度脆弱。本文提出了一个统一且统计基础的鲁棒神经分类框架，旨在在单一学习目标内解决这两种污染形式。我们将神经网络训练形式化为最小散度估计问题，并引入rSDNet，这是一种基于$S$-散度一般类的鲁棒学习算法。所得到的训练目标继承了经典统计估计的鲁棒性特性，通过模型概率自动降低异常观察的权重。我们建立了rSDNet的基本群体级属性，包括Fisher一致性、分类校准暗示贝叶斯最优性，以及在均匀标签噪声和无穷小特征污染下的鲁棒性保证。在三个基准图像分类数据集上的实验表明，rSDNet在保持干净数据的竞争性准确度的同时，提高了对标签损坏和对抗攻击的鲁棒性。我们的结果突出了最小散度学习作为在异质数据污染下进行鲁棒神经分类的原则性和有效框架。

Rel-Zero: Harnessing Patch-Pair Invariance for Robust Zero-Watermarking Against AI Editing
Authors: Pengzhen Chen, Yanwei Liu, Xiaoyan Gu, Xiaojun Chen, Wu Liu, Weiping Wang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-18T09:40:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T09:40:00+00:00
Comments: accepted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advancements in diffusion-based image editing pose a significant threat to the authenticity of digital visual content. Traditional embedding-based watermarking methods often introduce perceptible perturbations to maintain robustness, inevitably compromising visual fidelity. Meanwhile, existing zero-watermarking approaches, typically relying on global image features, struggle to withstand sophisticated manipulations. In this work, we uncover a key observation: while individual image patches undergo substantial alterations during AI-based editing, the relational distance between patch pairs remains relatively invariant. Leveraging this property, we propose Relational Zero-Watermarking (Rel-Zero), a novel framework that requires no modification to the original image but derives a unique zero-watermark from these editing-invariant patch relations. By grounding the watermark in intrinsic structural consistency rather than absolute appearance, Rel-Zero provides a non-invasive yet resilient mechanism for content authentication. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Rel-Zero achieves substantially improved robustness across diverse editing models and manipulations compared to prior zero-watermarking approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Rel-Zero：利用补丁对不变性实现对抗AI编辑的鲁棒零水印
最近基于扩散的图像编辑技术对数字视觉内容的真实性构成了重大威胁。传统的基于嵌入的水印方法通常会引入可感知的扰动以保持鲁棒性，必然会损害视觉保真度。同时，现有的零水印方法通常依赖于全局图像特征，难以抵御复杂的操控。在本研究中，我们发现一个关键观察：尽管单个图像补丁在基于AI的编辑过程中经历了显著的变化，但补丁对之间的关系距离保持相对不变。利用这一特性，我们提出了关系零水印（Rel-Zero），这是一个新颖的框架，无需对原始图像进行修改，而是从这些编辑不变的补丁关系中推导出独特的零水印。通过将水印基于内在结构一致性而非绝对外观，Rel-Zero 提供了一种非侵入性但又具有韧性的内容认证机制。大量实验表明，与之前的零水印方法相比，Rel-Zero 在各种编辑模型和操控中实现了显著提高的鲁棒性。

The motivation behind this research is to address the challenges posed by advanced diffusion-based image editing techniques that threaten the authenticity of digital visual content. Experimental results show that Rel-Zero significantly enhances robustness against various editing models and manipulations compared to existing zero-watermarking methods.

Proof-of-Authorship for Diffusion-based AI Generated Content
Authors: De Zhang Lee, Han Fang, Ee-Chien Chang
First: 2026-03-18T09:21:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T09:21:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advancements in AI-generated content (AIGC) have introduced new challenges in intellectual property protection and the authentication of generated objects. We focus on scenarios in which an author seeks to assert authorship of an object generated using latent diffusion models (LDMs), in the presence of adversaries who attempt to falsely claim authorship of objects they did not create. While proof-of-ownership has been studied in the context of multimedia content through techniques such as time-stamping and watermarking, these approaches face notable limitations. In contrast to traditional content creation sources (e.g., cameras), the LDM generation process offers greater control to the author. Specifically, the random seed used during generation can be deliberately chosen. By binding the seed to the author's identity using cryptographic pseudorandom functions, the author can assert to be the creator of the object. We refer to this stronger guarantee as proof-of-authorship, since only the creator of the object can legitimately claim the object. This contrasts with proof-of-ownership via time-stamping or watermarking, where any entity could potentially claim ownership of an object by being the first to timestamp or embed the watermark. We propose a proof-of-authorship framework involving a probabilistic adjudicator who quantifies the probability that a claim is false. Furthermore, unlike prior approaches, the proposed framework does not involve any secret. We explore various attack scenarios and analyze design choices using Stable Diffusion 2.1 (SD2.1) as representative case studies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于扩散的人工智能生成内容的作者证明
最近在人工智能生成内容（AIGC）方面的进展带来了知识产权保护和生成对象认证的新挑战。我们关注作者在潜在对手试图虚假声称未创建对象的情况下，如何主张使用潜在扩散模型（LDMs）生成的对象的作者身份。尽管在多媒体内容的所有权证明方面已经研究了时间戳和水印等技术，但这些方法面临显著的局限性。与传统内容创作来源（例如相机）相比，LDM生成过程为作者提供了更大的控制权。具体而言，生成过程中使用的随机种子可以被故意选择。通过使用加密伪随机函数将种子绑定到作者身份，作者可以主张自己是该对象的创作者。我们将这种更强的保证称为作者证明，因为只有对象的创作者才能合法地声称该对象。这与通过时间戳或水印的所有权证明形成对比，后者任何实体都可能通过首次时间戳或嵌入水印来声称对象的所有权。我们提出了一种作者证明框架，涉及一个概率裁决者，该裁决者量化声称为虚假的概率。此外，与之前的方法不同，所提出的框架不涉及任何秘密。我们探讨了各种攻击场景，并使用稳定扩散2.1（SD2.1）作为代表案例研究分析设计选择。
