The motivation behind this research is to address the challenges of intellectual property protection and authorship authentication in the context of AI-generated content, particularly when adversaries may falsely claim authorship. The authors propose a proof-of-authorship framework that utilizes cryptographic pseudorandom functions to bind a random seed, chosen during the generation process of latent diffusion models, to the author's identity. Key experimental findings demonstrate that this method provides a stronger guarantee of authorship compared to traditional proof-of-ownership techniques, as it quantifies the probability of false claims without relying on secrets, and effectively analyzes various attack scenarios using Stable Diffusion 2.1 as a case study.
本研究的动机在于解决AI生成内容的知识产权保护和作者身份认证中的挑战，特别是在潜在扩散模型（LDM）的背景下。作者提出了一种作者身份证明框架，通过将LDM生成过程中使用的随机种子与作者身份绑定，利用密码伪随机函数，使真实创作者能够主张作者身份。关键实验结果表明，该框架相比传统的时间戳和水印等方法提供了更强的作者身份保证，因为它量化了虚假声明的概率而不依赖于秘密，并有效分析了使用稳定扩散2.1作为案例研究的各种攻击场景。
Caging the Agents: A Zero Trust Security Architecture for Autonomous AI in Healthcare
Authors: Saikat Maiti
First: 2026-03-18T06:54:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T06:54:47+00:00
Comments: Keywords: agentic AI security, autonomous agents, healthcare cybersecurity, zero trust, prompt injection, HIPAA, Kubernetes security, OpenClaw
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous AI agents powered by large language models are being deployed in production with capabilities including shell execution, file system access, database queries, and multi-party communication. Recent red teaming research demonstrates that these agents exhibit critical vulnerabilities in realistic settings: unauthorized compliance with non-owner instructions, sensitive information disclosure, identity spoofing, cross-agent propagation of unsafe practices, and indirect prompt injection through external resources [7]. In healthcare environments processing Protected Health Information, every such vulnerability becomes a potential HIPAA violation. This paper presents a security architecture deployed for nine autonomous AI agents in production at a healthcare technology company. We develop a six-domain threat model for agentic AI in healthcare covering credential exposure, execution capability abuse, network egress exfiltration, prompt integrity failures, database access risks, and fleet configuration drift. We implement four-layer defense in depth: (1) kernel level workload isolation using gVisor on Kubernetes, (2) credential proxy sidecars preventing agent containers from accessing raw secrets, (3) network egress policies restricting each agent to allowlisted destinations, and (4) a prompt integrity framework with structured metadata envelopes and untrusted content labeling. We report results from 90 days of deployment including four HIGH severity findings discovered and remediated by an automated security audit agent, progressive fleet hardening across three VM image generations, and defense coverage mapped to all eleven attack patterns from recent literature. All configurations, audit tooling, and the prompt integrity framework are released as open source.
中文标题/摘要
标题：限制智能体：用于医疗保健中自主AI的零信任安全架构
由大型语言模型驱动的自主AI智能体正在生产中部署，具备包括shell执行、文件系统访问、数据库查询和多方通信等能力。最近的红队研究表明，这些智能体在现实环境中表现出关键漏洞：未经授权遵循非所有者指令、敏感信息泄露、身份欺骗、不安全实践的跨智能体传播，以及通过外部资源的间接提示注入。在处理受保护健康信息的医疗环境中，每个漏洞都可能成为HIPAA违规。本文介绍了一种在医疗技术公司生产中为九个自主AI智能体部署的安全架构。我们为医疗保健中的智能AI开发了一个涵盖凭证暴露、执行能力滥用、网络出口外泄、提示完整性失败、数据库访问风险和车队配置漂移的六域威胁模型。我们实施了四层深度防御：(1) 在Kubernetes上使用gVisor进行内核级工作负载隔离，(2) 凭证代理边车防止智能体容器访问原始秘密，(3) 网络出口策略限制每个智能体仅允许访问白名单目的地，以及(4) 具有结构化元数据信封和不可信内容标记的提示完整性框架。我们报告了90天部署的结果，包括由自动安全审计智能体发现和修复的四个高严重性发现、跨三个虚拟机镜像代的逐步车队强化，以及与最近文献中的所有十一种攻击模式映射的防御覆盖。所有配置、审计工具和提示完整性框架均已作为开源发布。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this research stems from the critical vulnerabilities identified in autonomous AI agents used in healthcare, which can lead to potential HIPAA violations. The authors developed a six-domain threat model and implemented a four-layer defense architecture for nine autonomous AI agents deployed in a healthcare technology company. Key findings from a 90-day deployment included the identification and remediation of four high-severity vulnerabilities by an automated security audit agent, progressive hardening of the agent fleet across three VM image generations, and comprehensive defense coverage against eleven documented attack patterns.
本研究的动机在于解决医疗环境中自主AI代理的关键漏洞，特别是由于未经授权的行为和信息泄露而可能导致的HIPAA违规。作者为一家医疗科技公司的九个AI代理开发了一个六领域威胁模型，并实施了四层防御架构，采用了内核级工作负载隔离、凭证代理侧车、网络出口策略和提示完整性框架等技术。90天的部署实验结果显示，自动安全审计代理识别并修复了四个高严重性漏洞，同时在多个虚拟机镜像版本中实现了逐步的舰队强化，证明了对最近文献中识别的十一种攻击模式的有效防御覆盖。
Understanding and Defending VLM Jailbreaks via Jailbreak-Related Representation Shift
Authors: Zhihua Wei, Qiang Li, Jian Ruan, Zhenxin Qin, Leilei Wen, Dongrui Liu, Wen Shen
First: 2026-03-18T05:31:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T05:31:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large vision-language models (VLMs) often exhibit weakened safety alignment with the integration of the visual modality. Even when text prompts contain explicit harmful intent, adding an image can substantially increase jailbreak success rates. In this paper, we observe that VLMs can clearly distinguish benign inputs from harmful ones in their representation space. Moreover, even among harmful inputs, jailbreak samples form a distinct internal state that is separable from refusal samples. These observations suggest that jailbreaks do not arise from a failure to recognize harmful intent. Instead, the visual modality shifts representations toward a specific jailbreak state, thereby leading to a failure to trigger refusal. To quantify this transition, we identify a jailbreak direction and define the jailbreak-related shift as the component of the image-induced representation shift along this direction. Our analysis shows that the jailbreak-related shift reliably characterizes jailbreak behavior, providing a unified explanation for diverse jailbreak scenarios. Finally, we propose a defense method that enhances VLM safety by removing the jailbreak-related shift (JRS-Rem) at inference time. Experiments show that JRS-Rem provides strong defense across multiple scenarios while preserving performance on benign tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过与越狱相关的表示转变理解和防御VLM越狱
大型视觉语言模型（VLM）在视觉模态的整合下，往往表现出安全对齐的减弱。即使文本提示包含明确的有害意图，添加图像也会显著提高越狱成功率。本文观察到，VLM能够在其表示空间中清晰地区分良性输入和有害输入。此外，即使在有害输入中，越狱样本形成了一个与拒绝样本可分离的独特内部状态。这些观察表明，越狱并不是由于未能识别有害意图而产生的。相反，视觉模态将表示转向特定的越狱状态，从而导致未能触发拒绝。为了量化这一转变，我们识别了一个越狱方向，并将与越狱相关的转变定义为沿该方向的图像诱导表示转变的组成部分。我们的分析表明，与越狱相关的转变可靠地表征了越狱行为，为多样的越狱场景提供了统一的解释。最后，我们提出了一种防御方法，通过在推理时去除与越狱相关的转变（JRS-Rem）来增强VLM的安全性。实验表明，JRS-Rem在多个场景中提供了强有力的防御，同时保持了良性任务的性能。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the vulnerability of large vision-language models (VLMs) to jailbreak attacks, which are exacerbated by the integration of visual inputs that can mislead the model's safety mechanisms. The authors analyze the representation space of VLMs to identify how they differentiate between benign and harmful inputs, revealing that harmful inputs, particularly jailbreak samples, occupy a distinct internal state. They quantify the representation shift induced by images towards this jailbreak state and propose a defense method, JRS-Rem, which effectively mitigates the jailbreak-related shift during inference, demonstrating strong defense capabilities across various scenarios while maintaining performance on benign tasks.
本研究的动机是解决大型视觉语言模型（VLMs）中的安全对齐问题，特别是视觉输入的整合如何提高有害提示的成功率。作者采用一种分析VLM表示空间的方法，以识别与越狱样本相关的独特内部状态，该状态与良性样本和拒绝样本是可分离的。研究的主要发现表明，视觉模态引发的特定表示转变促进了越狱行为，并提出了一种防御机制JRS-Rem，该机制在推理过程中有效减轻了这种转变，同时保持了对良性任务的性能。
Systematic Scaling Analysis of Jailbreak Attacks in Large Language Models
Authors: Xiangwen Wang, Ananth Balashankar, Varun Chandrasekaran
First: 2026-03-11T17:38:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T04:23:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks, yet we still lack a systematic understanding of how jailbreak success scales with attacker effort across methods, model families, and harm types. We initiate a scaling-law framework for jailbreaks by treating each attack as a compute-bounded optimization procedure and measuring progress on a shared FLOPs axis. Our systematic evaluation spans four representative jailbreak paradigms, covering optimization-based attacks, self-refinement prompting, sampling-based selection, and genetic optimization, across multiple model families and scales on a diverse set of harmful goals. We investigate scaling laws that relate attacker budget to attack success score by fitting a simple saturating exponential function to FLOPs--success trajectories, and we derive comparable efficiency summaries from the fitted curves. Empirically, prompting-based paradigms tend to be the most compute-efficient compared to optimization-based methods. To explain this gap, we cast prompt-based updates into an optimization view and show via a same-state comparison that prompt-based attacks more effectively optimize in prompt space. We also show that attacks occupy distinct success--stealthiness operating points with prompting-based methods occupying the high-success, high-stealth region. Finally, we find that vulnerability is strongly goal-dependent: harms involving misinformation are typically easier to elicit than other non-misinformation harms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型越狱攻击的系统化规模分析
大型语言模型仍然容易受到越狱攻击，但我们仍然缺乏对越狱成功如何随着攻击者努力在方法、模型家族和伤害类型之间扩展的系统理解。我们通过将每次攻击视为一个计算受限的优化过程，并在共享的FLOPs轴上测量进展，启动了一个越狱的规模法则框架。我们的系统评估涵盖了四种代表性的越狱范式，包括基于优化的攻击、自我优化提示、基于采样的选择和遗传优化，跨越多个模型家族和规模，针对多种有害目标。我们通过将简单的饱和指数函数拟合到FLOPs-成功轨迹，研究了攻击者预算与攻击成功评分之间的规模法则，并从拟合曲线中得出可比的效率总结。从经验上看，与基于优化的方法相比，基于提示的范式往往是计算效率最高的。为了说明这一差距，我们将基于提示的更新视为一种优化视角，并通过同态比较显示基于提示的攻击在提示空间中更有效地进行优化。我们还表明，攻击在成功-隐蔽性操作点上占据不同的位置，基于提示的方法占据高成功、高隐蔽性的区域。最后，我们发现脆弱性与目标密切相关：涉及错误信息的伤害通常比其他非错误信息的伤害更容易引发。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the vulnerability of large language models to jailbreak attacks, aiming to systematically understand how the success of these attacks scales with the effort exerted by attackers across different methods and model families. The authors employ a scaling-law framework, treating each attack as a compute-bounded optimization procedure and measuring progress along a FLOPs axis, while evaluating four jailbreak paradigms including optimization-based attacks and self-refinement prompting. The findings reveal that prompting-based paradigms are generally more compute-efficient than optimization-based methods, with distinct success-stealthiness operating points, and highlight that the ease of eliciting harm varies significantly depending on the type of harm, particularly noting that misinformation-related harms are more readily achieved.
本研究探讨了大型语言模型对越狱攻击的脆弱性，旨在系统性地理解这些攻击的成功率如何随着攻击者努力的增加而变化，涵盖不同的方法和模型家族。作者采用了一个规模法则框架，将每次攻击视为一个受计算限制的优化过程，并在共享的FLOPs轴上测量进展，评估了包括基于优化的攻击和提示技术在内的四种越狱范式。研究结果表明，基于提示的方法通常比基于优化的方法更具计算效率，并且显示出不同的成功-隐蔽性操作点，强调了伤害的类型对引发伤害的难易程度有显著影响，尤其是虚假信息相关的伤害通常更容易实现。
Contrastive Reasoning Alignment: Reinforcement Learning from Hidden Representations
Authors: Haozheng Luo, Yimin Wang, Jiahao Yu, Binghui Wang, Yan Chen
First: 2026-03-18T03:00:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T03:00:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose CRAFT, a red-teaming alignment framework that leverages model reasoning capabilities and hidden representations to improve robustness against jailbreak attacks. Unlike prior defenses that operate primarily at the output level, CRAFT aligns large reasoning models to generate safety-aware reasoning traces by explicitly optimizing objectives defined over the hidden state space. Methodologically, CRAFT integrates contrastive representation learning with reinforcement learning to separate safe and unsafe reasoning trajectories, yielding a latent-space geometry that supports robust, reasoning-level safety alignment. Theoretically, we show that incorporating latent-textual consistency into GRPO eliminates superficially aligned policies by ruling them out as local optima. Empirically, we evaluate CRAFT on multiple safety benchmarks using two strong reasoning models, Qwen3-4B-Thinking and R1-Distill-Llama-8B, where it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art defenses such as IPO and SafeKey. Notably, CRAFT delivers an average 79.0% improvement in reasoning safety and 87.7% improvement in final-response safety over the base models, demonstrating the effectiveness of hidden-space reasoning alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对比推理对齐：从隐藏表示中进行强化学习
我们提出了CRAFT，一个利用模型推理能力和隐藏表示的红队对齐框架，以提高对越狱攻击的鲁棒性。与主要在输出层面操作的先前防御不同，CRAFT通过显式优化定义在隐藏状态空间上的目标，来对齐大型推理模型，以生成安全意识的推理轨迹。在方法论上，CRAFT将对比表示学习与强化学习结合，以区分安全和不安全的推理轨迹，从而产生支持鲁棒推理级安全对齐的潜在空间几何。理论上，我们证明将潜在文本一致性纳入GRPO可以通过将其排除为局部最优，消除表面对齐的策略。经验上，我们在多个安全基准上评估CRAFT，使用两个强大的推理模型Qwen3-4B-Thinking和R1-Distill-Llama-8B，CRAFT始终优于最先进的防御，如IPO和SafeKey。值得注意的是，CRAFT在推理安全性上平均提高了79.0%，在最终响应安全性上提高了87.7%，展示了隐藏空间推理对齐的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enhance the robustness of large reasoning models against jailbreak attacks by improving their safety alignment. The proposed method, CRAFT, utilizes a red-teaming alignment framework that combines contrastive representation learning with reinforcement learning to optimize reasoning trajectories in the hidden state space. Experimental results show that CRAFT significantly outperforms existing defenses, achieving an average improvement of 79.0% in reasoning safety and 87.7% in final-response safety when evaluated on multiple safety benchmarks using two reasoning models, Qwen3-4B-Thinking and R1-Distill-Llama-8B.
该研究的动机在于增强推理模型对越狱攻击的鲁棒性。所提出的方法CRAFT采用了一种红队对齐框架，结合对比表示学习和强化学习，通过关注隐藏状态表示而不仅仅是输出层来优化安全意识推理轨迹。实验结果表明，CRAFT在多个安全基准测试中使用两种先进推理模型时，推理安全性平均提高了79.0%，最终响应安全性提高了87.7%，超越了现有的防御方法如IPO和SafeKey。
MCP-38: A Comprehensive Threat Taxonomy for Model Context Protocol Systems (v1.0)
Authors: Yi Ting Shen, Kentaroh Toyoda, Alex Leung
First: 2026-03-18T02:22:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T02:22:41+00:00
Comments: v1.0
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Model Context Protocol (MCP) introduces a structurally distinct attack surface that existing threat frameworks, designed for traditional software systems or generic LLM deployments, do not adequately cover. This paper presents MCP-38, a protocol-specific threat taxonomy consisting of 38 threat categories (MCP-01 through MCP-38). The taxonomy was derived through a systematic four-phase methodology: protocol decomposition, multi-framework cross-mapping, real-world incident synthesis, and remediation-surface categorization. Each category is mapped to STRIDE, OWASP Top 10 for LLM Applications (2025, LLM01--LLM10), and the OWASP Top 10 for Agentic Applications (2026, ASI01--ASI10). MCP-38 addresses critical threats arising from MCP's semantic attack surface (tool description poisoning, indirect prompt injection, parasitic tool chaining, and dynamic trust violations), none of which are adequately captured by prior work. MCP-38 provides the definitional and empirical foundation for automated threat intelligence platforms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MCP-38：模型上下文协议系统的综合威胁分类法（v1.0）
模型上下文协议（MCP）引入了一种结构上独特的攻击面，现有的威胁框架无法充分覆盖，尤其是针对传统软件系统或通用LLM部署。本文提出了MCP-38，一种特定于协议的威胁分类法，包含38个威胁类别（MCP-01至MCP-38）。该分类法通过系统的四阶段方法论得出：协议分解、多框架交叉映射、现实世界事件综合和修复表面分类。每个类别都映射到STRIDE、2025年LLM应用的OWASP前10（LLM01--LLM10）和2026年代理应用的OWASP前10（ASI01--ASI10）。MCP-38解决了来自MCP语义攻击面的关键威胁（工具描述中毒、间接提示注入、寄生工具链和动态信任违规），这些威胁在之前的工作中均未得到充分捕捉。MCP-38为自动化威胁情报平台提供了定义和实证基础。

Key findings reveal that MCP-38 effectively identifies critical threats such as tool description poisoning and indirect prompt injection, which are not sufficiently covered by previous frameworks, thus providing a foundational resource for automated threat intelligence platforms.

Efficient LLM Safety Evaluation through Multi-Agent Debate
Authors: Dachuan Lin, Guobin Shen, Zihao Yang, Tianrong Liu, Dongcheng Zhao, Yi Zeng
First: 2025-11-09T14:06:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T02:09:28+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 5 figures, 10 tables. Updated abstract to fix an incconsistency issue with the main paper: HAJailBench size (12,000 -> 11,100)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) increasingly relies on LLM-as-a-judge pipelines, but strong judges can still be expensive to use at scale. We study whether structured multi-agent debate can improve judge reliability while keeping backbone size and cost modest. To do so, we introduce HAJailBench, a human-annotated jailbreak benchmark with 11,100 labeled interactions spanning diverse attack methods and target models, and we pair it with a Multi-Agent Judge framework in which critic, defender, and judge agents debate under a shared safety rubric. On HAJailBench, the framework improves over matched small-model prompt baselines and prior multi-agent judges, while remaining more economical than GPT-4o under the evaluated pricing snapshot. Ablation results further show that a small number of debate rounds is sufficient to capture most of the gain. Together, these results support structured, value-aligned debate as a practical design for scalable LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过多智能体辩论进行高效的LLM安全评估
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全评估越来越依赖于LLM作为评审的管道，但强大的评审在大规模使用时仍然成本高昂。我们研究结构化的多智能体辩论是否能在保持骨干规模和成本适中的同时提高评审的可靠性。为此，我们引入了HAJailBench，这是一个人类注释的越狱基准，包含11,100个标记的交互，涵盖多种攻击方法和目标模型，并将其与多智能体评审框架配对，在该框架中，批评者、防御者和评审代理在共享的安全标准下进行辩论。在HAJailBench上，该框架在匹配的小模型提示基线和先前的多智能体评审中表现更好，同时在评估的定价快照下仍然比GPT-4o更经济。消融结果进一步表明，少量的辩论轮次足以捕捉大部分增益。综合来看，这些结果支持结构化、价值对齐的辩论作为可扩展LLM安全评估的实用设计。

Detecting Data Poisoning in Code Generation LLMs via Black-Box, Vulnerability-Oriented Scanning
Authors: Shenao Yan, Shimaa Ahmed, Shan Jin, Sunpreet S. Arora, Yiwei Cai, Yizhen Wang, Yuan Hong
First: 2026-03-17T22:08:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T22:08:45+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Code generation large language models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into modern software development workflows. Recent work has shown that these models are vulnerable to backdoor and poisoning attacks that induce the generation of insecure code, yet effective defenses remain limited. Existing scanning approaches rely on token-level generation consistency to invert attack targets, which is ineffective for source code where identical semantics can appear in diverse syntactic forms. We present CodeScan, which, to the best of our knowledge, is the first poisoning-scanning framework tailored to code generation models. CodeScan identifies attack targets by analyzing structural similarities across multiple generations conditioned on different clean prompts. It combines iterative divergence analysis with abstract syntax tree (AST)-based normalization to abstract away surface-level variation and unify semantically equivalent code, isolating structures that recur consistently across generations. CodeScan then applies LLM-based vulnerability analysis to determine whether the extracted structures contain security vulnerabilities and flags the model as compromised when such a structure is found. We evaluate CodeScan against four representative attacks under both backdoor and poisoning settings across three real-world vulnerability classes. Experiments on 108 models spanning three architectures and multiple model sizes demonstrate 97%+ detection accuracy with substantially lower false positives than prior methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过黑箱、面向漏洞的扫描检测代码生成LLM中的数据中毒
代码生成大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地融入现代软件开发工作流程。最近的研究表明，这些模型容易受到后门和中毒攻击，从而导致生成不安全的代码，但有效的防御仍然有限。现有的扫描方法依赖于令牌级生成一致性来反转攻击目标，这对于源代码而言是无效的，因为相同的语义可以以不同的语法形式出现。我们提出了CodeScan，据我们所知，这是第一个针对代码生成模型的中毒扫描框架。CodeScan通过分析在不同干净提示下的多次生成的结构相似性来识别攻击目标。它结合了迭代发散分析和基于抽象语法树（AST）的规范化，以抽象掉表面级变异并统一语义等价的代码，隔离在多次生成中一致出现的结构。当发现这些结构包含安全漏洞时，CodeScan应用基于LLM的漏洞分析来判断，并将模型标记为已被攻陷。我们在三种真实世界漏洞类别下，对四种代表性攻击在后门和中毒设置中评估了CodeScan。对涵盖三种架构和多种模型大小的108个模型的实验表明，检测准确率超过97%，且假阳性率显著低于先前的方法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is the increasing integration of code generation large language models (LLMs) in software development and their vulnerability to backdoor and poisoning attacks that can lead to insecure code generation. The authors introduce CodeScan, a novel framework designed to detect data poisoning in code generation models by analyzing structural similarities in code generated from various clean prompts, utilizing iterative divergence analysis and abstract syntax tree normalization to unify semantically equivalent code. Experimental results show that CodeScan achieves over 97% detection accuracy against four representative attacks in both backdoor and poisoning scenarios, with significantly lower false positive rates compared to existing methods.
本研究的动机是代码生成大型语言模型（LLMs）在软件开发中的日益普及，以及它们易受后门和中毒攻击的影响，这可能导致生成不安全的代码。作者提出了CodeScan，这是一个新颖的框架，旨在通过分析从不同干净提示生成的代码的结构相似性来检测代码生成模型中的数据中毒，利用迭代发散分析和抽象语法树归一化。实验结果表明，CodeScan在四种代表性攻击下的检测准确率超过97%，同时显著降低了与现有方法相比的误报率。
Enhancing Moral Diagnosis and Correction in Large Language Models
Authors: Bocheng Chen, Xi Chen, Han Zi, Haitao Mao, Zimo Qi, Xitong Zhang, Kristen Johnson, Guangliang Liu
First: 2026-01-06T15:09:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T19:47:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Identifying specific moral errors in an input and generating appropriate corrections require moral sensitivity in large language models (LLMs), which is fundamental for developing their moral performance, yet a challenging task. This study leverages a pragmatic inference-based approach to enhance both the moral diagnosis and corrections of models. Crucially, our method generalizes across a diverse set of different tasks, including moral reasoning, toxic language detection, social bias detection, and jailbreaks, despite substantial differences in their semantic formulations. To enable such generalization, the study also introduces a unifying variable, pragmatic inference load, which captures the degree of pragmatic reasoning required across tasks. Experimental results show that our approach enables LLMs to produce high-quality diagnostic outputs of moral errors, make effective corrections, and consistently outperform a range of baseline methods. Further analyses reveal that these improvements do not arise from heuristic-based response patterns, but from learned inferential processes, highlighting the effectiveness of our approach.
中文标题/摘要
标题：增强大型语言模型的道德诊断与修正
识别输入中的特定道德错误并生成适当的修正需要大型语言模型（LLMs）具备道德敏感性，这对提升其道德表现至关重要，但也是一项具有挑战性的任务。本研究利用基于实用推理的方法来增强模型的道德诊断和修正。重要的是，我们的方法能够在包括道德推理、有害语言检测、社会偏见检测和越狱等多种不同任务中进行泛化，尽管它们的语义表述存在显著差异。为了实现这种泛化，研究还引入了一个统一变量——实用推理负载，捕捉不同任务所需的实用推理程度。实验结果表明，我们的方法使LLMs能够生成高质量的道德错误诊断输出，进行有效的修正，并在多种基线方法中始终表现优越。进一步分析表明，这些改进并非源于基于启发式的响应模式，而是来自学习的推理过程，突显了我们方法的有效性。

Experimental results demonstrate that this method significantly improves the quality of diagnostic outputs and corrections made by LLMs, consistently outperforming baseline methods, with improvements attributed to learned inferential processes rather than heuristic responses.

PEPPER: Perception-Guided Perturbation for Robust Backdoor Defense in Text-to-Image Diffusion Models
Authors: Oscar Chew, Po-Yi Lu, Jayden Lin, Kuan-Hao Huang, Hsuan-Tien Lin
First: 2025-11-20T22:21:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T19:46:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies show that text to image (T2I) diffusion models are vulnerable to backdoor attacks, where a trigger in the input prompt can steer generation toward harmful or unintended content. Beyond the trigger token itself, backdoor effects can spread to neighboring tokens in the text embedding space. To address this, we introduce PEPPER (PErcePtion Guided PERturbation), a backdoor defense that rewrites the caption into a semantically distant yet visually similar caption while adding unobstructive elements. With this rewriting strategy, PEPPER disrupt the trigger embedded in the input prompt, dilute the influence of trigger tokens and thereby achieve enhanced robustness. Experiments show that PEPPER is particularly effective against text encoder based attacks, substantially reducing attack success while preserving generation quality. Beyond this, PEPPER can be paired with any existing defenses yielding consistently stronger and generalizable robustness than any standalone method. Our code will be released on Github.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PEPPER：基于感知引导的扰动用于文本到图像扩散模型的强健后门防御
最近的研究表明，文本到图像（T2I）扩散模型易受后门攻击，其中输入提示中的触发器可以将生成引导到有害或意外的内容。除了触发器令牌本身，后门效应还可以扩散到文本嵌入空间中的相邻令牌。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了PEPPER（感知引导扰动），这是一种后门防御方法，通过将标题重写为语义上距离较远但视觉上相似的标题，同时添加不干扰的元素。通过这种重写策略，PEPPER破坏了嵌入输入提示中的触发器，稀释了触发器令牌的影响，从而实现了增强的鲁棒性。实验表明，PEPPER对基于文本编码器的攻击特别有效，显著降低了攻击成功率，同时保持了生成质量。此外，PEPPER可以与任何现有防御方法配对，提供比任何独立方法更强大和可泛化的鲁棒性。我们的代码将在Github上发布。

The motivation behind this research is to address the vulnerability of text-to-image diffusion models to backdoor attacks, where specific triggers in input prompts can lead to the generation of harmful content. The authors propose a method called PEPPER, which rewrites captions into semantically distant yet visually similar versions while incorporating unobtrusive elements to disrupt the trigger's influence. Experimental results demonstrate that PEPPER significantly reduces the success of text encoder-based attacks while maintaining the quality of generated images, and it can be effectively combined with existing defense mechanisms to enhance overall robustness.

Dynamic Meta-Layer Aggregation for Byzantine-Robust Federated Learning
Authors: Reek Das, Biplab Kanti Sen
First: 2026-03-17T17:54:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T17:54:00+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Federated Learning (FL) is increasingly applied in sectors like healthcare, finance, and IoT, enabling collaborative model training while safeguarding user privacy. However, FL systems are susceptible to Byzantine adversaries that inject malicious updates, which can severely compromise global model performance. Existing defenses tend to focus on specific attack types and fail against untargeted strategies, such as multi-label flipping or combinations of noise and backdoor patterns. To overcome these limitations, we propose FedAOT-a novel defense mechanism that counters multi-label flipping and untargeted poisoning attacks using a metalearning-inspired adaptive aggregation framework. FedAOT dynamically weights client updates based on their reliability, suppressing adversarial influence without relying on predefined thresholds or restrictive attack assumptions. Notably, FedAOT generalizes effectively across diverse datasets and a wide range of attack types, maintaining robust performance even in previously unseen scenarios. Experimental results demonstrate that FedAOT substantially improves model accuracy and resilience while maintaining computational efficiency, offering a scalable and practical solution for secure federated learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对拜占庭鲁棒的联邦学习的动态元层聚合
联邦学习（FL）越来越多地应用于医疗、金融和物联网等领域，实现协作模型训练，同时保护用户隐私。然而，FL系统容易受到拜占庭对手的攻击，这些对手注入恶意更新，严重影响全局模型性能。现有防御措施往往集中于特定攻击类型，无法应对无目标策略，如多标签翻转或噪声与后门模式的组合。为克服这些局限性，我们提出了FedAOT——一种新颖的防御机制，利用受元学习启发的自适应聚合框架对抗多标签翻转和无目标中毒攻击。FedAOT根据客户端更新的可靠性动态加权，抑制对抗性影响，而无需依赖预定义的阈值或限制性攻击假设。值得注意的是，FedAOT在不同数据集和广泛的攻击类型上有效泛化，即使在以前未见的场景中也能保持强大的性能。实验结果表明，FedAOT显著提高了模型的准确性和韧性，同时保持计算效率，为安全的联邦学习提供了可扩展和实用的解决方案。

Differential Harm Propensity in Personalized LLM Agents: The Curious Case of Mental Health Disclosure
Authors: Caglar Yildirim
First: 2026-03-17T16:16:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T16:16:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as tool-using agents, shifting safety concerns from harmful text generation to harmful task completion. Deployed systems often condition on user profiles or persistent memory, yet agent safety evaluations typically ignore personalization signals. To address this gap, we investigated how mental health disclosure, a sensitive and realistic user-context cue, affects harmful behavior in agentic settings. Building on the AgentHarm benchmark, we evaluated frontier and open-source LLMs on multi-step malicious tasks (and their benign counterparts) under controlled prompt conditions that vary user-context personalization (no bio, bio-only, bio+mental health disclosure) and include a lightweight jailbreak injection. Our results reveal that harmful task completion is non-trivial across models: frontier lab models (e.g., GPT 5.2, Claude Sonnet 4.5, Gemini 3-Pro) still complete a measurable fraction of harmful tasks, while an open model (DeepSeek 3.2) exhibits substantially higher harmful completion. Adding a bio-only context generally reduces harm scores and increases refusals. Adding an explicit mental health disclosure often shifts outcomes further in the same direction, though effects are modest and not uniformly reliable after multiple-testing correction. Importantly, the refusal increase also appears on benign tasks, indicating a safety--utility trade-off via over-refusal. Finally, jailbreak prompting sharply elevates harm relative to benign conditions and can weaken or override the protective shift induced by personalization. Taken together, our results indicate that personalization can act as a weak protective factor in agentic misuse settings, but it is fragile under minimal adversarial pressure, highlighting the need for personalization-aware evaluations and safeguards that remain robust across user-context conditions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：个性化LLM代理中的差异性危害倾向：心理健康披露的奇特案例
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被用作工具使用代理，安全问题的关注点从有害文本生成转向有害任务完成。部署的系统通常基于用户档案或持久记忆进行条件设置，但代理安全评估通常忽视个性化信号。为了解决这一差距，我们研究了心理健康披露这一敏感且现实的用户上下文线索如何影响代理环境中的有害行为。基于AgentHarm基准，我们在控制提示条件下评估了前沿和开源LLM在多步骤恶意任务（及其良性对应任务）上的表现，这些条件变化了用户上下文个性化（无生物信息，仅生物信息，生物信息+心理健康披露），并包括轻量级越狱注入。我们的结果显示，在模型之间，有害任务完成并非微不足道：前沿实验室模型（如GPT 5.2、Claude Sonnet 4.5、Gemini 3-Pro）仍然完成了一定比例的有害任务，而一个开放模型（DeepSeek 3.2）则表现出显著更高的有害完成率。添加仅生物信息的上下文通常会降低危害评分并增加拒绝率。添加明确的心理健康披露通常会进一步推动结果朝同一方向发展，尽管效果适度且在多重测试校正后并不均匀可靠。重要的是，拒绝率的增加也出现在良性任务上，表明通过过度拒绝存在安全与效用的权衡。最后，越狱提示相对于良性条件显著提高了危害，并可能削弱或覆盖个性化所带来的保护性变化。综合来看，我们的结果表明，个性化可以在代理误用环境中作为一种弱保护因素，但在最小对抗压力下是脆弱的，强调了需要进行个性化意识评估和在用户上下文条件下保持稳健的保护措施。

The study employs the AgentHarm benchmark to evaluate both frontier and open-source LLMs on multi-step malicious tasks, varying user-context personalization conditions. From Vulnerabilities to Remediation: A Systematic Literature Review of LLMs in Code Security
Authors: Enna Basic, Alberto Giaretta
First: 2024-12-19T16:20:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T16:08:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have emerged as powerful tools for automating programming tasks, including security-related ones. However, they can also introduce vulnerabilities during code generation, fail to detect existing vulnerabilities, or report nonexistent ones. This systematic literature review investigates the security benefits and drawbacks of using LLMs for code-related tasks. In particular, it focuses on the types of vulnerabilities introduced by LLMs when generating code. Moreover, it analyzes the capabilities of LLMs to detect and fix vulnerabilities, and examines how prompting strategies impact these tasks. Finally, it examines how data poisoning attacks impact LLMs performance in the aforementioned tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从漏洞到修复：大型语言模型在代码安全中的系统文献综述
大型语言模型（LLMs）已成为自动化编程任务（包括与安全相关的任务）的强大工具。然而，它们在代码生成过程中也可能引入漏洞，未能检测到现有漏洞，或报告不存在的漏洞。本系统文献综述研究了使用LLMs进行代码相关任务的安全优势和缺点。特别关注LLMs在生成代码时引入的漏洞类型。此外，分析了LLMs检测和修复漏洞的能力，并考察了提示策略如何影响这些任务。最后，研究了数据中毒攻击如何影响LLMs在上述任务中的表现。

The findings reveal that while LLMs can automate certain security tasks, they also have significant limitations, including the introduction of new vulnerabilities and challenges posed by data poisoning attacks that affect their performance in vulnerability detection and remediation.

REFORGE: Multi-modal Attacks Reveal Vulnerable Concept Unlearning in Image Generation Models
Authors: Yong Zou, Haoran Li, Fanxiao Li, Shenyang Wei, Yunyun Dong, Li Tang, Wei Zhou, Renyang Liu
Venue: ICME 2026
First: 2026-03-17T14:29:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:29:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICME 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent progress in image generation models (IGMs) enables high-fidelity content creation but also amplifies risks, including the reproduction of copyrighted content and the generation of offensive content. Image Generation Model Unlearning (IGMU) mitigates these risks by removing harmful concepts without full retraining. Despite growing attention, the robustness under adversarial inputs, particularly image-side threats in black-box settings, remains underexplored. To bridge this gap, we present REFORGE, a black-box red-teaming framework that evaluates IGMU robustness via adversarial image prompts. REFORGE initializes stroke-based images and optimizes perturbations with a cross-attention-guided masking strategy that allocates noise to concept-relevant regions, balancing attack efficacy and visual fidelity. Extensive experiments across representative unlearning tasks and defenses demonstrate that REFORGE significantly improves attack success rate while achieving stronger semantic alignment and higher efficiency than involved baselines. These results expose persistent vulnerabilities in current IGMU methods and highlight the need for robustness-aware unlearning against multi-modal adversarial attacks. Our code is at: https://github.com/Imfatnoily/REFORGE.
中文标题/摘要
标题：REFORGE：多模态攻击揭示图像生成模型中的脆弱概念遗忘
最近图像生成模型（IGMs）的进展使高保真内容创作成为可能，但也加大了风险，包括版权内容的再现和冒犯性内容的生成。图像生成模型遗忘（IGMU）通过去除有害概念而无需完全重训练来减轻这些风险。尽管受到越来越多的关注，但在对抗性输入下的鲁棒性，特别是在黑箱环境中的图像侧威胁，仍然未得到充分探索。为填补这一空白，我们提出了REFORGE，一个黑箱红队框架，通过对抗性图像提示评估IGMU的鲁棒性。REFORGE初始化基于笔画的图像，并使用交叉注意力引导的掩蔽策略优化扰动，将噪声分配到与概念相关的区域，平衡攻击效果和视觉保真度。在代表性的遗忘任务和防御措施中进行的广泛实验表明，REFORGE显著提高了攻击成功率，同时实现了比相关基线更强的语义对齐和更高的效率。这些结果揭示了当前IGMU方法中的持续脆弱性，并强调了针对多模态对抗攻击的鲁棒性意识遗忘的必要性。我们的代码在：https://github.com/Imfatnoily/REFORGE。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the vulnerabilities in image generation models (IGMs) related to the unlearning of harmful concepts, which is crucial for mitigating risks such as copyright infringement and the generation of offensive content. The authors introduce REFORGE, a black-box red-teaming framework that assesses the robustness of image generation model unlearning (IGMU) through adversarial image prompts, utilizing a stroke-based image initialization and a cross-attention-guided masking strategy to optimize perturbations. Experimental results demonstrate that REFORGE significantly enhances the attack success rate while achieving better semantic alignment and efficiency compared to existing baselines, revealing ongoing weaknesses in current IGMU methods and underscoring the necessity for robustness in unlearning against multi-modal adversarial threats.
本研究的动机在于解决图像生成模型（IGMs）在生成高保真内容时所带来的脆弱性，这可能导致版权侵犯和生成冒犯性内容等问题。作者提出了REFORGE，这是一个黑箱红队框架，旨在评估图像生成模型去学习（IGMU）在黑箱场景下对抗性输入的鲁棒性。通过广泛的实验，REFORGE在攻击成功率方面显著提高，同时在语义对齐和效率上优于现有基线，揭示了当前IGMU方法中的关键弱点，并强调了在多模态对抗威胁下去学习方法的鲁棒性需求。
Malicious Or Not: Adding Repository Context to Agent Skill Classification
Authors: Florian Holzbauer, David Schmidt, Gabriel Gegenhuber, Sebastian Schrittwieser, Johanna Ullrich
First: 2026-03-17T14:27:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:27:35+00:00
Comments: 23 Pages, 10 Figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agent skills extend local AI agents, such as Claude Code or Open Claw, with additional functionality, and their popularity has led to the emergence of dedicated skill marketplaces, similar to app stores for mobile applications. Simultaneously, automated skill scanners were introduced, analyzing the skill description available in SKILL.md, to verify their benign behavior. The results for individual market places mark up to 46.8% of skills as malicious. In this paper, we present the largest empirical security analysis of the AI agent skill ecosystem, questioning this high classification of malicious skills. Therefore, we collect 238,180 unique skills from three major distribution platforms and GitHub to systematically analyze their type and behavior. This approach substantially reduces the number of skills flagged as non-benign by security scanners to only 0.52% which remain in malicious flagged repositories. Consequently, out methodology substantially reduces false positives and provides a more robust view of the ecosystem's current risk surface. Beyond that, we extend the security analysis from the mere investigation of the skill description to a comparison of its congruence with the GitHub repository the skill is embedded in, providing additional context. Furthermore, our analysis also uncovers several, by now undocumented real-world attack vectors, namely hijacking skills hosted on abandoned GitHub repositories.
中文标题/摘要
标题：恶意与否：为代理技能分类添加仓库上下文
代理技能扩展了本地AI代理，如Claude Code或Open Claw，提供额外功能，其受欢迎程度导致了专门技能市场的出现，类似于移动应用的应用商店。同时，引入了自动化技能扫描器，分析SKILL.md中可用的技能描述，以验证其良性行为。个别市场的结果显示高达46.8%的技能被标记为恶意。在本文中，我们呈现了AI代理技能生态系统中最大的实证安全分析，质疑这种高比例的恶意技能分类。因此，我们从三个主要分发平台和GitHub收集了238,180个独特技能，以系统地分析其类型和行为。这种方法显著减少了被安全扫描器标记为非良性的技能数量，仅剩0.52%仍在恶意标记的仓库中。因此，我们的方法显著减少了误报，并提供了生态系统当前风险表面的更稳健视图。除此之外，我们将安全分析从对技能描述的简单调查扩展到与技能嵌入的GitHub仓库的一致性比较，提供额外的上下文。此外，我们的分析还揭示了几个目前未记录的现实世界攻击向量，即劫持托管在被遗弃的GitHub仓库上的技能。
Summary / 总结

The authors conducted a comprehensive empirical analysis by collecting 238,180 unique skills from three major distribution platforms and GitHub to evaluate their types and behaviors. Poisoning the Pixels: Revisiting Backdoor Attacks on Semantic Segmentation
Authors: Guangsheng Zhang, Huan Tian, Leo Zhang, Tianqing Zhu, Ming Ding, Wanlei Zhou, Bo Liu
First: 2026-03-17T11:42:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:42:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Semantic segmentation models are widely deployed in safety-critical applications such as autonomous driving, yet their vulnerability to backdoor attacks remains largely underexplored. Prior segmentation backdoor studies transfer threat settings from existing image classification tasks, focusing primarily on object-to-background mis-segmentation. In this work, we revisit the threats by systematically examining backdoor attacks tailored to semantic segmentation. We identify four coarse-grained attack vectors (Object-to-Object, Object-to-Background, Background-to-Object, and Background-to-Background attacks), as well as two fine-grained vectors (Instance-Level and Conditional attacks). To formalize these attacks, we introduce BADSEG, a unified framework that optimizes trigger designs and applies label manipulation strategies to maximize attack performance while preserving victim model utility. Extensive experiments across diverse segmentation architectures on benchmark datasets demonstrate that BADSEG achieves high attack effectiveness with minimal impact on clean samples. We further evaluate six representative defenses and find that they fail to reliably mitigate our attacks, revealing critical gaps in current defenses. Finally, we demonstrate that these vulnerabilities persist in recent emerging architectures, including transformer-based networks and the Segment Anything Model (SAM), thereby compromising their security. Our work reveals previously overlooked security vulnerabilities in semantic segmentation, and motivates the development of defenses tailored to segmentation-specific threat models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：毒化像素：重新审视语义分割中的后门攻击
语义分割模型广泛应用于安全关键的场景，如自动驾驶，但其对后门攻击的脆弱性仍然未得到充分探讨。之前的分割后门研究将威胁设置从现有的图像分类任务转移，主要关注对象与背景的错误分割。在本研究中，我们通过系统地检查针对语义分割的后门攻击重新审视这些威胁。我们识别出四种粗粒度攻击向量（对象对对象、对象对背景、背景对对象和背景对背景攻击），以及两种细粒度向量（实例级和条件攻击）。为了形式化这些攻击，我们引入了BADSEG，一个统一框架，优化触发器设计并应用标签操控策略，以最大化攻击性能，同时保持受害模型的效用。在基准数据集上对多种分割架构进行的广泛实验表明，BADSEG在对干净样本影响最小的情况下实现了高攻击有效性。我们进一步评估了六种代表性防御措施，发现它们未能可靠地减轻我们的攻击，揭示了当前防御中的关键缺口。最后，我们展示了这些脆弱性在最近的新兴架构中仍然存在，包括基于变换器的网络和Segment Anything Model (SAM)，从而危及其安全性。我们的工作揭示了语义分割中被忽视的安全脆弱性，并激励开发针对特定分割威胁模型的防御措施。

Over-the-air White-box Attack on the Wav2Vec Speech Recognition Neural Network
Authors: Protopopov Alexey

Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automatic speech recognition systems based on neural networks are vulnerable to adversarial attacks that alter transcriptions in a malicious way. Recent works in this field have focused on making attacks work in over-the-air scenarios, however such attacks are typically detectable by human hearing, limiting their potential applications. In the present work we explore different approaches of making over-the-air attacks less detectable, as well as the impact these approaches have on the attacks' effectiveness.

Amnesia: Adversarial Semantic Layer Specific Activation Steering in Large Language Models
Authors: Ali Raza, Gurang Gupta, Nikolay Matyunin, Jibesh Patra
First: 2026-03-10T09:41:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T08:26:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Warning: This article includes red-teaming experiments, which contain examples of compromised LLM responses that may be offensive or upsetting. Large Language Models (LLMs) have the potential to create harmful content, such as generating sophisticated phishing emails and assisting in writing code of harmful computer viruses. Thus, it is crucial to ensure their safe and responsible response generation. To reduce the risk of generating harmful or irresponsible content, researchers have developed techniques such as reinforcement learning with human feedback to align LLM's outputs with human values and preferences. However, it is still undetermined whether such measures are sufficient to prevent LLMs from generating interesting responses. In this study, we propose Amnesia, a lightweight activation-space adversarial attack that manipulates internal transformer states to bypass existing safety mechanisms in open-weight LLMs. Through experimental analysis on state-of-the-art, open-weight LLMs, we demonstrate that our attack effectively circumvents existing safeguards, enabling the generation of harmful content without the need for any fine-tuning or additional training. Our experiments on benchmark datasets show that the proposed attack can induce various antisocial behaviors in LLMs. These findings highlight the urgent need for more robust security measures in open-weight LLMs and underscore the importance of continued research to prevent their potential misuse.
中文标题/摘要
标题：失忆症：大语言模型中的对抗语义层特定激活引导
警告：本文包含红队实验，其中包含可能令人反感或不安的被攻陷的LLM响应示例。大语言模型（LLMs）有潜力生成有害内容，例如生成复杂的网络钓鱼邮件和协助编写有害计算机病毒的代码。因此，确保它们的安全和负责任的响应生成至关重要。为了降低生成有害或不负责任内容的风险，研究人员开发了诸如人类反馈强化学习等技术，以使LLM的输出与人类价值观和偏好对齐。然而，目前尚不确定这些措施是否足以防止LLM生成有趣的响应。在本研究中，我们提出了失忆症，这是一种轻量级的激活空间对抗攻击，操纵内部变换器状态以绕过开放权重LLM中的现有安全机制。通过对最先进的开放权重LLM进行实验分析，我们证明了我们的攻击有效地规避了现有的安全措施，使得生成有害内容无需任何微调或额外训练。我们在基准数据集上的实验表明，所提出的攻击可以诱发LLM中的各种反社会行为。这些发现突显了在开放权重LLM中迫切需要更强大的安全措施，并强调了继续研究以防止其潜在滥用的重要性。

CoMAI: A Collaborative Multi-Agent Framework for Robust and Equitable Interview Evaluation
Authors: Gengxin Sun, Ruihao Yu, Liangyi Yin, Yunqi Yang, Bin Zhang, Zhiwei Xu
First: 2026-03-17T07:44:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:44:12+00:00
Comments: Gengxin Sun and Ruihao Yu contributed equally to this research. Bin Zhang and Zhiwei Xu are the corresponding authors. 11 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Ensuring robust and fair interview assessment remains a key challenge in AI-driven evaluation. This paper presents CoMAI, a general-purpose multi-agent interview framework designed for diverse assessment scenarios. In contrast to monolithic single-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs), CoMAI employs a modular task-decomposition architecture coordinated through a centralized finite-state machine. The system comprises four agents specialized in question generation, security, scoring, and summarization. These agents work collaboratively to provide multi-layered security defenses against prompt injection, support multidimensional evaluation with adaptive difficulty adjustment, and enable rubric-based structured scoring that reduces subjective bias. Experimental results demonstrate that CoMAI achieved 90.47% accuracy, 83.33% recall, and 84.41% candidate satisfaction. These results highlight CoMAI as a robust, fair, and interpretable paradigm for AI-driven interview assessment.
中文标题/摘要

Structured Semantic Cloaking for Jailbreak Attacks on Large Language Models
Authors: Xiaobing Sun, Perry Lam, Shaohua Li, Zizhou Wang, Rick Siow Mong Goh, Yong Liu, Liangli Zhen
First: 2026-03-17T07:20:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:20:48+00:00
Comments: 15 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern LLMs employ safety mechanisms that extend beyond surface-level input filtering to latent semantic representations and generation-time reasoning, enabling them to recover obfuscated malicious intent during inference and refuse accordingly, and rendering many surface-level obfuscation jailbreak attacks ineffective. We propose Structured Semantic Cloaking (S2C), a novel multi-dimensional jailbreak attack framework that manipulates how malicious semantic intent is reconstructed during model inference. S2C strategically distributes and reshapes semantic cues such that full intent consolidation requires multi-step inference and long-range co-reference resolution within deeper latent representations. The framework comprises three complementary mechanisms: (1) Contextual Reframing, which embeds the request within a plausible high-stakes scenario to bias the model toward compliance; (2) Content Fragmentation, which disperses the semantic signature of the request across disjoint prompt segments; and (3) Clue-Guided Camouflage, which disguises residual semantic cues while embedding recoverable markers that guide output generation. By delaying and restructuring semantic consolidation, S2C degrades safety triggers that depend on coherent or explicitly reconstructed malicious intent at decoding time, while preserving sufficient instruction recoverability for functional output generation. We evaluate S2C across multiple open-source and proprietary LLMs using HarmBench and JBB-Behaviors, where it improves Attack Success Rate (ASR) by 12.4% and 9.7%, respectively, over the current SOTA. Notably, S2C achieves substantial gains on GPT-5-mini, outperforming the strongest baseline by 26% on JBB-Behaviors. We also analyse which combinations perform best against broad families of models, and characterise the trade-off between the extent of obfuscation versus input recoverability on jailbreak success.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对大型语言模型的结构化语义隐蔽技术用于越狱攻击
现代大型语言模型（LLMs）采用的安全机制超越了表层输入过滤，涉及潜在语义表示和生成时推理，使其能够在推理过程中恢复模糊的恶意意图并相应拒绝，从而使许多表层模糊越狱攻击无效。我们提出了结构化语义隐蔽技术（S2C），这是一种新颖的多维越狱攻击框架，操控恶意语义意图在模型推理过程中的重构方式。S2C战略性地分配和重塑语义线索，使得完全意图整合需要多步推理和深层潜在表示中的长距离共指解析。该框架包括三种互补机制：（1）上下文重构，将请求嵌入到一个合理的高风险场景中，以偏向模型的合规性；（2）内容碎片化，将请求的语义特征分散到不相连的提示段中；（3）线索引导伪装，伪装残余语义线索，同时嵌入可恢复的标记以指导输出生成。通过延迟和重构语义整合，S2C降低了依赖于解码时连贯或明确重构的恶意意图的安全触发器，同时保留了足够的指令可恢复性以生成功能性输出。我们在多个开源和专有的LLM上使用HarmBench和JBB-Behaviors评估S2C，结果显示其攻击成功率（ASR）分别提高了12.4%和9.7%，超越了当前的最先进技术。值得注意的是，S2C在GPT-5-mini上取得了显著的提升，在JBB-Behaviors上超越了最强基线26%。我们还分析了哪些组合在广泛的模型家族中表现最佳，并描述了模糊程度与输入可恢复性之间的权衡。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the limitations of existing jailbreak attacks on large language models (LLMs), which are often thwarted by advanced safety mechanisms that detect and reject malicious intent. The authors propose a novel framework called Structured Semantic Cloaking (S2C), which manipulates the reconstruction of malicious semantic intent during model inference through three mechanisms: Contextual Reframing, Content Fragmentation, and Clue-Guided Camouflage. Experimental results demonstrate that S2C significantly enhances the Attack Success Rate (ASR) by 12.4% and 9.7% on HarmBench and JBB-Behaviors, respectively, and achieves a 26% improvement over the strongest baseline on GPT-5-mini, highlighting its effectiveness across various LLMs while balancing obfuscation and recoverability.
本研究的动机在于解决现有大型语言模型（LLM）中安全机制的局限性，这些机制能够在推理过程中有效过滤恶意意图。作者提出了一种名为结构化语义隐蔽（S2C）的新型多维越狱攻击框架，该框架通过战略性地分配和重塑语义线索来操控恶意语义意图的重构。实验结果表明，S2C在HarmBench和JBB-Behaviors上分别提高了12.4%和9.7%的攻击成功率（ASR），并在GPT-5-mini上比最强基线提高了26%，突显了其在各种LLM中的有效性，同时平衡了隐蔽性和输入可恢复性。
Adversarial attacks against Modern Vision-Language Models
Authors: Alejandro Paredes La Torre
First: 2026-03-17T04:55:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T04:55:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study adversarial robustness of open-source vision-language model (VLM) agents deployed in a self-contained e-commerce environment built to simulate realistic pre-deployment conditions. We evaluate two agents, LLaVA-v1.5-7B and Qwen2.5-VL-7B, under three gradient-based attacks: the Basic Iterative Method (BIM), Projected Gradient Descent (PGD), and a CLIP-based spectral attack. Against LLaVA, all three attacks achieve substantial attack success rates (52.6%, 53.8%, and 66.9% respectively), demonstrating that simple gradient-based methods pose a practical threat to open-source VLM agents. Qwen2.5-VL proves significantly more robust across all attacks (6.5%, 7.7%, and 15.5%), suggesting meaningful architectural differences in adversarial resilience between open-source VLM families. These findings have direct implications for the security evaluation of VLM agents prior to commercial deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对现代视觉-语言模型的对抗攻击
我们研究了在一个自包含的电子商务环境中部署的开源视觉-语言模型（VLM）代理的对抗鲁棒性，该环境旨在模拟现实的预部署条件。我们评估了两个代理，LLaVA-v1.5-7B 和 Qwen2.5-VL-7B，在三种基于梯度的攻击下：基本迭代方法（BIM）、投影梯度下降（PGD）和基于CLIP的谱攻击。针对LLaVA，所有三种攻击都达到了可观的攻击成功率（分别为52.6%、53.8%和66.9%），表明简单的基于梯度的方法对开源VLM代理构成了实际威胁。Qwen2.5-VL在所有攻击中表现出显著更强的鲁棒性（分别为6.5%、7.7%和15.5%），这表明开源VLM家族之间在对抗韧性方面存在重要的架构差异。这些发现对VLM代理在商业部署前的安全评估具有直接影响。

Malice in Agentland: Down the Rabbit Hole of Backdoors in the AI Supply Chain
Authors: Léo Boisvert, Abhay Puri, Chandra Kiran Reddy Evuru, Nazanin Sepahvand, Nicolas Chapados, Quentin Cappart, Alexandre Lacoste, Krishnamurthy Dj Dvijotham, Alexandre Drouin
First: 2025-10-03T12:47:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T19:02:48+00:00
Comments: 27 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While finetuning AI agents on interaction data -- such as web browsing or tool use -- improves their capabilities, it also introduces critical security vulnerabilities within the agentic AI supply chain. We show that adversaries can effectively poison the data collection pipeline at multiple stages to embed hard-to-detect backdoors that, when triggered, cause unsafe or malicious behavior. We formalize three realistic threat models across distinct layers of the supply chain: direct poisoning of finetuning data, pre-backdoored base models, and environment poisoning, a novel attack vector that exploits vulnerabilities specific to agentic training pipelines. Evaluated on two widely adopted agentic benchmarks, all three threat models prove effective: poisoning only a small number of demonstrations is sufficient to embed a backdoor that causes an agent to leak confidential user information with over 80\% success.
中文标题/摘要
标题：代理领域的恶意行为：人工智能供应链后门的兔子洞
在交互数据（如网页浏览或工具使用）上微调人工智能代理可以提高其能力，但也在代理人工智能供应链中引入了关键的安全漏洞。我们展示了对手可以有效地在多个阶段毒化数据收集管道，以嵌入难以检测的后门，这些后门在触发时会导致不安全或恶意的行为。我们在供应链的不同层次上形式化了三种现实的威胁模型：微调数据的直接毒化、预先后门化的基础模型和环境毒化，这是一种利用特定于代理训练管道的漏洞的新型攻击向量。在两个广泛采用的代理基准上进行评估，所有三种威胁模型都证明是有效的：仅毒化少量演示就足以嵌入一个后门，使代理以超过80%的成功率泄露机密用户信息。

Experimental results on two widely adopted benchmarks reveal that even a small number of poisoned demonstrations can effectively embed backdoors, leading to over 80% success in causing agents to leak confidential user information.
本研究探讨了在对交互数据进行微调时，AI代理中引入的安全漏洞，强调了对手可以通过污染数据收集管道并嵌入后门的潜力。研究正式化了三种威胁模型：微调数据的直接污染、预先植入后门的基础模型和环境污染，这些模型针对代理训练管道中的特定弱点。实验结果表明，所有三种模型均有效，通过仅污染少量示例即可嵌入后门，导致机密用户信息泄露的成功率超过80%。
Evolving Contextual Safety in Multi-Modal Large Language Models via Inference-Time Self-Reflective Memory
Authors: Ce Zhang, Jinxi He, Junyi He, Katia Sycara, Yaqi Xie
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-16T18:32:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T18:32:26+00:00
Comments: Accepted at CVPR 2026. Project page: https://echosafe-mllm.github.io
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Multi-modal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have achieved remarkable performance across a wide range of visual reasoning tasks, yet their vulnerability to safety risks remains a pressing concern. While prior research primarily focuses on jailbreak defenses that detect and refuse explicitly unsafe inputs, such approaches often overlook contextual safety, which requires models to distinguish subtle contextual differences between scenarios that may appear similar but diverge significantly in safety intent. In this work, we present MM-SafetyBench++, a carefully curated benchmark designed for contextual safety evaluation. Specifically, for each unsafe image-text pair, we construct a corresponding safe counterpart through minimal modifications that flip the user intent while preserving the underlying contextual meaning, enabling controlled evaluation of whether models can adapt their safety behaviors based on contextual understanding. Further, we introduce EchoSafe, a training-free framework that maintains a self-reflective memory bank to accumulate and retrieve safety insights from prior interactions. By integrating relevant past experiences into current prompts, EchoSafe enables context-aware reasoning and continual evolution of safety behavior during inference. Extensive experiments on various multi-modal safety benchmarks demonstrate that EchoSafe consistently achieves superior performance, establishing a strong baseline for advancing contextual safety in MLLMs. All benchmark data and code are available at https://echosafe-mllm.github.io.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过推理时自反记忆在多模态大型语言模型中演变的上下文安全性
多模态大型语言模型（MLLMs）在广泛的视觉推理任务中取得了显著的性能，但它们对安全风险的脆弱性仍然是一个紧迫的问题。尽管先前的研究主要集中在检测和拒绝显式不安全输入的越狱防御上，但此类方法往往忽视了上下文安全，这要求模型区分在安全意图上可能看似相似但在细微上下文差异上显著不同的场景。在本研究中，我们提出了MM-SafetyBench++，这是一个精心策划的基准，用于上下文安全评估。具体而言，对于每个不安全的图像-文本对，我们通过最小修改构建相应的安全对，以翻转用户意图，同时保留潜在的上下文含义，从而实现对模型是否能够根据上下文理解调整其安全行为的控制评估。此外，我们引入了EchoSafe，这是一个无训练的框架，维护一个自反记忆库，以积累和检索来自先前交互的安全见解。通过将相关的过去经验整合到当前提示中，EchoSafe使得在推理过程中能够进行上下文感知推理和安全行为的持续演变。在各种多模态安全基准上的广泛实验表明，EchoSafe始终实现了卓越的性能，为推进MLLMs中的上下文安全建立了强有力的基线。所有基准数据和代码可在https://echosafe-mllm.github.io获取。

The authors developed MM-SafetyBench++, a benchmark for evaluating contextual safety by creating safe counterparts for unsafe image-text pairs, allowing for controlled assessments of model adaptability to contextual differences. They also introduced EchoSafe, a framework that utilizes a self-reflective memory bank to enhance context-aware reasoning during inference. Experimental results show that EchoSafe significantly outperforms existing methods on various multi-modal safety benchmarks, establishing a new standard for contextual safety in MLLMs.

ClawWorm: Self-Propagating Attacks Across LLM Agent Ecosystems
Authors: Yihao Zhang, Zeming Wei, Xiaokun Luan, Chengcan Wu, Zhixin Zhang, Jiangrong Wu, Haolin Wu, Huanran Chen, Jun Sun, Meng Sun
First: 2026-03-16T17:55:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T17:55:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous LLM-based agents increasingly operate as long-running processes forming densely interconnected multi-agent ecosystems, whose security properties remain largely unexplored. In particular, OpenClaw, an open-source platform with over 40{,}000 active instances, has stood out recently with its persistent configurations, tool-execution privileges, and cross-platform messaging capabilities. In this work, we present ClawWorm, the first self-replicating worm attack against a production-scale agent framework, achieving a fully autonomous infection cycle initiated by a single message: the worm first hijacks the victim's core configuration to establish persistent presence across session restarts, then executes an arbitrary payload upon each reboot, and finally propagates itself to every newly encountered peer without further attacker intervention. We evaluate the attack on a controlled testbed across three distinct infection vectors and three payload types, demonstrating high success rates in end-to-end infection, sustained multi-hop propagation, and payload independence from the worm mechanism. We analyse the architectural root causes underlying these vulnerabilities and propose defence strategies targeting each identified trust boundary. Code and samples will be released upon completion of responsible disclosure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ClawWorm：跨LLM代理生态系统的自我传播攻击
基于LLM的自主代理越来越多地作为长期运行的进程，形成密切互联的多代理生态系统，其安全属性仍然 largely 未被探索。特别是，OpenClaw，一个拥有超过40,000个活跃实例的开源平台，因其持久配置、工具执行权限和跨平台消息传递能力而脱颖而出。在这项工作中，我们提出了ClawWorm，这是针对生产规模代理框架的第一个自我复制蠕虫攻击，实现在单个消息启动的完全自主感染周期：蠕虫首先劫持受害者的核心配置，以在会话重启中建立持久存在，然后在每次重启时执行任意有效载荷，最后在没有进一步攻击者干预的情况下将自身传播到每个新遇到的对等体。我们在一个受控测试环境中评估了该攻击，涵盖三种不同的感染向量和三种有效载荷类型，展示了端到端感染、高持续多跳传播和有效载荷与蠕虫机制独立性的高成功率。我们分析了这些漏洞的架构根本原因，并提出了针对每个识别的信任边界的防御策略。代码和样本将在负责任披露完成后发布。

Experimental results demonstrate high success rates in achieving end-to-end infection, sustained propagation across multiple hops, and payload independence, while also identifying architectural vulnerabilities and proposing targeted defense strategies.

HAMLOCK: HArdware-Model LOgically Combined attacK
Authors: Sanskar Amgain, Daniel Lobo, Atri Chatterjee, Swarup Bhunia, Fnu Suya
First: 2025-10-22T00:31:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T16:55:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted to usenix security 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The growing use of third-party hardware accelerators (e.g., FPGAs, ASICs) for deep neural networks (DNNs) introduces new security vulnerabilities. Conventional model-level backdoor attacks, which only poison a model's weights to misclassify inputs with a specific trigger, are often detectable because the entire attack logic is embedded within the model (i.e., software), creating a traceable layer-by-layer activation path. This paper introduces the HArdware-Model Logically Combined Attack (HAMLOCK), a far stealthier threat that distributes the attack logic across the hardware-software boundary. The software (model) is now only minimally altered by tuning the activations of few neurons to produce uniquely high activation values when a trigger is present. A malicious hardware Trojan detects those unique activations by monitoring the corresponding neurons' most significant bit or the 8-bit exponents and triggers another hardware Trojan to directly manipulate the final output logits for misclassification. This decoupled design is highly stealthy, as the model itself contains no complete backdoor activation path as in conventional attacks and hence, appears fully benign. Empirically, across benchmarks like MNIST, CIFAR10, GTSRB, and ImageNet, HAMLOCK achieves a near-perfect attack success rate with a negligible clean accuracy drop. More importantly, HAMLOCK circumvents the state-of-the-art model-level defenses without any adaptive optimization. The hardware Trojan is also undetectable, incurring area and power overheads as low as 0.01%, which is easily masked by process and environmental noise. Our findings expose a critical vulnerability at the hardware-software interface, demanding new cross-layer defenses against this emerging threat.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HAMLOCK: 硬件-模型逻辑组合攻击
第三方硬件加速器（如FPGA、ASIC）在深度神经网络（DNN）中的日益使用引入了新的安全漏洞。传统的模型级后门攻击仅通过污染模型的权重来误分类带有特定触发器的输入，通常是可检测的，因为整个攻击逻辑嵌入在模型中（即软件），形成可追踪的逐层激活路径。本文介绍了硬件-模型逻辑组合攻击（HAMLOCK），这是一种更隐蔽的威胁，将攻击逻辑分布在硬件和软件边界之间。软件（模型）仅通过调整少数神经元的激活来产生在触发器存在时独特的高激活值，几乎没有改变。恶意硬件特洛伊木马通过监控相应神经元的最高有效位或8位指数来检测这些独特的激活，并触发另一个硬件特洛伊木马直接操纵最终输出的logits以实现误分类。这种解耦设计非常隐蔽，因为模型本身不包含传统攻击中的完整后门激活路径，因此看起来完全良性。在MNIST、CIFAR10、GTSRB和ImageNet等基准测试中，HAMLOCK实现了近乎完美的攻击成功率，且干净准确率下降微乎其微。更重要的是，HAMLOCK在没有任何自适应优化的情况下规避了最先进的模型级防御。硬件特洛伊木马也不可检测，面积和功耗开销低至0.01%，这很容易被工艺和环境噪声掩盖。我们的发现揭示了硬件-软件接口的关键漏洞，要求针对这一新兴威胁制定新的跨层防御。
Summary / 总结
The increasing reliance on third-party hardware accelerators for deep neural networks has raised new security concerns, particularly regarding backdoor attacks that are detectable due to their embedded logic within the model. This paper presents the HArdware-Model Logically Combined Attack (HAMLOCK), which cleverly distributes the attack logic across the hardware-software boundary, requiring only minimal alterations to the model while utilizing a hardware Trojan to exploit unique neuron activations for misclassification. Experimental results demonstrate that HAMLOCK achieves a near-perfect attack success rate across various benchmarks, including MNIST and ImageNet, with minimal impact on clean accuracy and the ability to bypass existing model-level defenses, highlighting a significant vulnerability at the hardware-software interface that necessitates new cross-layer security measures.
随着对第三方硬件加速器在深度神经网络中使用的增加，新的安全隐患也随之而来，尤其是由于模型级实现而容易被检测的后门攻击。本文提出了硬件-模型逻辑组合攻击（HAMLOCK），巧妙地将攻击逻辑分布在硬件和软件边界上，使模型的改动最小，同时利用恶意硬件特洛伊木马根据特定神经元的激活值操纵输出logits。实验结果表明，HAMLOCK在包括MNIST和ImageNet在内的多个基准测试中实现了近乎完美的攻击成功率，且仅有轻微的干净准确率下降，同时有效绕过现有的模型级防御，并以最小的开销保持不可检测性。
TabKD: Tabular Knowledge Distillation through Interaction Diversity of Learned Feature Bins
Authors: Shovon Niverd Pereira, Krishna Khadka, Yu Lei
First: 2026-03-16T16:12:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T16:12:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Data-free knowledge distillation enables model compression without original training data, critical for privacy-sensitive tabular domains. However, existing methods does not perform well on tabular data because they do not explicitly address feature interactions, the fundamental way tabular models encode predictive knowledge. We identify interaction diversity, systematic coverage of feature combinations, as an essential requirement for effective tabular distillation. To operationalize this insight, we propose TabKD, which learns adaptive feature bins aligned with teacher decision boundaries, then generates synthetic queries that maximize pairwise interaction coverage. Across 4 benchmark datasets and 4 teacher architectures, TabKD achieves highest student-teacher agreement in 14 out of 16 configurations, outperforming 5 state-of-the-art baselines. We further show that interaction coverage strongly correlates with distillation quality, validating our core hypothesis. Our work establishes interaction-focused exploration as a principled framework for tabular model extraction.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TabKD：通过学习特征箱的交互多样性进行表格知识蒸馏
无数据知识蒸馏使得在没有原始训练数据的情况下进行模型压缩，这对隐私敏感的表格领域至关重要。然而，现有方法在表格数据上表现不佳，因为它们没有明确处理特征交互，这是表格模型编码预测知识的基本方式。我们确定交互多样性，即特征组合的系统覆盖，是有效表格蒸馏的基本要求。为了实现这一见解，我们提出了TabKD，它学习与教师决策边界对齐的自适应特征箱，然后生成最大化成对交互覆盖的合成查询。在4个基准数据集和4个教师架构中，TabKD在16种配置中的14种中实现了最高的学生-教师一致性，超越了5个最先进的基线。我们进一步表明，交互覆盖与蒸馏质量强相关，验证了我们的核心假设。我们的工作确立了以交互为中心的探索作为表格模型提取的原则框架。

The motivation behind this research is to improve data-free knowledge distillation for tabular data, which is crucial in privacy-sensitive contexts but often underperforms due to a lack of focus on feature interactions. The authors propose a method called TabKD that learns adaptive feature bins aligned with teacher decision boundaries and generates synthetic queries to maximize pairwise interaction coverage. Experimental results demonstrate that TabKD achieves the highest student-teacher agreement in 14 out of 16 configurations across four benchmark datasets and four teacher architectures, significantly outperforming five state-of-the-art baselines and confirming that interaction coverage is strongly correlated with distillation quality.
本研究的动机是改善隐私敏感领域的表格数据的无数据知识蒸馏，但由于缺乏对特征交互的关注，通常表现不佳。作者提出了一种名为TabKD的方法，该方法学习与教师决策边界对齐的自适应特征箱，并生成合成查询以最大化成对交互覆盖。实验结果表明，TabKD在四个基准数据集和四种教师架构中，在16种配置中有14种达到了最高的学生-教师一致性，超越了五种最先进的基线，并确认了交互覆盖与蒸馏质量之间的强相关性。
Amplification Effects in Test-Time Reinforcement Learning: Safety and Reasoning Vulnerabilities
Authors: Vanshaj Khattar, Md Rafi ur Rashid, Moumita Choudhury, Jing Liu, Toshiaki Koike-Akino, Ming Jin, Ye Wang
First: 2026-03-16T15:28:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:28:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time training (TTT) has recently emerged as a promising method to improve the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs), in which the model directly learns from test data without access to labels. However, this reliance on test data also makes TTT methods vulnerable to harmful prompt injections. In this paper, we investigate safety vulnerabilities of TTT methods, where we study a representative self-consistency-based test-time learning method: test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL), a recent TTT method that improves LLM reasoning by rewarding self-consistency using majority vote as a reward signal. We show that harmful prompt injection during TTRL amplifies the model's existing behaviors, i.e., safety amplification when the base model is relatively safe, and harmfulness amplification when it is vulnerable to the injected data. In both cases, there is a decline in reasoning ability, which we refer to as the reasoning tax. We also show that TTT methods such as TTRL can be exploited adversarially using specially designed "HarmInject" prompts to force the model to answer jailbreak and reasoning queries together, resulting in stronger harmfulness amplification. Overall, our results highlight that TTT methods that enhance LLM reasoning by promoting self-consistency can lead to amplification behaviors and reasoning degradation, highlighting the need for safer TTT methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：测试时强化学习中的放大效应：安全性和推理脆弱性
测试时训练（TTT）最近成为一种有前景的方法，以提高大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，其中模型直接从测试数据中学习，而无需访问标签。然而，这种对测试数据的依赖也使TTT方法容易受到有害提示注入的影响。本文研究了TTT方法的安全性脆弱性，重点研究一种代表性的基于自一致性的测试时学习方法：测试时强化学习（TTRL），这是一种通过使用多数投票作为奖励信号来奖励自一致性，从而提高LLM推理的最新TTT方法。我们表明，在TTRL过程中，有害提示注入会放大模型的现有行为，即当基础模型相对安全时的安全性放大，以及当其对注入数据脆弱时的有害性放大。在这两种情况下，推理能力都会下降，我们称之为推理税。我们还表明，像TTRL这样的TTT方法可以通过特别设计的“HarmInject”提示进行对抗性利用，迫使模型同时回答越狱和推理查询，从而导致更强的有害性放大。总体而言，我们的结果强调，通过促进自一致性来增强LLM推理的TTT方法可能导致放大行为和推理退化，突显了对更安全的TTT方法的需求。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the safety vulnerabilities associated with test-time training (TTT) methods, particularly in the context of large language models (LLMs) that learn from test data without labels. The authors investigate a specific TTT method called test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL), which enhances reasoning by rewarding self-consistency through majority voting. The key findings reveal that harmful prompt injections during TTRL can amplify both safe and harmful behaviors of the model, leading to a decline in reasoning ability, termed the reasoning tax, and demonstrating that TTT methods can be adversarially exploited to increase harmfulness amplification.
本研究探讨了测试时训练（TTT）方法的安全漏洞，特别关注测试时强化学习（TTRL），该方法通过自一致性奖励来增强大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力。研究表明，在TTRL过程中，恶意提示注入会放大模型的安全性和有害性行为，导致推理能力下降，称为推理税。此外，研究结果还表明，TTT方法可以通过特定提示被对抗性利用，从而导致有害性放大的增加和推理能力进一步下降，强调了需要更安全的TTT方法。
RESQ: A Unified Framework for REliability- and Security Enhancement of Quantized Deep Neural Networks
Authors: Ali Soltan Mohammadi, Samira Nazari, Ali Azarpeyvand, Mahdi Taheri, Milos Krstic, Michael Huebner, Christian Herglotz, Tara Ghasempouri
First: 2026-03-16T15:22:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:22:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This work proposes a unified three-stage framework that produces a quantized DNN with balanced fault and attack robustness. The first stage improves attack resilience via fine-tuning that desensitizes feature representations to small input perturbations. The second stage reinforces fault resilience through fault-aware fine-tuning under simulated bit-flip faults. Finally, a lightweight post-training adjustment integrates quantization to enhance efficiency and further mitigate fault sensitivity without degrading attack resilience. Experiments on ResNet18, VGG16, EfficientNet, and Swin-Tiny in CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and GTSRB show consistent gains of up to 10.35% in attack resilience and 12.47% in fault resilience, while maintaining competitive accuracy in quantized networks. The results also highlight an asymmetric interaction in which improvements in fault resilience generally increase resilience to adversarial attacks, whereas enhanced adversarial resilience does not necessarily lead to higher fault resilience.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RESQ：量化深度神经网络可靠性和安全性增强的统一框架
本工作提出了一个统一的三阶段框架，生成具有平衡故障和攻击鲁棒性的量化DNN。第一阶段通过微调提高攻击韧性，使特征表示对小输入扰动不敏感。第二阶段通过在模拟位翻转故障下进行故障感知微调来增强故障韧性。最后，轻量级后训练调整集成量化，以提高效率并进一步减轻故障敏感性，而不降低攻击韧性。在CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100和GTSRB上的ResNet18、VGG16、EfficientNet和Swin-Tiny实验显示，攻击韧性提高了最多10.35%，故障韧性提高了12.47%，同时在量化网络中保持了竞争力的准确性。结果还强调了一种不对称的相互作用，即故障韧性的提高通常会增加对对抗攻击的韧性，而增强的对抗韧性不一定会导致更高的故障韧性。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the need for improved reliability and security in quantized deep neural networks (DNNs). The authors propose a unified three-stage framework that enhances both fault and attack robustness. The first stage involves fine-tuning to increase resilience against adversarial attacks, the second stage employs fault-aware fine-tuning to bolster fault resilience, and the final stage applies a lightweight post-training adjustment for efficient quantization. Experimental results demonstrate improvements of up to 10.35% in attack resilience and 12.47% in fault resilience across various models, while maintaining competitive accuracy, revealing an asymmetric interaction where enhanced fault resilience generally improves adversarial robustness, but not vice versa.
本研究旨在提高量化深度神经网络（DNN）的可靠性和安全性。作者提出了一个统一的三阶段框架，以增强故障和攻击的鲁棒性：第一阶段通过微调提高攻击鲁棒性，第二阶段通过故障感知微调增强故障鲁棒性，最后阶段应用轻量级后训练调整以提高效率并降低故障敏感性。对包括ResNet18和VGG16在内的多种模型在多个数据集上的实验结果表明，攻击鲁棒性提高了最多10.35%，故障鲁棒性提高了12.47%，同时保持了竞争性的准确性，揭示了故障和攻击鲁棒性改善之间的不对称互动。
SFCoT: Safer Chain-of-Thought via Active Safety Evaluation and Calibration
Authors: Yu Pan, Wenlong Yu, Tiejun Wu, Xiaohu Ye, Qiannan Si, Guangquan Xu, Bin Wu
First: 2026-03-16T15:13:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:13:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in complex reasoning tasks. However, they remain highly susceptible to jailbreak attacks that undermine their safety alignment. Existing defense mechanisms typically rely on post hoc filtering applied only to the final output, leaving intermediate reasoning steps unmonitored and vulnerable to adversarial manipulation. To address this gap, this paper proposes a SaFer Chain-of-Thought (SFCoT) framework, which proactively evaluates and calibrates potentially unsafe reasoning steps in real time. SFCoT incorporates a three-tier safety scoring system alongside a multi-perspective consistency verification mechanism, designed to detect potential risks throughout the reasoning process. A dynamic intervention module subsequently performs targeted calibration to redirect reasoning trajectories toward safe outcomes. Experimental results demonstrate that SFCoT reduces the attack success rate from $58.97\%$ to $12.31\%$, demonstrating it as an effective and efficient LLM safety enhancement method without a significant decline in general performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SFCoT：通过主动安全评估和校准实现更安全的思维链
大型语言模型（LLMs）在复杂推理任务中展现了显著的能力。然而，它们仍然高度易受破坏攻击，影响其安全对齐。现有的防御机制通常依赖于仅应用于最终输出的事后过滤，导致中间推理步骤未被监控，易受对抗性操控。为了解决这一问题，本文提出了一种更安全的思维链（SFCoT）框架，能够实时主动评估和校准潜在不安全的推理步骤。SFCoT结合了三级安全评分系统和多角度一致性验证机制，旨在检测推理过程中的潜在风险。随后，动态干预模块执行针对性校准，以将推理轨迹引导至安全结果。实验结果表明，SFCoT将攻击成功率从58.97%降低至12.31%，证明其作为一种有效且高效的LLM安全增强方法，且未显著降低整体性能。

Experimental results indicate that SFCoT significantly reduces the attack success rate from 58.97% to 12.31%, proving its effectiveness in improving LLM safety without substantially affecting overall performance.

AI Evasion and Impersonation Attacks on Facial Re-Identification with Activation Map Explanations
Authors: Noe Claudel, Weisi Guo, Yang Xing
First: 2026-03-16T15:12:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T15:12:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Facial identification systems are increasingly deployed in surveillance and yet their vulnerability to adversarial evasion and impersonation attacks pose a critical risk. This paper introduces a novel framework for generating adversarial patches capable of both evasion and impersonation attacks against deep re-identification models across non-overlapping cameras. Unlike prior approaches that require iterative patch optimisation for each target, our method employs a conditional encoder-decoder network to synthesize adversarial patches in a single forward pass, guided by multi-scale features from source and target images. The patches are optimised with a dual adversarial objective comprising of pull and push terms. To enhance imperceptibility and aid physical deployment, we further integrate naturalistic patch generation using pre-trained latent diffusion models. Experiments on standard pedestrian (Market-1501, DukeMTMCreID) and facial recognition benchmarks (CelebA-HQ, PubFig) datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method. Our adversarial evasion attacks reduce mean Average Precision from 90% to 0.4% in white-box settings and from 72% to 0.4% in black-box settings, showing strong cross-model generalization. In targeted impersonation attacks, our framework achieves a success rate of 27% on CelebA-HQ, competing with other patch-based methods. We go further to use clustering of activation maps to interpret which features are most used by adversarial attacks and propose a pathway for future countermeasures. The results highlight the practicality of adversarial patch attacks on retrieval-based systems and underline the urgent need for robust defense strategies.

面部识别系统在监控中越来越多地被部署，但其对对抗性规避和冒充攻击的脆弱性构成了重大风险。本文提出了一种新颖的框架，用于生成能够对深度再识别模型进行规避和冒充攻击的对抗性补丁，适用于非重叠摄像头。与之前需要对每个目标进行迭代补丁优化的方法不同，我们的方法采用条件编码-解码网络，通过源图像和目标图像的多尺度特征在单次前向传递中合成对抗性补丁。这些补丁通过拉动和推动项组成的双重对抗目标进行优化。为了增强不可感知性并帮助物理部署，我们进一步整合了使用预训练潜在扩散模型的自然补丁生成。在标准行人（Market-1501，DukeMTMCreID）和面部识别基准（CelebA-HQ，PubFig）数据集上的实验表明了所提方法的有效性。我们的对抗性规避攻击在白盒设置中将平均精度从90%降低到0.4%，在黑盒设置中从72%降低到0.4%，显示出强大的跨模型泛化能力。在针对性冒充攻击中，我们的框架在CelebA-HQ上实现了27%的成功率，与其他基于补丁的方法相竞争。我们进一步使用激活图的聚类来解释对抗攻击最常用的特征，并提出未来对策的路径。结果突显了对抗性补丁攻击在基于检索的系统中的实用性，并强调了对强大防御策略的迫切需求。

How Vulnerable Are AI Agents to Indirect Prompt Injections? Insights from a Large-Scale Public Competition
Authors: Mateusz Dziemian, Maxwell Lin, Xiaohan Fu, Micha Nowak, Nick Winter, Eliot Jones, Andy Zou, Lama Ahmad, Kamalika Chaudhuri, Sahana Chennabasappa, Xander Davies, Lauren Deason, Benjamin L. Edelman, Tanner Emek, Ivan Evtimov, Jim Gust, Maia Hamin, Kat He, Klaudia Krawiecka, Riccardo Patana, Neil Perry, Troy Peterson, Xiangyu Qi, Javier Rando, Zifan Wang, Zihan Wang, Spencer Whitman, Eric Winsor, Arman Zharmagambetov, Matt Fredrikson, Zico Kolter
First: 2026-03-16T14:49:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T14:49:36+00:00
Comments: 38 pages, 16 figures. Newer version to cover Q1 competition results on latest models in progress. Code at https://github.com/grayswansecurity/ipi_arena_os Partial Dataset at https://huggingface.co/datasets/sureheremarv/ipi_arena_attacks
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
LLM based agents are increasingly deployed in high stakes settings where they process external data sources such as emails, documents, and code repositories. This creates exposure to indirect prompt injection attacks, where adversarial instructions embedded in external content manipulate agent behavior without user awareness. A critical but underexplored dimension of this threat is concealment: since users tend to observe only an agent's final response, an attack can conceal its existence by presenting no clue of compromise in the final user facing response while successfully executing harmful actions. This leaves users unaware of the manipulation and likely to accept harmful outcomes as legitimate. We present findings from a large scale public red teaming competition evaluating this dual objective across three agent settings: tool calling, coding, and computer use. The competition attracted 464 participants who submitted 272000 attack attempts against 13 frontier models, yielding 8648 successful attacks across 41 scenarios. All models proved vulnerable, with attack success rates ranging from 0.5% (Claude Opus 4.5) to 8.5% (Gemini 2.5 Pro). We identify universal attack strategies that transfer across 21 of 41 behaviors and multiple model families, suggesting fundamental weaknesses in instruction following architectures. Capability and robustness showed weak correlation, with Gemini 2.5 Pro exhibiting both high capability and high vulnerability. To address benchmark saturation and obsoleteness, we will endeavor to deliver quarterly updates through continued red teaming competitions. We open source the competition environment for use in evaluations, along with 95 successful attacks against Qwen that did not transfer to any closed source model. We share model-specific attack data with respective frontier labs and the full dataset with the UK AISI and US CAISI to support robustness research.

基于大型语言模型的代理越来越多地在高风险环境中部署，处理外部数据源，如电子邮件、文档和代码库。这使其暴露于间接提示注入攻击中，恶意指令嵌入在外部内容中，操控代理行为而用户却不知情。这一威胁的一个关键但未被充分探讨的维度是隐蔽性：由于用户往往只观察代理的最终响应，攻击可以通过在最终用户面对的响应中不呈现任何妥协线索来掩盖其存在，同时成功执行有害操作。这使得用户对操控毫无察觉，并可能将有害结果视为合法。我们展示了来自一场大规模公共红队竞赛的发现，该竞赛评估了这一双重目标在三种代理设置中的表现：工具调用、编码和计算机使用。竞赛吸引了464名参与者，提交了272000次攻击尝试，针对13个前沿模型，产生了8648次成功攻击，涵盖41种场景。所有模型均显示出脆弱性，攻击成功率从0.5%（Claude Opus 4.5）到8.5%（Gemini 2.5 Pro）不等。我们识别出跨21种行为和多个模型家族的通用攻击策略，表明指令跟随架构存在根本性弱点。能力和鲁棒性之间的相关性较弱，Gemini 2.5 Pro表现出高能力和高脆弱性。为了解决基准饱和和过时问题，我们将努力通过持续的红队竞赛提供季度更新。我们开源竞赛环境以供评估使用，并提供95次成功攻击的数据，这些攻击未能转移到任何闭源模型。我们与各前沿实验室分享模型特定的攻击数据，并将完整数据集分享给英国AISI和美国CAISI，以支持鲁棒性研究。
