Truth as a Compression Artifact in Language Model Training
Authors: Konstantin Krestnikov
First: 2026-03-12T09:52:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T14:11:02+00:00
Comments: v2: Significantly revised and polished the Abstract for improved clarity, readability, flow and academic tone while preserving all original results and numbers (83.1%, 67.0%, 57.7%) unchanged. Fixed placeholder GitHub link and minor typographical issues
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Why do language models trained on contradictory data prefer correct answers? In controlled experiments with small transformers (3.5M--86M parameters), we show that this preference tracks the compressibility structure of errors rather than truth per se. We train GPT-2 style models on corpora where each mathematical problem appears with both correct and incorrect solutions -- a denoising design that directly models conflicting information about the same fact. When errors are random, models extract the correct signal with accuracy scaling from 65% to 85% with model size. When errors follow a coherent alternative rule system, accuracy drops to chance (~45--51%): the model cannot distinguish the false system from truth. A multi-rule experiment reveals a sharp crossover: a single coherent alternative rule eliminates truth bias entirely, but adding a second competing rule restores most of it (47%->78%), with continued growth through N=10 (88%). The same pattern reproduces on real Wikipedia text (71% vs 46%). We propose the Compression--Consistency Principle as an explanatory hypothesis: in these settings, gradient descent favors the most compressible answer cluster, not truth per se. Truth bias emerges only when falsehood is structurally incoherent. Whether this principle extends to large-scale pretraining remains an open question.
中文标题/摘要
标题：语言模型训练中的真理作为压缩伪影
为什么在矛盾数据上训练的语言模型更倾向于正确答案？在小型变换器（3.5M--86M参数）的受控实验中，我们展示了这种偏好跟踪错误的可压缩性结构，而不是真理本身。我们在包含正确和错误解答的数学问题语料库上训练GPT-2风格的模型——一种去噪设计，直接建模关于同一事实的冲突信息。当错误是随机的时，模型提取正确信号的准确率随着模型规模从65%提升到85%。当错误遵循一致的替代规则系统时，准确率降至偶然水平（约45--51%）：模型无法区分虚假系统与真理。多规则实验揭示了一个明显的交叉点：单一一致的替代规则完全消除了真理偏见，但添加第二个竞争规则则恢复了大部分偏见（47%->78%），并在N=10时持续增长（88%）。在真实的维基百科文本中也重现了相同的模式（71%对46%）。我们提出压缩-一致性原则作为解释假设：在这些设置中，梯度下降更倾向于最可压缩的答案集，而不是单纯的真理。真理偏见仅在虚假结构不一致时出现。这个原则是否适用于大规模预训练仍然是一个悬而未决的问题。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates why language models trained on contradictory data tend to favor correct answers, motivated by the observation that this preference aligns with the compressibility of errors rather than the truth itself. The authors employed controlled experiments using small transformer models, training them on datasets containing both correct and incorrect solutions to mathematical problems. The findings reveal that when errors are random, the models achieve an accuracy ranging from 65% to 85% as model size increases, but when errors follow a coherent alternative rule system, accuracy drops to chance levels. A multi-rule experiment shows that a single coherent alternative rule eliminates truth bias, while introducing additional competing rules restores most of the bias, suggesting that gradient descent favors the most compressible answer cluster rather than truth in these contexts.
本研究探讨了为什么在矛盾数据上训练的语言模型倾向于选择正确答案，重点关注错误可压缩性与真理之间的关系。作者使用小型变换器模型进行控制实验，训练它们在包含正确和错误解的数学问题数据集上。研究结果显示，当错误是随机时，模型的准确率在65%到85%之间，但当错误遵循一致的替代规则系统时，准确率下降到约45-51%。多规则实验表明，单一一致的替代规则可以消除真理偏差，而引入额外的竞争规则则恢复了大部分偏差，准确率从47%提高到78%。在真实的维基百科文本中也观察到了这种模式，因此提出了压缩-一致性原则，认为梯度下降更倾向于选择最可压缩的答案集，而非真理本身，真理偏差仅在缺乏结构一致的虚假信息时出现。
Towards Model Extraction Attacks in GAN-Based Image Translation via Domain Shift Mitigation
Authors: Di Mi, Yanjun Zhang, Leo Yu Zhang, Shengshan Hu, Qi Zhong, Haizhuan Yuan, Shirui Pan
Venue: AAAI 2024
First: 2024-03-12T14:06:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T14:02:15+00:00
Comments: Accepted by AAAI 2024
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model extraction attacks (MEAs) enable an attacker to replicate the functionality of a victim deep neural network (DNN) model by only querying its API service remotely, posing a severe threat to the security and integrity of pay-per-query DNN-based services. Although the majority of current research on MEAs has primarily concentrated on neural classifiers, there is a growing prevalence of image-to-image translation (I2IT) tasks in our everyday activities. However, techniques developed for MEA of DNN classifiers cannot be directly transferred to the case of I2IT, rendering the vulnerability of I2IT models to MEA attacks often underestimated. This paper unveils the threat of MEA in I2IT tasks from a new perspective. Diverging from the traditional approach of bridging the distribution gap between attacker queries and victim training samples, we opt to mitigate the effect caused by the different distributions, known as the domain shift. This is achieved by introducing a new regularization term that penalizes high-frequency noise, and seeking a flatter minimum to avoid overfitting to the shifted distribution. Extensive experiments on different image translation tasks, including image super-resolution and style transfer, are performed on different backbone victim models, and the new design consistently outperforms the baseline by a large margin across all metrics. A few real-life I2IT APIs are also verified to be extremely vulnerable to our attack, emphasizing the need for enhanced defenses and potentially revised API publishing policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于GAN的图像翻译中的模型提取攻击及其领域转移缓解
模型提取攻击（MEAs）使攻击者能够通过远程查询受害者深度神经网络（DNN）模型的API服务来复制其功能，严重威胁按查询付费的DNN服务的安全性和完整性。尽管目前大多数关于MEAs的研究主要集中在神经分类器上，但图像到图像翻译（I2IT）任务在我们的日常活动中越来越普遍。然而，针对DNN分类器的MEA技术无法直接转移到I2IT的情况，这使得I2IT模型对MEA攻击的脆弱性常常被低估。本文从一个新视角揭示了I2IT任务中MEA的威胁。我们选择缓解由不同分布引起的影响，即领域转移，而不是传统的弥合攻击者查询和受害者训练样本之间的分布差距。这是通过引入一个新的正则化项来惩罚高频噪声，并寻求一个更平坦的最小值以避免对转移分布的过拟合。我们在不同的图像翻译任务上进行了广泛的实验，包括图像超分辨率和风格迁移，使用不同的基础受害者模型，新的设计在所有指标上始终大幅超越基线。我们还验证了一些现实生活中的I2IT API对我们的攻击极为脆弱，强调了增强防御和可能修订API发布政策的必要性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the security vulnerabilities posed by model extraction attacks (MEAs) in image-to-image translation (I2IT) tasks, which have been largely overlooked compared to neural classifiers. The authors propose a novel method that mitigates the effects of domain shift by introducing a regularization term that penalizes high-frequency noise, aiming to achieve a flatter minimum to prevent overfitting. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach significantly outperforms baseline methods across various image translation tasks, including super-resolution and style transfer, and reveals that several real-life I2IT APIs are highly susceptible to MEAs, highlighting the urgent need for improved defenses and policy revisions.
本研究的动机在于解决图像到图像翻译（I2IT）任务中模型提取攻击（MEA）所带来的安全漏洞，这些漏洞相比于神经分类器被大大忽视。作者提出了一种新方法，通过引入惩罚高频噪声的正则化项来减轻领域转移的影响，并旨在寻找更平坦的最小值以防止过拟合。实验结果表明，该方法在超分辨率和风格迁移等多种图像翻译任务中显著优于基线方法，并揭示了多个现实生活中的I2IT API对这些攻击高度敏感，强调了改善防御和修订API政策的紧迫性。
Directional Embedding Smoothing for Robust Vision Language Models
Authors: Ye Wang, Jing Liu, Toshiaki Koike-Akino
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-16T13:25:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T13:25:29+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026 Workshop on Agents in the Wild
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The safety and reliability of vision-language models (VLMs) are a crucial part of deploying trustworthy agentic AI systems. However, VLMs remain vulnerable to jailbreaking attacks that undermine their safety alignment to yield harmful outputs. In this work, we extend the Randomized Embedding Smoothing and Token Aggregation (RESTA) defense to VLMs and evaluate its performance against the JailBreakV-28K benchmark of multi-modal jailbreaking attacks. We find that RESTA is effective in reducing attack success rate over this diverse corpus of attacks, in particular, when employing directional embedding noise, where the injected noise is aligned with the original token embedding vectors. Our results demonstrate that RESTA can contribute to securing VLMs within agentic systems, as a lightweight, inference-time defense layer of an overall security framework.

视觉语言模型（VLMs）的安全性和可靠性是部署可信代理AI系统的重要组成部分。然而，VLMs仍然容易受到监狱破解攻击，这会破坏其安全对齐，导致有害输出。在这项工作中，我们将随机嵌入平滑和令牌聚合（RESTA）防御扩展到VLMs，并评估其在多模态监狱破解攻击的JailBreakV-28K基准上的表现。我们发现，RESTA在减少这一多样化攻击语料库的攻击成功率方面是有效的，特别是在采用方向嵌入噪声时，其中注入的噪声与原始令牌嵌入向量对齐。我们的结果表明，RESTA可以作为整体安全框架的轻量级推理时防御层，有助于保护代理系统中的VLMs。

AWARE: Audio Watermarking with Adversarial Resistance to Edits
Authors: Kosta Pavlović, Lazar Stanarević, Petar Nedić, Elena Nešović Slavko Kovačević, Igor Djurović
First: 2025-10-20T13:10:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:48:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Prevailing practice in learning-based audio watermarking is to pursue robustness by expanding the set of simulated distortions during training. However, such surrogates are narrow and prone to overfitting. This paper presents AWARE (Audio Watermarking with Adversarial Resistance to Edits), an alternative approach that avoids reliance on attack-simulation stacks and handcrafted differentiable distortions. Embedding is obtained through adversarial optimization in the time-frequency domain under a level-proportional perceptual budget. Detection employs a time-order-agnostic detector with a Bitwise Readout Head (BRH) that aggregates temporal evidence into one score per watermark bit, enabling reliable watermark decoding even under desynchronization and temporal cuts. Empirically, AWARE attains high audio quality and speech intelligibility (PESQ/STOI) and consistently low BER across various audio edits, often surpassing representative state-of-the-art learning-based systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AWARE：具有对编辑的对抗抵抗能力的音频水印
基于学习的音频水印的主流做法是通过扩展训练期间模拟失真的集合来追求鲁棒性。然而，这种替代方法狭窄且容易过拟合。本文提出了AWARE（具有对抗抵抗能力的音频水印），一种避免依赖攻击模拟堆栈和手工可微失真的替代方法。嵌入通过在时间-频率域下的对抗优化获得，遵循与感知预算成比例的水平。检测采用时间顺序无关的检测器，配备位读取头（BRH），将时间证据聚合为每个水印位的一个分数，即使在不同步和时间切割的情况下也能实现可靠的水印解码。实证表明，AWARE在各种音频编辑中实现了高音频质量和语音可懂度（PESQ/STOI），并且在不同音频编辑中始终保持低比特错误率（BER），通常超越代表性的最先进的基于学习的系统。

The authors introduce AWARE, an innovative method that utilizes adversarial optimization in the time-frequency domain for embedding watermarks, while employing a time-order-agnostic detector with a Bitwise Readout Head for reliable decoding. Experimental results demonstrate that AWARE achieves high audio quality and speech intelligibility, as well as consistently low bit error rates across various audio edits, outperforming existing state-of-the-art learning-based systems.
本研究的动机在于提高音频水印技术的鲁棒性，这些技术通常依赖于有限的模拟失真，可能导致过拟合。作者提出了AWARE，一种新颖的方法，通过在时频域中利用对抗优化来嵌入水印，避免传统的攻击模拟方法。实验结果表明，AWARE在音频质量和语音可懂度方面表现出色，PESQ和STOI的测量结果均高，同时在各种音频编辑中保持了较低的比特错误率，超越了现有的最先进学习系统。
Unsupervised Corpus Poisoning Attacks in Continuous Space for Dense Retrieval
Authors: Yongkang Li, Panagiotis Eustratiadis, Simon Lupart, Evangelos Kanoulas
Venue: SIGIR 2025
First: 2025-04-24T18:46:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T10:43:47+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted as a full paper at SIGIR 2025 and will be presented orally
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper concerns corpus poisoning attacks in dense information retrieval, where an adversary attempts to compromise the ranking performance of a search algorithm by injecting a small number of maliciously generated documents into the corpus. Our work addresses two limitations in the current literature. First, attacks that perform adversarial gradient-based word substitution search do so in the discrete lexical space, while retrieval itself happens in the continuous embedding space. We thus propose an optimization method that operates in the embedding space directly. Specifically, we train a perturbation model with the objective of maintaining the geometric distance between the original and adversarial document embeddings, while also maximizing the token-level dissimilarity between the original and adversarial documents. Second, it is common for related work to have a strong assumption that the adversary has prior knowledge about the queries. In this paper, we focus on a more challenging variant of the problem where the adversary assumes no prior knowledge about the query distribution (hence, unsupervised). Our core contribution is an adversarial corpus attack that is fast and effective. We present comprehensive experimental results on both in- and out-of-domain datasets, focusing on two related tasks: a top-1 attack and a corpus poisoning attack. We consider attacks under both a white-box and a black-box setting. Notably, our method can generate successful adversarial examples in under two minutes per target document; four times faster compared to the fastest gradient-based word substitution methods in the literature with the same hardware. Furthermore, our adversarial generation method generates text that is more likely to occur under the distribution of natural text (low perplexity), and is therefore more difficult to detect.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续空间中的无监督语料中毒攻击用于密集检索
本文涉及密集信息检索中的语料中毒攻击，攻击者试图通过将少量恶意生成的文档注入语料库来破坏搜索算法的排名性能。我们的工作解决了当前文献中的两个局限性。首先，执行对抗性基于梯度的词替换搜索的攻击是在离散词汇空间中进行的，而检索本身发生在连续嵌入空间中。因此，我们提出了一种直接在嵌入空间中操作的优化方法。具体而言，我们训练了一个扰动模型，旨在保持原始文档和对抗文档嵌入之间的几何距离，同时最大化原始文档和对抗文档之间的令牌级不相似性。其次，相关工作通常强假设攻击者对查询有先验知识。本文关注一个更具挑战性的变体，其中攻击者假设对查询分布没有先验知识（因此是无监督的）。我们的核心贡献是一个快速有效的对抗性语料攻击。我们在领域内和领域外的数据集上呈现了全面的实验结果，重点关注两个相关任务：top-1攻击和语料中毒攻击。我们考虑在白盒和黑盒设置下的攻击。值得注意的是，我们的方法可以在每个目标文档下生成成功的对抗示例，时间少于两分钟；与文献中相同硬件下最快的基于梯度的词替换方法相比，速度快四倍。此外，我们的对抗生成方法生成的文本在自然文本分布下更可能出现（低困惑度），因此更难以检测。

This paper investigates corpus poisoning attacks in dense information retrieval, motivated by the need to understand how adversaries can degrade search algorithm performance by injecting malicious documents. The authors propose a novel optimization method that operates directly in the continuous embedding space, training a perturbation model to maintain geometric distances between original and adversarial document embeddings while maximizing token-level dissimilarity. Experimental results demonstrate that their approach is both fast and effective, achieving successful adversarial example generation in under two minutes per target document, which is four times faster than existing gradient-based methods, while producing text that aligns closely with natural language distributions, making detection more challenging.
本文研究了在密集信息检索中进行语料库中毒攻击的问题，旨在提高搜索算法对对抗性操控的有效性。作者提出了一种直接在连续嵌入空间中操作的优化方法，训练一个扰动模型，以保持原始文档和对抗文档嵌入之间的几何距离，同时最大化标记级别的不相似性。实验结果表明，他们的方法能够在每个目标文档下生成成功的对抗示例，时间少于两分钟，显著快于现有的基于梯度的方法，同时生成的文本与自然文本分布高度一致，使得检测更加困难。
Beyond Benchmark Islands: Toward Representative Trustworthiness Evaluation for Agentic AI
Authors: Jinhu Qi, Yifan Li, Minghao Zhao, Wentao Zhang, Zijian Zhang, Yaoman Li, Irwin King
Venue: KDD 2026
First: 2026-03-16T08:51:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T08:51:33+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 1 figure. Submitted to KDD 2026 Blue Sky Track
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As agentic AI systems move beyond static question answering into open-ended, tool-augmented, and multi-step real-world workflows, their increased authority poses greater risks of system misuse and operational failures. However, current evaluation practices remain fragmented, measuring isolated capabilities such as coding, hallucination, jailbreak resistance, or tool use in narrowly defined settings. We argue that the central limitation is not merely insufficient coverage of evaluation dimensions, but the lack of a principled notion of representativeness: an agent's trustworthiness should be assessed over a representative socio-technical scenario distribution rather than a collection of disconnected benchmark instances. To this end, we propose the Holographic Agent Assessment Framework (HAAF), a systematic evaluation paradigm that characterizes agent trustworthiness over a scenario manifold spanning task types, tool interfaces, interaction dynamics, social contexts, and risk levels. The framework integrates four complementary components: (i) static cognitive and policy analysis, (ii) interactive sandbox simulation, (iii) social-ethical alignment assessment, and (iv) a distribution-aware representative sampling engine that jointly optimizes coverage and risk sensitivity -- particularly for rare but high-consequence tail risks that conventional benchmarks systematically overlook. These components are connected through an iterative Trustworthy Optimization Factory. Through cycles of red-team probing and blue-team hardening, this paradigm progressively narrows the vulnerabilities to meet deployment standards, shifting agent evaluation from benchmark islands toward representative, real-world trustworthiness. Code and data for the illustrative instantiation are available at https://github.com/TonyQJH/haaf-pilot.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越基准岛屿：面向代理人工智能的代表性可信度评估
随着代理人工智能系统从静态问答转向开放式、工具增强和多步骤的现实工作流程，其增强的权威性带来了更大的系统滥用和操作失败风险。然而，目前的评估实践仍然是碎片化的，仅在狭义定义的环境中测量孤立的能力，如编码、幻觉、越狱抵抗或工具使用。我们认为，主要限制不仅在于评估维度的覆盖不足，而在于缺乏原则性的代表性概念：代理的可信度应在代表性的社会技术场景分布上进行评估，而不是一系列不相关的基准实例。为此，我们提出了全息代理评估框架（HAAF），这是一种系统的评估范式，表征代理在跨越任务类型、工具接口、互动动态、社会背景和风险水平的场景流形上的可信度。该框架整合了四个互补组件：（i）静态认知和政策分析，（ii）互动沙盒模拟，（iii）社会伦理对齐评估，以及（iv）一个分布感知的代表性采样引擎，联合优化覆盖和风险敏感性——特别是对于传统基准系统性忽视的稀有但高后果的尾部风险。这些组件通过一个迭代的可信优化工厂连接。通过红队探测和蓝队强化的循环，这一范式逐步缩小脆弱性，以满足部署标准，将代理评估从基准岛屿转向代表性的现实可信度。示例实例的代码和数据可在 https://github.com/TonyQJH/haaf-pilot 获取。

The authors propose the Holographic Agent Assessment Framework (HAAF), which systematically evaluates agent trustworthiness across a diverse range of socio-technical scenarios. Key experimental findings indicate that HAAF effectively integrates various evaluation components, including cognitive analysis, interactive simulations, and ethical assessments, leading to improved identification of vulnerabilities and enhanced trustworthiness in real-world applications.
本研究的动机在于需要对日益用于复杂现实任务的代理人工智能系统进行更全面的评估，因为这些系统在被误用时会带来重大风险。作者提出了全息代理评估框架（HAAF），作为一种系统的评估方法，能够在多样的社会技术场景中评估代理的可信度，而不是孤立的基准测试。主要实验结果表明，HAAF有效整合了认知分析、互动模拟、社会伦理评估和代表性抽样引擎，从而改善了对脆弱性的识别，并增强了在现实应用中的可信度。
Rethinking LLM Watermark Detection in Black-Box Settings: A Non-Intrusive Third-Party Framework
Authors: Zhuoshang Wang, Yubing Ren, Yanan Cao, Fang Fang, Xiaoxue Li, Li Guo
First: 2026-03-16T08:28:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T08:28:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While watermarking serves as a critical mechanism for LLM provenance, existing secret-key schemes tightly couple detection with injection, requiring access to keys or provider-side scheme-specific detectors for verification. This dependency creates a fundamental barrier for real-world governance, as independent auditing becomes impossible without compromising model security or relying on the opaque claims of service providers. To resolve this dilemma, we introduce TTP-Detect, a pioneering black-box framework designed for non-intrusive, third-party watermark verification. By decoupling detection from injection, TTP-Detect reframes verification as a relative hypothesis testing problem. It employs a proxy model to amplify watermark-relevant signals and a suite of complementary relative measurements to assess the alignment of the query text with watermarked distributions. Extensive experiments across representative watermarking schemes, datasets and models demonstrate that TTP-Detect achieves superior detection performance and robustness against diverse attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在黑箱环境中重新思考LLM水印检测：一种非侵入式第三方框架
水印作为LLM来源的重要机制，现有的秘密密钥方案将检测与注入紧密耦合，要求访问密钥或提供方特定检测器进行验证。这种依赖性为现实世界的治理创造了根本障碍，因为独立审计在不妥协模型安全或依赖服务提供商不透明声明的情况下变得不可能。为了解决这一困境，我们引入了TTP-Detect，这是一种开创性的黑箱框架，旨在实现非侵入式的第三方水印验证。通过将检测与注入解耦，TTP-Detect将验证重新构建为相对假设检验问题。它采用代理模型来放大与水印相关的信号，并使用一系列互补的相对测量来评估查询文本与水印分布的一致性。针对代表性水印方案、数据集和模型的广泛实验表明，TTP-Detect在检测性能和对多种攻击的鲁棒性方面表现优越。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the limitations of existing watermark detection methods for large language models (LLMs), which require access to secret keys and specific detectors, hindering independent auditing. The authors propose TTP-Detect, a novel black-box framework that allows for non-intrusive third-party watermark verification by decoupling detection from injection and framing verification as a relative hypothesis testing problem. Experimental results show that TTP-Detect significantly outperforms existing methods in detection performance and demonstrates robustness against various attacks across multiple watermarking schemes, datasets, and models.
本研究的动机在于解决现有大型语言模型（LLM）水印检测方法的局限性，这些方法需要访问秘密密钥或特定检测器，从而阻碍独立审计和治理。作者提出了TTP-Detect，这是一种新颖的黑箱框架，允许非侵入式第三方水印验证，通过将检测与注入解耦并将其框架化为相对假设检验问题。实验结果表明，TTP-Detect在多个水印方案、数据集和模型中，在检测性能和对各种攻击的鲁棒性方面显著优于现有方法。
BackdoorIDS: Zero-shot Backdoor Detection for Pretrained Vision Encoder
Authors: Siquan Huang, Yijiang Li, Ningzhi Gao, Xingfu Yan, Leyu Shi, Ying Gao
First: 2026-03-12T08:32:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T08:21:21+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 10 figures, 6 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Self-supervised and multimodal vision encoders learn strong visual representations that are widely adopted in downstream vision tasks and large vision-language models (LVLMs). However, downstream users often rely on third-party pretrained encoders with uncertain provenance, exposing them to backdoor attacks. In this work, we propose BackdoorIDS, a simple yet effective zero-shot, inference-time backdoor samples detection method for pretrained vision encoders. BackdoorIDS is motivated by two observations: Attention Hijacking and Restoration. Under progressive input masking, a backdoored image initially concentrates attention on malicious trigger features. Once the masking ratio exceeds the trigger's robustness threshold, the trigger is deactivated, and attention rapidly shifts to benign content. This transition induces a pronounced change in the image embedding, whereas embeddings of clean images evolve more smoothly across masking progress. BackdoorIDS operationalizes this signal by extracting an embedding sequence along the masking trajectory and applying density-based clustering such as DBSCAN. An input is flagged as backdoored if its embedding sequence forms more than one cluster. Extensive experiments show that BackdoorIDS consistently outperforms existing defenses across diverse attack types, datasets, and model families. Notably, it is a plug-and-play approach that requires no retraining and operates fully zero-shot at inference time, making it compatible with a wide range of encoder architectures, including CNNs, ViTs, CLIP, and LLaVA-1.5.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BackdoorIDS：针对预训练视觉编码器的零样本后门检测
自监督和多模态视觉编码器学习强大的视觉表示，广泛应用于下游视觉任务和大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）。然而，下游用户通常依赖于来源不明的第三方预训练编码器，这使他们面临后门攻击。在本研究中，我们提出了BackdoorIDS，一种简单而有效的零样本推理时后门样本检测方法，专为预训练视觉编码器设计。BackdoorIDS的动机源于两个观察：注意力劫持和恢复。在逐步输入掩蔽下，后门图像最初将注意力集中在恶意触发特征上。一旦掩蔽比例超过触发器的鲁棒性阈值，触发器被停用，注意力迅速转向良性内容。这一过渡导致图像嵌入发生显著变化，而干净图像的嵌入在掩蔽进程中则更平滑地演变。BackdoorIDS通过沿掩蔽轨迹提取嵌入序列并应用基于密度的聚类（如DBSCAN）来实现这一信号。如果输入的嵌入序列形成多个聚类，则该输入被标记为后门。大量实验表明，BackdoorIDS在各种攻击类型、数据集和模型家族中始终优于现有防御。值得注意的是，它是一种即插即用的方法，无需重新训练，并在推理时完全零样本操作，使其与包括CNN、ViTs、CLIP和LLaVA-1.5在内的多种编码器架构兼容。

The motivation behind this research is the vulnerability of pretrained vision encoders to backdoor attacks, which can compromise the integrity of downstream vision tasks. The authors propose BackdoorIDS, a zero-shot detection method that identifies backdoored samples during inference by analyzing changes in image embeddings as input masking progresses. Experimental results demonstrate that BackdoorIDS effectively outperforms existing detection methods across various attack types and model architectures, highlighting its robustness and compatibility without the need for retraining.

Cheating Stereo Matching in Full-scale: Physical Adversarial Attack against Binocular Depth Estimation in Autonomous Driving
Authors: Kangqiao Zhao, Shuo Huai, Xurui Song, Jun Luo
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2025-11-18T11:45:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T07:06:52+00:00
Comments: AAAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Though deep neural models adopted to realize the perception of autonomous driving have proven vulnerable to adversarial examples, known attacks often leverage 2D patches and target mostly monocular perception. Therefore, the effectiveness of Physical Adversarial Examples (PAEs) on stereo-based binocular depth estimation remains largely unexplored. To this end, we propose the first texture-enabled physical adversarial attack against stereo matching models in the context of autonomous driving. Our method employs a 3D PAE with global camouflage texture rather than a local 2D patch-based one, ensuring both visual consistency and attack effectiveness across different viewpoints of stereo cameras. To cope with the disparity effect of these cameras, we also propose a new 3D stereo matching rendering module that allows the PAE to be aligned with real-world positions and headings in binocular vision. We further propose a novel merging attack that seamlessly blends the target into the environment through fine-grained PAE optimization. It has significantly enhanced stealth and lethality upon existing hiding attacks that fail to get seamlessly merged into the background. Extensive evaluations show that our PAEs can successfully fool the stereo models into producing erroneous depth information.

标题：全尺度欺骗立体匹配：针对自动驾驶中双目深度估计的物理对抗攻击
尽管用于实现自动驾驶感知的深度神经模型已被证明对对抗样本脆弱，但已知攻击通常利用2D补丁，主要针对单目感知。因此，物理对抗样本（PAEs）在基于立体的双目深度估计中的有效性仍然 largely 未被探索。为此，我们提出了首个针对自动驾驶中立体匹配模型的纹理增强物理对抗攻击。我们的方法采用具有全球伪装纹理的3D PAE，而不是基于局部2D补丁的方式，确保在立体相机的不同视角下视觉一致性和攻击有效性。为了应对这些相机的视差效应，我们还提出了一个新的3D立体匹配渲染模块，使PAE能够与双目视觉中的真实世界位置和方向对齐。我们进一步提出了一种新颖的合并攻击，通过细粒度的PAE优化将目标无缝融入环境中。它显著增强了现有隐藏攻击的隐蔽性和致命性，这些攻击未能与背景无缝融合。广泛的评估表明，我们的PAEs可以成功欺骗立体模型产生错误的深度信息。

The authors propose a novel texture-enabled physical adversarial attack that utilizes a 3D PAE with global camouflage texture, ensuring visual consistency and effectiveness across various viewpoints of stereo cameras. Latent-Mark: An Audio Watermark Robust to Neural Resynthesis
Authors: Yen-Shan Chen, Shih-Yu Lai, Ying-Jung Tsou, Yi-Cheng Lin, Bing-Yu Chen, Yun-Nung Chen, Hung-yi Lee, Shang-Tse Chen
First: 2026-03-05T15:51:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T06:51:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While existing audio watermarking techniques have achieved strong robustness against traditional digital signal processing (DSP) attacks, they remain vulnerable to neural resynthesis. This occurs because modern neural audio codecs act as semantic filters and discard the imperceptible waveform variations used in prior watermarking methods. To address this limitation, we propose Latent-Mark, the first zero-bit audio watermarking framework designed to survive semantic compression. Our key insight is that robustness to the encode-decode process requires embedding the watermark within the codec's invariant latent space. We achieve this by optimizing the audio waveform to induce a detectable directional shift in its encoded latent representation, while constraining perturbations to align with the natural audio manifold to ensure imperceptibility. To prevent overfitting to a single codec's quantization rules, we introduce Cross-Codec Optimization, jointly optimizing the waveform across multiple surrogate codecs to target shared latent invariants. Extensive evaluations demonstrate robust zero-shot transferability to unseen neural codecs, achieving state-of-the-art resilience against traditional DSP attacks while preserving perceptual imperceptibility. Our work inspires future research into universal watermarking frameworks capable of maintaining integrity across increasingly complex and diverse generative distortions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：潜在水印：一种对神经重合成鲁棒的音频水印
尽管现有的音频水印技术在抵御传统数字信号处理（DSP）攻击方面取得了强大的鲁棒性，但它们仍然容易受到神经重合成的影响。这是因为现代神经音频编解码器充当语义过滤器，丢弃了先前水印方法中使用的不可感知的波形变化。为了解决这一限制，我们提出了潜在水印，这是第一个旨在抵御语义压缩的零比特音频水印框架。我们的关键见解是，对编码-解码过程的鲁棒性需要将水印嵌入编解码器的不变潜在空间。我们通过优化音频波形来诱导其编码潜在表示中的可检测方向性偏移，同时限制扰动与自然音频流形对齐，以确保不可感知性。为了防止对单一编解码器量化规则的过拟合，我们引入了跨编解码器优化，联合优化多个替代编解码器中的波形，以针对共享的潜在不变性。广泛的评估表明，对未见过的神经编解码器具有强大的零-shot 可转移性，在保持感知不可感知性的同时，实现了对传统 DSP 攻击的最先进的抗性。我们的工作激励了未来对能够在日益复杂和多样化的生成失真中保持完整性的通用水印框架的研究。

Experimental results show that Latent-Mark achieves strong resilience against both traditional digital signal processing attacks and neural codecs, demonstrating effective zero-shot transferability to unseen codecs and paving the way for future universal watermarking frameworks.

Two Birds, One Projection: Harmonizing Safety and Utility in LVLMs via Inference-time Feature Projection
Authors: Yewon Han, Yumin Seol, EunGyung Kong, Minsoo Jo, Taesup Kim
First: 2026-03-16T04:59:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T04:59:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing jailbreak defence frameworks for Large Vision-Language Models often suffer from a safety utility tradeoff, where strengthening safety inadvertently degrades performance on general visual-grounded reasoning tasks. In this work, we investigate whether safety and utility are inherently antagonistic objectives. We focus on a modality induced bias direction consistently observed across datasets, which arises from suboptimal coupling between the Large Language Model backbone and visual encoders. We further demonstrate that this direction undermines performance on both tasks. Leveraging this insight, we propose Two Birds, One Projection, an efficient inference time jailbreak defence that projects cross-modal features onto the null space of the identified bias direction to remove the corresponding components. Requiring only a single forward pass, our method effectively breaks the conventional tradeoff, simultaneously improving both safety and utility across diverse benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双鸟，一投影：通过推理时特征投影协调大型视觉语言模型的安全性和实用性
现有的大型视觉语言模型的越狱防御框架常常面临安全性与实用性之间的权衡，增强安全性往往会无意中降低在一般视觉基础推理任务上的性能。在本研究中，我们探讨安全性和实用性是否本质上是对立的目标。我们关注在各数据集中一致观察到的模态诱导偏差方向，这源于大型语言模型主干与视觉编码器之间的次优耦合。我们进一步证明，这一方向削弱了两项任务的性能。利用这一见解，我们提出了“双鸟，一投影”，一种高效的推理时越狱防御方法，它将跨模态特征投影到识别的偏差方向的零空间中，以去除相应的成分。只需一次前向传递，我们的方法有效打破了传统的权衡，同时在多样化基准上提高了安全性和实用性。

The authors investigate the inherent antagonism between safety and utility by identifying a modality-induced bias direction that negatively impacts both objectives due to suboptimal integration between language models and visual encoders. They propose a novel method called Two Birds, One Projection, which projects cross-modal features onto the null space of the identified bias direction during inference, effectively enhancing both safety and utility without the need for multiple passes, as demonstrated through various benchmarks.

BadLLM-TG: A Backdoor Defender powered by LLM Trigger Generator
Authors: Ruyi Zhang, Heng Gao, Songlei Jian, Yusong Tan, Haifang Zhou
First: 2026-03-16T03:31:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T03:31:54+00:00
Comments: 5pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Backdoor attacks compromise model reliability by using triggers to manipulate outputs. Trigger inversion can accurately locate these triggers via a generator and is therefore critical for backdoor defense. However, the discrete nature of text prevents existing noise-based trigger generator from being applied to nature language processing (NLP). To overcome the limitations, we employ the rich knowledge embedded in large language models (LLMs) and propose a Backdoor defender powered by LLM Trigger Generator, termed BadLLM-TG. It is optimized through prompt-driven reinforcement learning, using the victim model's feedback loss as the reward signal. The generated triggers are then employed to mitigate the backdoor via adversarial training. Experiments show that our method reduces the attack success rate by 76.2\% on average, outperforming the second-best defender by 13.7.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BadLLM-TG：一种由LLM触发器生成器驱动的后门防御器
后门攻击通过使用触发器操纵输出，危害模型的可靠性。触发器反演可以通过生成器准确定位这些触发器，因此对后门防御至关重要。然而，文本的离散性使得现有的基于噪声的触发器生成器无法应用于自然语言处理（NLP）。为克服这些限制，我们利用大型语言模型（LLMs）中嵌入的丰富知识，提出了一种由LLM触发器生成器驱动的后门防御器，称为BadLLM-TG。它通过基于提示的强化学习进行优化，使用受害模型的反馈损失作为奖励信号。生成的触发器随后用于通过对抗训练减轻后门影响。实验表明，我们的方法平均降低了76.2%的攻击成功率，优于第二名防御器13.7%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enhance model reliability by addressing backdoor attacks that manipulate outputs through triggers. The authors propose a novel approach called BadLLM-TG, which utilizes a large language model (LLM) trigger generator optimized through prompt-driven reinforcement learning, leveraging feedback loss from the victim model as a reward signal. Experimental results demonstrate that this method significantly reduces the attack success rate by an average of 76.2%, outperforming the next best defender by 13.7%.

BrainBench: Exposing the Commonsense Reasoning Gap in Large Language Models
Authors: Yuzhe Tang
First: 2026-03-16T02:50:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T02:50:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) achieve impressive scores on standard benchmarks yet routinely fail questions that any human would answer correctly in seconds. We introduce BrainBench, a benchmark of 100 brainteaser questions spanning 20 carefully designed categories, each targeting a specific commonsense reasoning failure mode in LLMs. Categories range from implicit physical constraints ("Should I walk or drive my rental car to the return lot?") to semantic scope tricks and default assumption hijacks. We evaluate eight frontier models -- four from the Claude family and four from the GPT family -- using a zero-shot protocol with 10 independent runs per question. The best model, Claude Opus 4.6 with extended thinking, achieves only 80.3% accuracy; the worst, GPT-4o, scores 39.7%. Even top-performing models exhibit a 6-16 percentage-point gap between accuracy and consistency, revealing stochastic reasoning. Cross-lingual evaluation in Chinese shows most models degrade by 2-8 percentage points, confirming that these failures reflect reasoning deficits rather than language-specific artifacts. BrainBench provides a fine-grained diagnostic tool for identifying where and why LLMs substitute surface heuristics for genuine commonsense reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BrainBench：揭示大型语言模型中的常识推理差距
大型语言模型（LLMs）在标准基准测试中取得了令人印象深刻的分数，但在任何人都能在几秒钟内正确回答的问题上却常常失败。我们推出了BrainBench，这是一个包含100个脑筋急转弯问题的基准，涵盖20个精心设计的类别，每个类别针对LLMs中特定的常识推理失败模式。类别从隐含的物理约束（“我应该步行还是开租车去还车地点？”）到语义范围技巧和默认假设劫持。我们使用零-shot协议对八个前沿模型进行评估——四个来自Claude家族，四个来自GPT家族，每个问题进行10次独立运行。表现最好的模型Claude Opus 4.6在扩展思维下仅达到80.3%的准确率；表现最差的GPT-4o得分为39.7%。即使是表现最好的模型，准确率和一致性之间也存在6-16个百分点的差距，揭示了随机推理。中文的跨语言评估显示大多数模型下降了2-8个百分点，确认这些失败反映的是推理缺陷，而非语言特定的伪影。BrainBench提供了一种细致的诊断工具，用于识别LLMs在何处以及为何用表面启发式替代真正的常识推理。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the significant gap in commonsense reasoning exhibited by large language models (LLMs), which perform well on standard benchmarks but struggle with basic reasoning tasks. The authors introduce BrainBench, a benchmark consisting of 100 brainteaser questions across 20 categories that target specific reasoning failure modes in LLMs. The evaluation of eight advanced models, including four from the Claude family and four from the GPT family, reveals that even the best-performing model, Claude Opus 4.6, achieves only 80.3% accuracy, while the lowest, GPT-4o, scores 39.7%. Additionally, a notable inconsistency is observed, with a 6-16 percentage-point gap between accuracy and consistency, and cross-lingual tests indicate a 2-8 percentage-point degradation in performance, highlighting that these issues stem from reasoning deficits rather than language-specific problems.
本研究的动机在于解决大型语言模型（LLMs）在常识推理方面存在的显著差距，这些模型在标准基准测试中表现良好，但在基本推理任务上却表现不佳。作者提出了BrainBench，一个包含100个脑筋急转弯问题的基准，涵盖20个旨在揭示LLMs特定推理失败的类别。对包括Claude家族和GPT家族的八个先进模型进行零样本协议评估，结果显示即使是表现最佳的模型Claude Opus 4.6也仅达到80.3%的准确率，而最低的GPT-4o仅得39.7%。此外，观察到6-16个百分点的准确性与一致性差距，跨语言测试表明大多数模型的性能下降2-8个百分点，这表明这些缺陷反映的是根本的推理缺陷，而不仅仅是语言问题。
Self Voice Conversion as an Attack against Neural Audio Watermarking
Authors: Yigitcan Özer, Wanying Ge, Zhe Zhang, Xin Wang, Junichi Yamagishi
First: 2026-01-28T09:41:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-16T02:07:34+00:00
Comments: 7 pages; 2 figures; 2 tables; accepted at IEICE, SP/SLP 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Audio watermarking embeds auxiliary information into speech while maintaining speaker identity, linguistic content, and perceptual quality. Although recent advances in neural and digital signal processing-based watermarking methods have improved imperceptibility and embedding capacity, robustness is still primarily assessed against conventional distortions such as compression, additive noise, and resampling. However, the rise of deep learning-based attacks introduces novel and significant threats to watermark security. In this work, we investigate self voice conversion as a universal, content-preserving attack against audio watermarking systems. Self voice conversion remaps a speaker's voice to the same identity while altering acoustic characteristics through a voice conversion model. We demonstrate that this attack severely degrades the reliability of state-of-the-art watermarking approaches and highlight its implications for the security of modern audio watermarking techniques.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自我声音转换作为对神经音频水印的攻击
音频水印在保持说话者身份、语言内容和感知质量的同时，将辅助信息嵌入语音中。尽管基于神经和数字信号处理的水印方法的最新进展提高了不可感知性和嵌入容量，但其鲁棒性仍主要针对传统失真（如压缩、加性噪声和重采样）进行评估。然而，基于深度学习的攻击的兴起为水印安全性带来了新颖且重大的威胁。在本研究中，我们探讨了自我声音转换作为对音频水印系统的通用、内容保留攻击。自我声音转换通过声音转换模型将说话者的声音重新映射到相同身份，同时改变声学特征。我们证明这种攻击严重降低了最先进水印方法的可靠性，并强调其对现代音频水印技术安全性的影响。

GPM: The Gaussian Pancake Mechanism for Planting Undetectable Backdoors in Differential Privacy
Authors: Haochen Sun, Xi He
First: 2025-09-28T12:14:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T22:15:36+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACM SIGMOD 2026. Please refer to https://github.com/jvhs0706/GPM for code and raw experiment logs
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Differential privacy (DP) has become the gold standard for preserving individual privacy in data analysis. However, an implicit yet fundamental assumption underlying these rigorous privacy guarantees is the correct implementation and execution of DP mechanisms. Several incidents of unintended privacy loss have occurred due to numerical issues and inappropriate configurations of DP software, which have been successfully exploited in privacy attacks. To better understand the seriousness of defective DP software, we ask the following question: is it possible to elevate these passive defects into active privacy attacks while maintaining covertness? To address this question, we present the Gaussian pancake mechanism (GPM), a novel mechanism that is computationally indistinguishable from the widely used Gaussian mechanism (GM), yet exhibits arbitrarily weaker statistical DP guarantees. This unprecedented separation enables a new class of backdoor attacks: by indistinguishably passing off as the authentic GM, GPM can covertly degrade statistical privacy. Unlike the unintentional privacy loss caused by GM's numerical issues, GPM is an adversarial yet undetectable backdoor attack against data privacy. We formally prove GPM's covertness, characterize its statistical leakage, and demonstrate a concrete distinguishing attack that can achieve near-perfect success rates under suitable parameter choices, both theoretically and empirically. Our results underscore the importance of using transparent, open-source DP libraries and highlight the need for rigorous scrutiny and formal verification of DP implementations to prevent subtle, undetectable privacy compromises in real-world systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GPM：用于在差分隐私中植入不可检测后门的高斯煎饼机制
差分隐私（DP）已成为数据分析中保护个人隐私的黄金标准。然而，这些严格隐私保证的一个隐含但基本的假设是DP机制的正确实施和执行。由于数值问题和DP软件的不当配置，已经发生了几起意外的隐私损失事件，这些事件在隐私攻击中被成功利用。为了更好地理解缺陷DP软件的严重性，我们提出以下问题：是否可以将这些被动缺陷提升为主动隐私攻击，同时保持隐蔽性？为了解决这个问题，我们提出了高斯煎饼机制（GPM），这是一种计算上与广泛使用的高斯机制（GM）不可区分的新机制，但表现出任意较弱的统计DP保证。这种前所未有的分离使得一种新的后门攻击类别成为可能：通过不可区分地伪装成真实的GM，GPM可以隐蔽地降低统计隐私。与GM的数值问题导致的无意隐私损失不同，GPM是一种对数据隐私的对抗性但不可检测的后门攻击。我们正式证明了GPM的隐蔽性，表征了其统计泄漏，并展示了一种具体的区分攻击，在适当的参数选择下可以实现近乎完美的成功率，理论上和经验上均如此。我们的结果强调了使用透明、开源DP库的重要性，并突出了对DP实现进行严格审查和形式验证的必要性，以防止现实系统中微妙、不可检测的隐私妥协。

Experimental results demonstrate that GPM can effectively function as a covert backdoor attack, allowing for significant degradation of statistical privacy without detection, and the study emphasizes the necessity for rigorous verification of DP implementations to safeguard against such vulnerabilities.

On Google's SynthID-Text LLM Watermarking System: Theoretical Analysis and Empirical Validation
Authors: Romina Omidi, Yun Dong, Binghui Wang
First: 2026-03-03T17:49:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T16:32:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Google's SynthID-Text, the first ever production-ready generative watermark system for large language model, designs a novel Tournament-based method that achieves the state-of-the-art detectability for identifying AI-generated texts. The system's innovation lies in: 1) a new Tournament sampling algorithm for watermarking embedding, 2) a detection strategy based on the introduced score function (e.g., Bayesian or mean score), and 3) a unified design that supports both distortionary and non-distortionary watermarking methods. This paper presents the first theoretical analysis of SynthID-Text, with a focus on its detection performance and watermark robustness, complemented by empirical validation. For example, we prove that the mean score is inherently vulnerable to increased tournament layers, and design a layer inflation attack to break SynthID-Text. We also prove the Bayesian score offers improved watermark robustness w.r.t. layers and further establish that the optimal Bernoulli distribution for watermark detection is achieved when the parameter is set to 0.5. Together, these theoretical and empirical insights not only deepen our understanding of SynthID-Text, but also open new avenues for analyzing effective watermark removal strategies and designing robust watermarking techniques. Source code is available at https: //github.com/romidi80/Synth-ID-Empirical-Analysis.

Protecting Deep Neural Network Intellectual Property with Chaos-Based White-Box Watermarking
Authors: Sangeeth B, Serena Nicolazzo, Deepa K., Vinod P
First: 2025-12-18T15:26:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T16:21:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid proliferation of deep neural networks (DNNs) across several domains has led to increasing concerns regarding intellectual property (IP) protection and model misuse. Trained DNNs represent valuable assets, often developed through significant investments. However, the ease with which models can be copied, redistributed, or repurposed highlights the urgent need for effective mechanisms to assert and verify model ownership. In this work, we propose an efficient and resilient white-box watermarking framework that embeds ownership information into the internal parameters of a DNN using chaotic sequences. The watermark is generated using a logistic map, a well-known chaotic function, producing a sequence that is sensitive to its initialization parameters. This sequence is injected into the weights of a chosen intermediate layer without requiring structural modifications to the model or degradation in predictive performance. To validate ownership, we introduce a verification process based on a genetic algorithm that recovers the original chaotic parameters by optimizing the similarity between the extracted and regenerated sequences. The effectiveness of the proposed approach is demonstrated through extensive experiments on image classification tasks using MNIST and CIFAR-10 datasets. The results show that the embedded watermark remains detectable after fine-tuning, with negligible loss in model accuracy. In addition to numerical recovery of the watermark, we perform visual analyses using weight density plots and construct activation-based classifiers to distinguish between original, watermarked, and tampered models. Overall, the proposed method offers a flexible and scalable solution for embedding and verifying model ownership in white-box settings well-suited for real-world scenarios where IP protection is critical.

标题：基于混沌的白盒水印保护深度神经网络知识产权

AJF: Adaptive Jailbreak Framework Based on the Comprehension Ability of Black-Box Large Language Models
Authors: Mingyu Yu, Wei Wang, Yanjie Wei, Sujuan Qin, Fei Gao, Wenmin Li
First: 2025-05-29T12:50:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T13:40:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advancements in adversarial jailbreak attacks have exposed critical vulnerabilities in Large Language Models (LLMs), enabling the circumvention of alignment safeguards through increasingly sophisticated prompt manipulations. Our experiments find that the effectiveness of jailbreak strategies is influenced by the comprehension ability of the target LLM. Building on this insight, we propose an Adaptive Jailbreak Framework (AJF) based on the comprehension ability of black-box large language models. Specifically, AJF first categorizes the comprehension ability of the LLM and then applies different strategies accordingly: For models with limited comprehension ability (Type-I LLMs), AJF integrates layered semantic mutations with an encryption technique (MuEn strategy), to more effectively evade the LLM's defenses during the input and inference stages. For models with strong comprehension ability (Type-II LLMs), AJF employs a more complex strategy that builds upon the MuEn strategy by adding an additional layer: inducing the LLM to generate an encrypted response. This forms a dual-end encryption scheme (MuDeEn strategy), further bypassing the LLM's defenses during the output stage. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach, achieving attack success rates of \textbf{98.9\%} on GPT-4o (29 May 2025 release) and \textbf{99.8\%} on GPT-4.1 (8 July 2025 release). Our work contributes to a deeper understanding of the vulnerabilities in current LLMs alignment mechanisms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AJF：基于黑箱大型语言模型理解能力的自适应越狱框架
最近的对抗性越狱攻击的进展暴露了大型语言模型（LLMs）中的关键漏洞，使得通过日益复杂的提示操控绕过对齐保护成为可能。我们的实验发现，越狱策略的有效性受到目标LLM理解能力的影响。基于这一见解，我们提出了一种基于黑箱大型语言模型理解能力的自适应越狱框架（AJF）。具体而言，AJF首先对LLM的理解能力进行分类，然后相应地应用不同的策略：对于理解能力有限的模型（Type-I LLMs），AJF将分层语义变异与加密技术（MuEn策略）结合，以更有效地在输入和推理阶段绕过LLM的防御。对于理解能力强的模型（Type-II LLMs），AJF采用更复杂的策略，在MuEn策略的基础上增加一个额外层：诱导LLM生成加密响应。这形成了一个双端加密方案（MuDeEn策略），进一步绕过LLM在输出阶段的防御。实验结果证明了我们方法的有效性，在GPT-4o（2025年5月29日发布）上实现了98.9%的攻击成功率，在GPT-4.1（2025年7月8日发布）上实现了99.8%的攻击成功率。我们的工作有助于更深入地理解当前LLMs对齐机制中的漏洞。

Guiding Giants: Lightweight Controllers for Weighted Activation Steering in LLMs
Authors: Amr Hegazy, Mostafa Elhoushi, Amr Alanwar
First: 2025-05-22T01:48:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T12:49:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Controlling undesirable Large Language Model (LLM) behaviors, such as the generation of unsafe content or failing to adhere to safety guidelines, often relies on costly fine-tuning. Activation steering provides an alternative for inference-time control, but existing methods typically lack fine-grained, adaptive mechanisms. We introduce a novel approach using a lightweight, trainable controller network integrated during inference. This controller network observes specific intermediate LLM activations and predicts both a global scaling factor and layer-specific weights. The predicted global scaling factor and layer-specific weights then dynamically modulate the intensity of a steering patch, derived from a pre-computed "refusal direction" vector, applied across the LLM's layers during generation. Trained on activations from both harmful and benign prompts, our controller learns to discriminatively apply nuanced, layer-aware interventions, activating steering primarily for harmful inputs. Experiments using safety benchmarks like ToxicChat & In-The-Wild Jailbreak Prompts demonstrate that our weighted steering controller significantly increases refusal rates compared to the base LLM, achieving targeted behavioral modification without altering the original model parameters. Our experiments with Llama-3.1-8B, Llama-3.2-1B & Mistral-7B show our approach outperforms existing methods, presenting an efficient and adaptive method for fine-grained control over LLM behavior at inference time.

标题：引导巨人：用于加权激活引导的轻量级控制器在大型语言模型中的应用
控制大型语言模型（LLM）不良行为，如生成不安全内容或未遵循安全指南，通常依赖于昂贵的微调。激活引导提供了一种推理时控制的替代方案，但现有方法通常缺乏细粒度的自适应机制。我们提出了一种新方法，使用在推理过程中集成的轻量级可训练控制器网络。该控制器网络观察特定的中间LLM激活，并预测全局缩放因子和层特定权重。预测的全局缩放因子和层特定权重动态调节来自预计算的“拒绝方向”向量的引导补丁的强度，该补丁在生成过程中应用于LLM的各层。我们的控制器在有害和良性提示的激活上进行训练，学习以区分性地应用细致的、层感知的干预，主要针对有害输入激活引导。使用ToxicChat和In-The-Wild Jailbreak Prompts等安全基准的实验表明，我们的加权引导控制器显著提高了拒绝率，相较于基础LLM，实现了目标行为修改而不改变原始模型参数。我们与Llama-3.1-8B、Llama-3.2-1B和Mistral-7B的实验表明，我们的方法优于现有方法，提供了一种高效且自适应的细粒度控制LLM行为的推理时方法。

Exposing Long-Tail Safety Failures in Large Language Models through Efficient Diverse Response Sampling
Authors: Suvadeep Hajra, Palash Nandi, Tanmoy Chakraborty
First: 2026-03-15T12:45:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T12:45:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety tuning through supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning from human feedback has substantially improved the robustness of large language models (LLMs). However, it often suppresses rather than eliminates unsafe behaviors, leaving rare but critical failures hidden in the long tail of the output distribution. While most red-teaming work emphasizes adversarial prompt search (input-space optimization), we show that safety failures can also be systematically exposed through diverse response generation (output-space exploration) for a fixed safety-critical prompt, where increasing the number and diversity of sampled responses can drive jailbreak success rates close to unity. To efficiently uncover such failures, we propose Progressive Diverse Population Sampling (PDPS), which combines stochastic token-level sampling with diversity-aware selection to explore a large candidate pool of responses and retain a compact, semantically diverse subset. Across multiple jailbreak benchmarks and open-source LLMs, PDPS achieves attack success rates comparable to large-scale IID sampling while using only 8% to 29% of the computational cost. Under limited-response settings, it improves success rates by 26% to 40% over IID sampling and Diverse Beam Search. Furthermore, responses generated by PDPS exhibit both a higher number and greater diversity of unsafe outputs, demonstrating its effectiveness in uncovering a broader range of failures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过高效多样化响应采样揭示大型语言模型中的长尾安全失败
通过监督微调和人类反馈的强化学习进行安全调优，显著提高了大型语言模型（LLMs）的鲁棒性。然而，它往往抑制而非消除不安全行为，导致在输出分布的长尾中隐藏着稀有但关键的失败。虽然大多数红队工作强调对抗性提示搜索（输入空间优化），我们表明安全失败也可以通过对固定安全关键提示的多样化响应生成（输出空间探索）系统性地揭示，增加采样响应的数量和多样性可以使越狱成功率接近1。为了高效揭示此类失败，我们提出了渐进多样化种群采样（PDPS），它结合了随机令牌级采样和关注多样性的选择，以探索大量候选响应池并保留一个紧凑的、语义多样的子集。在多个越狱基准和开源LLMs中，PDPS实现的攻击成功率可与大规模IID采样相媲美，同时仅使用8%到29%的计算成本。在有限响应设置下，它的成功率比IID采样和多样化束搜索提高了26%到40%。此外，PDPS生成的响应展示了更高数量和更大多样性的unsafe输出，证明了其在揭示更广泛失败方面的有效性。

State-Dependent Safety Failures in Multi-Turn Language Model Interaction
Authors: Pengcheng Li, Jie Zhang, Tianwei Zhang, Han Qiu, Zhang kejun, Weiming Zhang, Nenghai Yu, Wenbo Zhou
First: 2026-03-15T12:13:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T12:13:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment in large language models is typically evaluated under isolated queries, yet real-world use is inherently multi-turn. Although multi-turn jailbreaks are empirically effective, the structure of conversational safety failure remains insufficiently understood. In this work, we study safety failures from a state-space perspective and show that many multi-turn failures arise from structured contextual state evolution rather than isolated prompt vulnerabilities. We introduce STAR, a state-oriented diagnostic framework that treats dialogue history as a state transition operator and enables controlled analysis of safety behavior along interaction trajectories. Rather than optimizing attack strength, STAR provides a principled probe of how aligned models traverse the safety boundary under autoregressive conditioning. Across multiple frontier language models, we find that systems that appear robust under static evaluation can undergo rapid and reproducible safety collapse under structured multi-turn interaction. Mechanistic analysis reveals monotonic drift away from refusal-related representations and abrupt phase transitions induced by role-conditioned context. Together, these findings motivate viewing language model safety as a dynamic, state-dependent process defined over conversational trajectories.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多轮语言模型交互中的状态依赖安全失败
大型语言模型的安全对齐通常在孤立查询下进行评估，但现实世界的使用本质上是多轮的。尽管多轮越狱在经验上有效，但对话安全失败的结构仍然理解不足。在这项工作中，我们从状态空间的角度研究安全失败，并表明许多多轮失败源于结构化的上下文状态演变，而不是孤立的提示脆弱性。我们引入了STAR，一个以状态为导向的诊断框架，将对话历史视为状态转移算子，并能够沿交互轨迹进行安全行为的控制分析。STAR并不是优化攻击强度，而是提供了一个原则性的探测，了解对齐模型在自回归条件下如何穿越安全边界。在多个前沿语言模型中，我们发现，在静态评估下看似稳健的系统在结构化多轮交互中可能会经历快速且可重复的安全崩溃。机制分析揭示了与拒绝相关的表征单调漂移，以及由角色条件上下文引发的突变相变。这些发现共同促使我们将语言模型安全视为一个动态的、状态依赖的过程，定义在对话轨迹上。

A Coin Flip for Safety: LLM Judges Fail to Reliably Measure Adversarial Robustness
Authors: Leo Schwinn, Moritz Ladenburger, Tim Beyer, Mehrnaz Mofakhami, Gauthier Gidel, Stephan Günnemann
First: 2026-02-04T15:13:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T11:52:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Automated \enquote{LLM-as-a-Judge} frameworks have become the de facto standard for scalable evaluation across natural language processing. For instance, in safety evaluation, these judges are relied upon to evaluate harmfulness in order to benchmark the robustness of safety against adversarial attacks. However, we show that existing validation protocols fail to account for substantial distribution shifts inherent to red-teaming: diverse victim models exhibit distinct generation styles, attacks distort output patterns, and semantic ambiguity varies significantly across jailbreak scenarios. Through a comprehensive audit using 6642 human-verified labels, we reveal that the unpredictable interaction of these shifts often causes judge performance to degrade to near random chance. This stands in stark contrast to the high human agreement reported in prior work. Crucially, we find that many attacks inflate their success rates by exploiting judge insufficiencies rather than eliciting genuinely harmful content. To enable more reliable evaluation, we propose ReliableBench, a benchmark of behaviors that remain more consistently judgeable, and JudgeStressTest, a dataset designed to expose judge failures. Data available at: https://github.com/SchwinnL/LLMJudgeReliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：安全的抛硬币：LLM评判者未能可靠地测量对抗鲁棒性
自动化的“LLM作为评判者”框架已成为自然语言处理领域可扩展评估的事实标准。例如，在安全评估中，这些评判者被依赖于评估有害性，以基准测试安全性对抗对抗性攻击的鲁棒性。然而，我们表明，现有的验证协议未能考虑到红队测试固有的重大分布变化：多样的受害者模型表现出不同的生成风格，攻击扭曲输出模式，语义模糊在越狱场景中显著变化。通过对6642个人工验证标签的全面审计，我们揭示了这些变化的不可预测交互常常导致评判者的表现降至接近随机机会。这与先前研究中报告的高人类一致性形成鲜明对比。关键是，我们发现许多攻击通过利用评判者的不足而非引发真正有害的内容来夸大其成功率。为了实现更可靠的评估，我们提出了ReliableBench，一个保持更一致可评判行为的基准，以及JudgeStressTest，一个旨在揭示评判者失败的数据集。数据可在：https://github.com/SchwinnL/LLMJudgeReliability获取。

The authors conducted a comprehensive audit using 6642 human-verified labels to assess the performance of these judges under various distribution shifts that occur during red-teaming. The key findings indicate that the performance of these judges often degrades to near random chance due to unpredictable interactions with diverse victim models and attack patterns, contrasting sharply with previous reports of high human agreement. Additionally, many attacks were found to inflate success rates by exploiting the judges' limitations rather than producing genuinely harmful content, leading to the proposal of ReliableBench and JudgeStressTest to improve evaluation reliability.

Activation Surgery: Jailbreaking White-box LLMs without Touching the Prompt
Authors: Maël Jenny, Jérémie Dentan, Sonia Vanier, Michaël Krajecki
First: 2026-03-15T08:24:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T08:24:38+00:00
Comments: To appear in Proceedings of ESORICS 2026 (Springer LNCS)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Most jailbreak techniques for Large Language Models (LLMs) primarily rely on prompt modifications, including paraphrasing, obfuscation, or conversational strategies. Meanwhile, abliteration techniques (also known as targeted ablations of internal components) have been used to study and explain LLM outputs by probing which internal structures causally support particular responses. In this work, we combine these two lines of research by directly manipulating the model's internal activations to alter its generation trajectory without changing the prompt. Our method constructs a nearby benign prompt and performs layer-wise activation substitutions using a sequential procedure. We show that this activation surgery method reveals where and how refusal arises, and prevents refusal signals from propagating across layers, thereby inhibiting the model's safety mechanisms. Finally, we discuss the security implications for open-weights models and instrumented inference environments.

标题：激活手术：在不触碰提示的情况下破解白盒LLM
大多数针对大型语言模型（LLM）的破解技术主要依赖于提示修改，包括改写、模糊化或对话策略。同时，消融技术（也称为内部组件的有针对性消融）已被用于研究和解释LLM输出，通过探测哪些内部结构因果支持特定响应。在本研究中，我们通过直接操控模型的内部激活来改变其生成轨迹，而不改变提示。我们的方法构建了一个附近的良性提示，并使用顺序程序进行逐层激活替换。我们展示了这种激活手术方法揭示了拒绝产生的地点和方式，并防止拒绝信号在层间传播，从而抑制模型的安全机制。最后，我们讨论了对开放权重模型和仪器化推理环境的安全影响。

本研究的动机在于探索不依赖于提示修改的新方法来破解大型语言模型（LLMs），而现有技术主要依赖于这种修改。作者提出了一种名为激活手术的新方法，通过在保持良性提示的同时进行逐层激活替换来操控模型的内部激活。关键实验结果表明，该方法有效揭示了LLMs中拒绝的内部机制，并防止拒绝信号的传播，从而绕过模型的安全机制，并对开放权重模型和仪器推理环境提出了安全隐患。
EcoAlign: An Economically Rational Framework for Efficient LVLM Alignment
Authors: Ruoxi Cheng, Haoxuan Ma, Teng Ma, Hongyi Zhang
First: 2025-11-14T13:38:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T07:20:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) exhibit powerful reasoning capabilities but suffer sophisticated jailbreak vulnerabilities. Fundamentally, aligning LVLMs is not just a safety challenge but a problem of economic efficiency. Current alignment methods struggle with the trade-off between safety, utility, and operational costs. Critically, a focus solely on final outputs (process-blindness) wastes significant computational budget on unsafe deliberation. This flaw allows harmful reasoning to be disguised with benign justifications, thereby circumventing simple additive safety scores. To address this, we propose EcoAlign, an inference-time framework that reframes alignment as an economically rational search by treating the LVLM as a boundedly rational agent. EcoAlign incrementally expands a thought graph and scores actions using a forward-looking function (analogous to net present value) that dynamically weighs expected safety, utility, and cost against the remaining budget. To prevent deception, path safety is enforced via the weakest-link principle. Extensive experiments across 3 closed-source and 2 open-source models on 6 datasets show that EcoAlign matches or surpasses state-of-the-art safety and utility at a lower computational cost, thereby offering a principled, economical pathway to robust LVLM alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EcoAlign：高效LVLM对齐的经济理性框架
大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）展现出强大的推理能力，但存在复杂的越狱漏洞。从根本上讲，对齐LVLM不仅是安全挑战，也是经济效率问题。目前的对齐方法在安全性、效用和运营成本之间的权衡上存在困难。关键是，单纯关注最终输出（过程盲目性）会在不安全的推理上浪费大量计算预算。这一缺陷使得有害推理可以用良性理由掩盖，从而规避简单的加性安全评分。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了EcoAlign，一个推理时框架，通过将LVLM视为有限理性代理，将对齐重新构建为经济理性的搜索。EcoAlign逐步扩展思维图，并使用前瞻性函数（类似于净现值）对行动进行评分，动态权衡预期安全性、效用和成本与剩余预算。为了防止欺骗，路径安全通过最弱环原则得到保障。在6个数据集上对3个闭源和2个开源模型进行的广泛实验表明，EcoAlign在较低的计算成本下匹配或超越了最先进的安全性和效用，从而提供了一条原则性、经济的稳健LVLM对齐路径。

The authors propose EcoAlign, an inference-time framework that treats LVLMs as boundedly rational agents, allowing for an economically rational search for alignment by incrementally expanding a thought graph and scoring actions based on a forward-looking function that balances safety, utility, and cost. Experimental results demonstrate that EcoAlign achieves comparable or superior safety and utility to existing methods while reducing computational costs across multiple models and datasets.

Faithful Bi-Directional Model Steering via Distribution Matching and Distributed Interchange Interventions
Authors: Yuntai Bao, Xuhong Zhang, Jintao Chen, Ge Su, Yuxiang Cai, Hao Peng, Bing Sun, Haiqin Weng, Liu Yan, Jianwei Yin
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-05T02:51:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T05:50:20+00:00
Comments: camera ready version; 55 pages, 25 figures; accepted for ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Intervention-based model steering offers a lightweight and interpretable alternative to prompting and fine-tuning. However, by adapting strong optimization objectives from fine-tuning, current methods are susceptible to overfitting and often underperform, sometimes generating unnatural outputs. We hypothesize that this is because effective steering requires the faithful identification of internal model mechanisms, not the enforcement of external preferences. To this end, we build on the principles of distributed alignment search (DAS), the standard for causal variable localization, to propose a new steering method: Concept DAS (CDAS). While we adopt the core mechanism of DAS, distributed interchange intervention (DII), we introduce a novel distribution matching objective tailored for the steering task by aligning intervened output distributions with counterfactual distributions. CDAS differs from prior work in two main ways: first, it learns interventions via weak-supervised distribution matching rather than probability maximization; second, it uses DIIs that naturally enable bi-directional steering and allow steering factors to be derived from data, reducing the effort required for hyperparameter tuning and resulting in more faithful and stable control. On AxBench, a large-scale model steering benchmark, we show that CDAS does not always outperform preference-optimization methods but may benefit more from increased model scale. In two safety-related case studies, overriding refusal behaviors of safety-aligned models and neutralizing a chain-of-thought backdoor, CDAS achieves systematic steering while maintaining general model utility. These results indicate that CDAS is complementary to preference-optimization approaches and conditionally constitutes a robust approach to intervention-based model steering. Our code is available at https://github.com/colored-dye/concept_das.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过分布匹配和分布式干预实现忠实的双向模型引导
基于干预的模型引导提供了一种轻量且可解释的替代方案，取代了提示和微调。然而，通过适应微调中的强优化目标，当前方法容易过拟合，且表现不佳，有时生成不自然的输出。我们假设这是因为有效的引导需要忠实识别内部模型机制，而不是强制执行外部偏好。为此，我们基于分布式对齐搜索（DAS）的原则，提出了一种新的引导方法：概念DAS（CDAS）。虽然我们采用DAS的核心机制，即分布式干预（DII），但我们引入了一种新颖的分布匹配目标，旨在通过将干预后的输出分布与反事实分布对齐来满足引导任务。CDAS与之前的工作有两个主要区别：首先，它通过弱监督分布匹配学习干预，而不是概率最大化；其次，它使用自然实现双向引导的DII，并允许从数据中推导引导因素，从而减少超参数调优所需的努力，并实现更忠实和稳定的控制。在AxBench这一大规模模型引导基准上，我们展示了CDAS并不总是优于偏好优化方法，但可能更能从模型规模的增加中受益。在两个与安全相关的案例研究中，覆盖安全对齐模型的拒绝行为和中和链式思维后门，CDAS实现了系统的引导，同时保持了模型的通用性。这些结果表明，CDAS与偏好优化方法是互补的，并在一定条件下构成了一种稳健的基于干预的模型引导方法。我们的代码可在https://github.com/colored-dye/concept_das获取。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to improve intervention-based model steering, which currently suffers from overfitting and unnatural outputs due to reliance on strong optimization objectives. The authors propose a new method called Concept DAS (CDAS), which builds on distributed alignment search principles and introduces a distribution matching objective that aligns intervened output distributions with counterfactual distributions. Experimental results on the AxBench benchmark indicate that while CDAS does not consistently outperform preference-optimization methods, it shows potential benefits with larger model scales and successfully demonstrates systematic steering in safety-related case studies, suggesting it is a complementary approach to existing methods.
本研究解决了当前基于干预的模型引导方法的局限性，这些方法通常因依赖强优化目标而遭受过拟合，并产生不自然的输出。为克服这些挑战，作者提出了一种新的引导方法，称为概念DAS（CDAS），该方法利用分布式对齐搜索原则，并引入了一种分布匹配目标，将输出分布与反事实分布对齐。AxBench基准上的实验结果表明，尽管CDAS并不总是优于偏好优化方法，但在更大模型规模下显示出潜在的好处，并在安全相关的案例研究中成功实现了系统引导，表明其在基于干预的模型引导方法中的互补作用。
Membership Inference for Contrastive Pre-training Models with Text-only PII Queries
Authors: Ruoxi Cheng, Yizhong Ding, Hongyi Zhang, Yiyan Huang
First: 2026-03-15T04:53:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T04:53:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Contrastive pretraining models such as CLIP and CLAP underpin many vision-language and audio-language systems, yet their reliance on web-scale data raises growing concerns about memorizing Personally Identifiable Information (PII). Auditing such models via membership inference is challenging in practice: shadow-model MIAs are computationally prohibitive for large multimodal backbones, and existing multimodal attacks typically require querying the target with paired biometric inputs, thereby directly exposing sensitive biometric information to the target model. We propose Unimodal Membership Inference Detector (UMID), a text-only auditing framework that performs text-guided cross-modal latent inversion and extracts two complementary signals, similarity (alignment to the queried text) and variability (consistency across randomized inversions). UMID compares these statistics to a lightweight non-member reference constructed from synthetic gibberish and makes decisions via an ensemble of unsupervised anomaly detectors. Comprehensive experiments across diverse CLIP and CLAP architectures demonstrate that UMID significantly improves the effectiveness and efficiency over prior MIAs, delivering strong detection performance with sub-second auditing cost while complying with realistic privacy constraints.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于文本的个人身份信息查询的对比预训练模型的成员推断
对比预训练模型如CLIP和CLAP支撑着许多视觉-语言和音频-语言系统，但它们对网络规模数据的依赖引发了对记忆个人身份信息（PII）的日益关注。通过成员推断审计这些模型在实践中具有挑战性：影子模型的成员推断攻击对大型多模态骨干网络计算成本高昂，现有的多模态攻击通常需要用成对的生物特征输入查询目标，从而直接将敏感的生物特征信息暴露给目标模型。我们提出了单模态成员推断检测器（UMID），这是一个仅基于文本的审计框架，执行文本引导的跨模态潜在反演，并提取两个互补信号：相似性（与查询文本的对齐）和变异性（在随机反演中的一致性）。UMID将这些统计数据与从合成无意义文本构建的轻量级非成员参考进行比较，并通过无监督异常检测器的集成做出决策。针对多种CLIP和CLAP架构的全面实验表明，UMID显著提高了相较于先前成员推断攻击的有效性和效率，以亚秒级的审计成本提供强大的检测性能，同时遵循现实的隐私约束。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing concerns regarding the memorization of Personally Identifiable Information (PII) by contrastive pretraining models like CLIP and CLAP, which are widely used in vision-language and audio-language systems. The authors introduce the Unimodal Membership Inference Detector (UMID), a text-only framework that utilizes text-guided cross-modal latent inversion to extract similarity and variability signals for auditing. Experimental results show that UMID outperforms previous membership inference attacks in both effectiveness and efficiency, achieving strong detection performance with sub-second auditing times while adhering to privacy constraints.
本研究关注对比预训练模型（如CLIP和CLAP）在记忆个人身份信息（PII）方面的日益担忧，这些模型广泛应用于视觉语言和音频语言系统。作者提出了一种文本导向的单模态成员推断检测器（UMID），该框架利用文本引导的跨模态潜在反演提取相似性和变异性信号进行审计。实验结果表明，UMID在检测性能和效率上显著优于以往的成员推断攻击，能够在遵循隐私约束的同时实现亚秒级的审计时间。
Safety-Potential Pruning for Enhancing Safety Prompts Against VLM Jailbreaking Without Retraining
Authors: Chongxin Li, Hanzhang Wang, Lian Duan
First: 2026-03-15T04:45:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T04:45:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication in Transactions of the Association for Computational Linguistics (TACL)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety prompts constitute an interpretable layer of defense against jailbreak attacks in vision-language models (VLMs); however, their efficacy is constrained by the models' latent structural responsiveness. We observe that such prompts consistently engage a sparse set of parameters that remain largely quiescent during benign use. This finding motivates the Safety Subnetwork Hypothesis: VLMs embed structurally distinct pathways capable of enforcing safety, but these pathways remain dormant without explicit stimulation. To expose and amplify these pathways, we introduce Safety-Potential Pruning, a one-shot pruning framework that amplifies safety-relevant activations by removing weights that are less responsive to safety prompts without additional retraining. Across three representative VLM architectures and three jailbreak benchmarks, our method reduces attack success rates by up to 22% relative to prompting alone, all while maintaining strong benign performance. These findings frame pruning not only as a model compression technique, but as a structural intervention to emerge alignment-relevant subnets, offering a new path to robust jailbreak resistance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：增强安全提示以防止视觉语言模型（VLM）越狱的安全潜力剪枝，无需重新训练
安全提示构成了对抗视觉语言模型（VLM）越狱攻击的可解释防御层；然而，它们的有效性受到模型潜在结构响应性的限制。我们观察到，这些提示始终涉及一组稀疏的参数，这些参数在正常使用期间大多处于静止状态。这个发现激发了安全子网络假说：VLM嵌入了能够强制执行安全的结构上不同的路径，但这些路径在没有明确刺激的情况下保持休眠。为了揭示和放大这些路径，我们引入了安全潜力剪枝，这是一种一次性剪枝框架，通过去除对安全提示反应较弱的权重来放大与安全相关的激活，而无需额外的重新训练。在三种代表性的VLM架构和三种越狱基准测试中，我们的方法相对于单独提示将攻击成功率降低了多达22%，同时保持强大的正常性能。这些发现将剪枝框架不仅视为模型压缩技术，还视为一种结构干预，以出现与对齐相关的子网络，为强大的越狱抵抗提供了一条新路径。
Summary / 总结
The research is motivated by the need to enhance the effectiveness of safety prompts in vision-language models (VLMs) against jailbreak attacks, as their current performance is limited by the models' structural responsiveness. The authors propose a novel method called Safety-Potential Pruning, which is a one-shot pruning framework designed to amplify safety-related activations by eliminating less responsive weights without requiring retraining. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach can reduce attack success rates by up to 22% compared to using prompts alone, while still preserving strong performance during benign use, thereby highlighting pruning as a viable strategy for improving model safety and robustness against attacks.
本研究的动机在于提高安全提示在视觉语言模型（VLM）中抵御越狱攻击的有效性，而这一有效性受到模型结构响应性的限制。作者提出了一种新方法，称为安全潜力剪枝，这是一种一次性剪枝框架，通过消除对安全提示反应较弱的权重来针对并放大与安全相关的激活，而无需重新训练。实验结果表明，该方法在三种VLM架构和三种越狱基准测试中，能够将攻击成功率降低多达22%，同时在正常使用中仍保持强大的性能，这表明剪枝可以作为改善模型安全性和抵御攻击的结构干预。
KEPo: Knowledge Evolution Poison on Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation
Authors: Qizhi Chen, Chao Qi, Yihong Huang, Muquan Li, Rongzheng Wang, Dongyang Zhang, Ke Qin, Shuang Liang
Venue: WWW 2026
First: 2026-03-12T03:40:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T02:27:17+00:00
Comments: Accepted in the ACM Web Conference 2026 (WWW 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) constructs the Knowledge Graph (KG) from external databases to enhance the timeliness and accuracy of Large Language Model (LLM) generations. However, this reliance on external data introduces new attack surfaces. Attackers can inject poisoned texts into databases to manipulate LLMs into producing harmful target responses for attacker-chosen queries. Existing research primarily focuses on attacking conventional RAG systems. However, such methods are ineffective against GraphRAG. This robustness derives from the KG abstraction of GraphRAG, which reorganizes injected text into a graph before retrieval, thereby enabling the LLM to reason based on the restructured context instead of raw poisoned passages. To expose latent security vulnerabilities in GraphRAG, we propose Knowledge Evolution Poison (KEPo), a novel poisoning attack method specifically designed for GraphRAG. For each target query, KEPo first generates a toxic event containing poisoned knowledge based on the target answer. By fabricating event backgrounds and forging knowledge evolution paths from original facts to the toxic event, it then poisons the KG and misleads the LLM into treating the poisoned knowledge as the final result. In multi-target attack scenarios, KEPo further connects multiple attack corpora, enabling their poisoned knowledge to mutually reinforce while expanding the scale of poisoned communities, thereby amplifying attack effectiveness. Experimental results across multiple datasets demonstrate that KEPo achieves state-of-the-art attack success rates for both single-target and multi-target attacks, significantly outperforming previous methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KEPo：图基检索增强生成中的知识演化毒素
基于图的检索增强生成（GraphRAG）从外部数据库构建知识图谱（KG），以提高大型语言模型（LLM）生成的时效性和准确性。然而，这种对外部数据的依赖引入了新的攻击面。攻击者可以向数据库注入有毒文本，以操纵LLM生成针对攻击者选择的查询的有害目标响应。现有研究主要集中在攻击传统的RAG系统上，但这些方法对GraphRAG无效。这种鲁棒性源于GraphRAG的KG抽象，它在检索之前将注入的文本重组为图，从而使LLM能够基于重构的上下文进行推理，而不是原始的有毒段落。为了揭示GraphRAG中的潜在安全漏洞，我们提出了知识演化毒素（KEPo），这是一种专门为GraphRAG设计的新型毒化攻击方法。对于每个目标查询，KEPo首先生成一个包含有毒知识的有毒事件。通过伪造事件背景和从原始事实到有毒事件的知识演化路径，它随后毒化KG，并误导LLM将有毒知识视为最终结果。在多目标攻击场景中，KEPo进一步连接多个攻击语料库，使其有毒知识相互增强，同时扩大有毒社区的规模，从而放大攻击效果。多个数据集的实验结果表明，KEPo在单目标和多目标攻击中均实现了最先进的攻击成功率，显著优于以前的方法。

The motivation behind this research is to address the security vulnerabilities in Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation (GraphRAG) systems, which enhance Large Language Model (LLM) outputs using external knowledge graphs. The authors propose a novel poisoning attack method called Knowledge Evolution Poison (KEPo) that generates toxic events to manipulate the knowledge graph and mislead the LLM into accepting poisoned information as valid. Experimental results show that KEPo achieves superior attack success rates in both single-target and multi-target scenarios compared to existing methods, highlighting its effectiveness in exploiting the unique structure of GraphRAG.
本研究的动机在于解决图基于检索增强生成（GraphRAG）系统中的安全漏洞，该系统通过外部知识图谱增强大型语言模型（LLM）的输出。作者提出了一种新颖的毒化攻击方法，称为知识演化毒药（KEPo），该方法生成有毒事件并伪造知识演化路径，以操纵知识图谱并误导LLM。实验结果表明，KEPo在单目标和多目标攻击场景中均实现了最先进的成功率，显著优于现有方法。
Secure and Robust Watermarking for AI-generated Images: A Comprehensive Survey
Authors: Jie Cao, Qi Li, Zelin Zhang, Jianbing Ni, Rongxing Lu
First: 2025-09-30T18:59:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-15T02:13:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid progress of Generative Artificial Intelligence (GenAI) has enabled the effortless synthesis of high-quality visual content, while simultaneously raising pressing concerns about intellectual property protection, authenticity, and accountability. Among various countermeasures, watermarking has emerged as a fundamental mechanism for tracing provenance, distinguishing AI-generated images from natural content, and supporting trustworthy digital ecosystems. This paper presents a comprehensive survey of AI-generated image watermarking, systematically reviewing the field from five perspectives: (1) the formalization and fundamental components of image watermarking systems; (2) existing watermarking methodologies and their comparative characteristics; (3) evaluation metrics in terms of visual fidelity, embedding capacity, and detectability; (4) known vulnerabilities under malicious attacks and recent advances in secure and robust watermarking designs; and (5) open challenges, emerging trends, and future research directions. The survey seeks to offer researchers a holistic understanding of watermarking technologies for AI-generated images and to facilitate their continued advancement toward secure and responsible AI-generated content practices.

Shapes are not enough: CONSERVAttack and its use for finding vulnerabilities and uncertainties in machine learning applications
Authors: Philip Bechtle, Lucie Flek, Philipp Alexander Jung, Akbar Karimi, Timo Saala, Alexander Schmidt, Matthias Schott, Philipp Soldin, Christopher Wiebusch, Ulrich Willemsen
First: 2026-03-14T14:53:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T14:53:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In High Energy Physics, as in many other fields of science, the application of machine learning techniques has been crucial in advancing our understanding of fundamental phenomena. Increasingly, deep learning models are applied to analyze both simulated and experimental data. In most experiments, a rigorous regime of testing for physically motivated systematic uncertainties is in place. The numerical evaluation of these tests for differences between the data on the one side and simulations on the other side quantifies the effect of potential sources of mismodelling on the machine learning output. In addition, thorough comparisons of marginal distributions and (linear) feature correlations between data and simulation in "control regions" are applied. However, the guidance by physical motivation, and the need to constrain comparisons to specific regions, does not guarantee that all possible sources of deviations have been accounted for. We therefore propose a new adversarial attack - the CONSERVAttack - designed to exploit the remaining space of hypothetical deviations between simulation and data after the above mentioned tests. The resulting adversarial perturbations are consistent within the uncertainty bounds - evading standard validation checks - while successfully fooling the underlying model. We further propose strategies to mitigate such vulnerabilities and argue that robustness to adversarial effects must be considered when interpreting results from deep learning in particle physics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：形状不足：CONSERVAttack及其在机器学习应用中发现漏洞和不确定性的使用
在高能物理学以及许多其他科学领域，机器学习技术的应用对推动我们对基本现象的理解至关重要。深度学习模型越来越多地被应用于分析模拟和实验数据。在大多数实验中，针对物理动机系统不确定性的严格测试制度已建立。对数据与模拟之间差异的数值评估量化了潜在模型不匹配源对机器学习输出的影响。此外，还对数据和模拟在“控制区域”中的边际分布和（线性）特征相关性进行了全面比较。然而，物理动机的指导以及将比较限制在特定区域的需要，并不能保证所有可能的偏差源都已被考虑。因此，我们提出了一种新的对抗攻击——CONSERVAttack，旨在利用上述测试后模拟与数据之间假设偏差的剩余空间。所产生的对抗扰动在不确定性范围内是一致的——规避了标准验证检查——同时成功欺骗了基础模型。我们进一步提出了减轻此类漏洞的策略，并认为在解释粒子物理学中深度学习的结果时，必须考虑对对抗效应的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结

The authors introduce a novel adversarial attack called CONSERVAttack, which targets the remaining hypothetical deviations between simulated and experimental data that are not captured by existing validation checks. Experimental results demonstrate that the adversarial perturbations generated by CONSERVAttack can successfully deceive deep learning models while remaining consistent within uncertainty bounds, highlighting the need for enhanced robustness measures in interpreting machine learning outcomes in particle physics.

DECEIVE-AFC: Adversarial Claim Attacks against Search-Enabled LLM-based Fact-Checking Systems
Authors: Haoran Ou, Kangjie Chen, Gelei Deng, Hangcheng Liu, Jie Zhang, Tianwei Zhang, Kwok-Yan Lam
First: 2026-01-31T03:49:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T14:37:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fact-checking systems with search-enabled large language models (LLMs) have shown strong potential for verifying claims by dynamically retrieving external evidence. However, the robustness of such systems against adversarial attack remains insufficiently understood. In this work, we study adversarial claim attacks against search-enabled LLM-based fact-checking systems under a realistic input-only threat model. We propose DECEIVE-AFC, an agent-based adversarial attack framework that integrates novel claim-level attack strategies and adversarial claim validity evaluation principles. DECEIVE-AFC systematically explores adversarial attack trajectories that disrupt search behavior, evidence retrieval, and LLM-based reasoning without relying on access to evidence sources or model internals. Extensive evaluations on benchmark datasets and real-world systems demonstrate that our attacks substantially degrade verification performance, reducing accuracy from 78.7% to 53.7%, and significantly outperform existing claim-based attack baselines with strong cross-system transferability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DECEIVE-AFC：针对搜索启用的基于LLM的事实检查系统的对抗性声明攻击
