The authors propose DECEIVE-AFC, an agent-based adversarial attack framework that employs innovative claim-level attack strategies and principles for evaluating adversarial claim validity. Experimental results show that DECEIVE-AFC significantly disrupts the verification performance of these systems, reducing accuracy from 78.7% to 53.7%, and demonstrates superior effectiveness compared to existing claim-based attack methods with notable cross-system transferability.
本研究的动机在于解决对基于搜索的大型语言模型（LLM）事实检查系统在面对对抗性攻击时的鲁棒性理解不足的问题。作者提出了DECEIVE-AFC，这是一种基于代理的对抗性攻击框架，采用了新颖的声明级攻击策略和对抗性声明有效性评估原则。实验结果表明，DECEIVE-AFC显著干扰了这些系统的验证性能，使准确率从78.7%降至53.7%，并展示了强大的跨系统迁移能力，超越了现有的基于声明的攻击方法。
When LoRA Betrays: Backdooring Text-to-Image Models by Masquerading as Benign Adapters
Authors: Liangwei Lyu, Jiaqi Xu, Jianwei Ding, Qiyao Deng
Venue: CVPR 2025
First: 2026-02-25T14:56:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T12:52:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2025 main track
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) has emerged as a leading technique for efficiently fine-tuning text-to-image diffusion models, and its widespread adoption on open-source platforms has fostered a vibrant culture of model sharing and customization. However, the same modular and plug-and-play flexibility that makes LoRA appealing also introduces a broader attack surface. To highlight this risk, we propose Masquerade-LoRA (MasqLoRA), the first systematic attack framework that leverages an independent LoRA module as the attack vehicle to stealthily inject malicious behavior into text-to-image diffusion models. MasqLoRA operates by freezing the base model parameters and updating only the low-rank adapter weights using a small number of "trigger word-target image" pairs. This enables the attacker to train a standalone backdoor LoRA module that embeds a hidden cross-modal mapping: when the module is loaded and a specific textual trigger is provided, the model produces a predefined visual output; otherwise, it behaves indistinguishably from the benign model, ensuring the stealthiness of the attack. Experimental results demonstrate that MasqLoRA can be trained with minimal resource overhead and achieves a high attack success rate of 99.8%. MasqLoRA reveals a severe and unique threat in the AI supply chain, underscoring the urgent need for dedicated defense mechanisms for the LoRA-centric sharing ecosystem.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当LoRA背叛时：通过伪装为良性适配器对文本到图像模型进行后门攻击
低秩适配（LoRA）已成为高效微调文本到图像扩散模型的领先技术，其在开源平台上的广泛应用促进了模型共享和定制的活跃文化。然而，使LoRA具有吸引力的模块化和即插即用灵活性也引入了更广泛的攻击面。为了突出这一风险，我们提出了Masquerade-LoRA（MasqLoRA），这是第一个系统性攻击框架，利用独立的LoRA模块作为攻击载体，悄悄地将恶意行为注入文本到图像扩散模型中。MasqLoRA通过冻结基础模型参数，仅使用少量“触发词-目标图像”对来更新低秩适配器权重。这使得攻击者能够训练一个独立的后门LoRA模块，嵌入一个隐藏的跨模态映射：当模块被加载并提供特定的文本触发时，模型会生成预定义的视觉输出；否则，它的行为与良性模型无异，确保了攻击的隐蔽性。实验结果表明，MasqLoRA可以以最小的资源开销进行训练，并实现99.8%的高攻击成功率。MasqLoRA揭示了AI供应链中的严重且独特的威胁，强调了对LoRA中心共享生态系统专门防御机制的迫切需求。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the security vulnerabilities introduced by the Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) technique in text-to-image diffusion models, which, while facilitating efficient fine-tuning, also expands the attack surface for potential exploitation. The authors propose a novel attack framework called Masquerade-LoRA (MasqLoRA), which utilizes an independent LoRA module to inject malicious behavior into these models by training it with a limited set of 'trigger word-target image' pairs while keeping the base model parameters fixed. Experimental results indicate that MasqLoRA can be effectively trained with minimal resources, achieving a high attack success rate of 99.8%, highlighting a significant threat within the AI supply chain and the necessity for robust defense mechanisms in LoRA-based model sharing environments.
本研究的动机在于低秩适应（LoRA）在微调文本到图像扩散模型中的广泛应用，这虽然带来了好处，但也为恶意利用创造了脆弱性。作者提出了伪装LoRA（MasqLoRA），这是一个系统的攻击框架，利用独立的LoRA模块在这些模型中隐秘地注入后门行为。通过冻结基础模型参数，仅用少量的“触发词-目标图像”对更新低秩适配器权重，该研究发现MasqLoRA可以以99.8%的高攻击成功率实现，且资源需求极低，突显了AI供应链中的重大威胁以及在基于LoRA的系统中改进防御策略的必要性。
Benchmarking the Energy Cost of Assurance in Neuromorphic Edge Robotics
Authors: Sylvester Kaczmarek
First: 2026-03-14T10:31:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T10:31:01+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 4 figures. Accepted and presented at the STEAR 2026 Workshop on Sustainable and Trustworthy Edge AI for Robotics, HiPEAC 2026, Krakow, Poland
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deploying trustworthy artificial intelligence on edge robotics imposes a difficult trade-off between high-assurance robustness and energy sustainability. Traditional defense mechanisms against adversarial attacks typically incur significant computational overhead, threatening the viability of power-constrained platforms in environments such as cislunar space. This paper quantifies the energy cost of assurance in event-driven neuromorphic systems. We benchmark the Hierarchical Temporal Defense (HTD) framework on the BrainChip Akida AKD1000 processor against a suite of adversarial temporal attacks. We demonstrate that unlike traditional deep learning defenses which often degrade efficiency significantly with increased robustness, the event-driven nature of the proposed architecture achieves a superior trade-off. The system reduces gradient-based adversarial success rates from 82.1% to 18.7% and temporal jitter success rates from 75.8% to 25.1%, while maintaining an energy consumption of approximately 45 microjoules per inference. We report a counter-intuitive reduction in dynamic power consumption in the fully defended configuration, attributed to volatility-gated plasticity mechanisms that induce higher network sparsity. These results provide empirical evidence that neuromorphic sparsity enables sustainable and high-assurance edge autonomy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：神经形态边缘机器人中保障的能量成本基准测试
在边缘机器人上部署可信的人工智能在高保障的鲁棒性和能源可持续性之间存在困难的权衡。传统的对抗攻击防御机制通常会产生显著的计算开销，威胁到在如月球间空间等能源受限环境中平台的可行性。本文量化了事件驱动神经形态系统中保障的能量成本。我们在BrainChip Akida AKD1000处理器上基准测试了分层时间防御（HTD）框架，针对一系列对抗性时间攻击。我们证明，与传统深度学习防御机制在提高鲁棒性时通常显著降低效率不同，所提架构的事件驱动特性实现了更优的权衡。该系统将基于梯度的对抗成功率从82.1%降低到18.7%，将时间抖动成功率从75.8%降低到25.1%，同时保持每次推理约45微焦耳的能量消耗。我们报告在完全防御配置中动态功耗的反直觉降低，这归因于波动门控可塑性机制导致的更高网络稀疏性。这些结果提供了实证证据，表明神经形态稀疏性使得可持续和高保障的边缘自主成为可能。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the challenge of balancing high-assurance robustness and energy sustainability in deploying trustworthy AI on edge robotics, particularly in power-constrained environments. The authors benchmark the Hierarchical Temporal Defense (HTD) framework on the BrainChip Akida AKD1000 processor against various adversarial temporal attacks. The findings reveal that the proposed event-driven architecture significantly reduces adversarial success rates while maintaining low energy consumption, achieving a reduction in gradient-based attack success from 82.1% to 18.7% and in temporal jitter success from 75.8% to 25.1%, with an energy cost of approximately 45 microjoules per inference, demonstrating that neuromorphic sparsity can support sustainable and robust edge autonomy.
本研究解决了在边缘机器人上部署可信人工智能时，高保障鲁棒性与能源可持续性之间的平衡挑战，特别是在受限电源环境中。作者在BrainChip Akida AKD1000处理器上对分层时间防御（HTD）框架进行了基准测试，针对各种对抗性时间攻击。研究结果表明，所提出的事件驱动架构显著降低了对抗成功率，同时保持每次推理约45微焦耳的低能耗，证明了神经形态稀疏性能够促进可持续和高保障的边缘自主性。
Inevitable Encounters: Backdoor Attacks Involving Lossy Compression
Authors: Qian Li, Yunuo Chen, Yuntian Chen
First: 2026-03-14T09:45:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T09:45:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real-world backdoor attacks often require poisoned datasets to be stored and transmitted before being used to compromise deep learning systems. However, in the era of big data, the inevitable use of lossy compression poses a fundamental challenge to invisible backdoor attacks. We find that triggers embedded in RGB images often become ineffective after the images are lossily compressed into binary bitstreams (e.g., JPEG files) for storage and transmission. As a result, the poisoned data lose its malicious effect after compression, causing backdoor injection to fail. In this paper, we highlight the necessity of explicitly accounting for the lossy compression process in backdoor attacks. This requires attackers to ensure that the transmitted binary bitstreams preserve malicious trigger information, so that effective triggers can be recovered in the decompressed data. Building on the region-of-interest (ROI) coding mechanism in image compression, we propose two poisoning strategies tailored to inevitable lossy compression. First, we introduce Universal Attack Activation, a universal method that uses sample-specific ROI masks to reactivate trigger information in binary bitstreams for learned image compression (LIC). Second, we present Compression-Adapted Attack, a new attack strategy that employs customized ROI masks to encode trigger information into binary bitstreams and is applicable to both traditional codecs and LIC. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of both strategies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：不可避免的遭遇：涉及有损压缩的后门攻击
现实世界中的后门攻击通常需要将被污染的数据集存储和传输，然后用于破坏深度学习系统。然而，在大数据时代，不可避免的有损压缩对隐形后门攻击构成了根本挑战。我们发现，嵌入在RGB图像中的触发器在图像被有损压缩为二进制比特流（例如JPEG文件）以进行存储和传输后，往往变得无效。因此，被污染的数据在压缩后失去了其恶意效果，导致后门注入失败。本文强调在后门攻击中明确考虑有损压缩过程的必要性。这要求攻击者确保传输的二进制比特流保留恶意触发信息，以便在解压缩数据中恢复有效触发器。基于图像压缩中的感兴趣区域（ROI）编码机制，我们提出了两种针对不可避免的有损压缩的污染策略。首先，我们引入了通用攻击激活，这是一种使用样本特定的ROI掩码来重新激活二进制比特流中触发信息的通用方法，适用于学习图像压缩（LIC）。其次，我们提出了压缩适应攻击，这是一种新的攻击策略，采用定制的ROI掩码将触发信息编码到二进制比特流中，适用于传统编解码器和LIC。大量实验表明这两种策略的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the challenge posed by lossy compression on the effectiveness of backdoor attacks in deep learning systems, as traditional poisoned datasets often lose their malicious triggers after compression. The authors propose two novel poisoning strategies that leverage the region-of-interest coding mechanism in image compression to ensure that trigger information is preserved in binary bitstreams. Experimental results show that both the Universal Attack Activation and Compression-Adapted Attack strategies effectively reactivate and encode trigger information, allowing backdoor attacks to succeed even after the data undergoes lossy compression.
本研究的动机在于解决有损压缩对深度学习系统中后门攻击有效性的挑战，因为在压缩后，受污染数据集中的触发器往往变得无效。作者提出了两种新策略，以确保在压缩过程中恶意触发信息的保留：通用攻击激活，利用特定样本的兴趣区域（ROI）掩码在二进制比特流中重新激活触发器，以及压缩适应攻击，使用定制的ROI掩码对触发器进行编码，适用于各种编解码器。实验结果表明，这两种策略成功地保持了后门攻击的有效性，尽管面临有损压缩的挑战。
Sirens' Whisper: Inaudible Near-Ultrasonic Jailbreaks of Speech-Driven LLMs
Authors: Zijian Ling, Pingyi Hu, Xiuyong Gao, Xiaojing Ma, Man Zhou, Jun Feng, Songfeng Lu, Dongmei Zhang, Bin Benjamin Zhu
First: 2026-03-14T09:01:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T09:01:48+00:00
Comments: USENIX Security'26 Camera-ready
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Speech-driven large language models (LLMs) are increasingly accessed through speech interfaces, introducing new security risks via open acoustic channels. We present Sirens' Whisper (SWhisper), the first practical framework for covert prompt-based attacks against speech-driven LLMs under realistic black-box conditions using commodity hardware. SWhisper enables robust, inaudible delivery of arbitrary target baseband audio-including long and structured prompts-on commodity devices by encoding it into near-ultrasound waveforms that demodulate faithfully after acoustic transmission and microphone nonlinearity. This is achieved through a simple yet effective approach to modeling nonlinear channel characteristics across devices and environments, combined with lightweight channel-inversion pre-compensation. Building on this high-fidelity covert channel, we design a voice-aware jailbreak generation method that ensures intelligibility, brevity, and transferability under speech-driven interfaces. Experiments across both commercial and open-source speech-driven LLMs demonstrate strong black-box effectiveness. On commercial models, SWhisper achieves up to 0.94 non-refusal (NR) and 0.925 specific-convincing (SC). A controlled user study further shows that the injected jailbreak audio is perceptually indistinguishable from background-only playback for human listeners. Although jailbreaks serve as a case study, the underlying covert acoustic channel enables a broader class of high-fidelity prompt-injection and commandexecution attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：海妖的低语：语音驱动的大语言模型的不可听近超声越狱
语音驱动的大语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地通过语音接口访问，这通过开放的声学通道引入了新的安全风险。我们提出了海妖的低语（SWhisper），这是第一个实用框架，用于在现实黑箱条件下对语音驱动的LLMs进行隐蔽的基于提示的攻击，使用普通硬件。SWhisper能够在普通设备上以近超声波形编码任意目标基带音频（包括长且结构化的提示），并在声学传输和麦克风非线性后忠实解调。这是通过一种简单而有效的方法来建模跨设备和环境的非线性通道特性，并结合轻量级的通道反演预补偿实现的。在这个高保真隐蔽通道的基础上，我们设计了一种语音感知的越狱生成方法，确保在语音驱动接口下的可理解性、简洁性和可转移性。对商业和开源语音驱动的LLMs的实验表明了强大的黑箱有效性。在商业模型上，SWhisper达到了最高0.94的非拒绝率（NR）和0.925的特定说服率（SC）。一项受控用户研究进一步表明，注入的越狱音频在听众中与仅播放背景音的感知上没有区别。尽管越狱作为案例研究，但潜在的隐蔽声学通道使得更广泛的高保真提示注入和命令执行攻击成为可能。

The authors present Sirens' Whisper (SWhisper), a novel framework for covert prompt-based attacks against these models under realistic black-box conditions using standard hardware. Experimental results indicate that SWhisper can effectively deliver inaudible audio prompts, achieving up to 0.94 non-refusal and 0.925 specific-convincing rates on commercial models, while a user study confirms that the injected audio is indistinguishable from background noise for listeners, highlighting the potential for broader applications in prompt-injection and command-execution attacks.
本研究的动机是解决通过语音接口访问的语音驱动大型语言模型（LLMs）所带来的新兴安全风险。作者提出了Sirens' Whisper（SWhisper），这是一个针对这些模型的隐蔽提示攻击的实用框架，能够在现实的黑箱条件下使用商品硬件。关键实验结果表明，SWhisper能够实现复杂音频提示的不可闻传递，在商业模型上达到高达0.94的非拒绝率和0.925的特定说服率，而用户研究表明，注入的音频对于人类听众来说与背景噪音无差别，突显了在提示注入和命令执行攻击中更广泛应用的潜力。
Boosting Active Defense Persistence: A Two-Stage Defense Framework Combining Interruption and Poisoning Against Deepfake
Authors: Hongrui Zheng, Yuezun Li, Liejun Wang, Yunfeng Diao, Zhiqing Guo
First: 2025-08-11T09:26:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T08:42:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Active defense strategies have been developed to counter the threat of deepfake technology. However, a primary challenge is their lack of persistence, as their effectiveness is often short-lived. Attackers can bypass these defenses by simply collecting protected samples and retraining their models. This means that static defenses inevitably fail when attackers retrain their models, which severely limits practical use. We argue that an effective defense not only distorts forged content but also blocks the model's ability to adapt, which occurs when attackers retrain their models on protected images. To achieve this, we propose an innovative Two-Stage Defense Framework (TSDF). Benefiting from the intensity separation mechanism designed in this paper, the framework uses dual-function adversarial perturbations to perform two roles. First, it can directly distort the forged results. Second, it acts as a poisoning vehicle that disrupts the data preparation process essential for an attacker's retraining pipeline. By poisoning the data source, TSDF aims to prevent the attacker's model from adapting to the defensive perturbations, thus ensuring the defense remains effective long-term. Comprehensive experiments show that the performance of traditional interruption methods degrades sharply when it is subjected to adversarial retraining. However, our framework shows a strong dual defense capability, which can improve the persistence of active defense. Our code will be available at https://github.com/vpsg-research/TSDF.
中文标题/摘要
标题：增强主动防御持久性：结合中断和毒化的双阶段防御框架对抗深伪技术
主动防御策略已被开发以应对深伪技术的威胁。然而，主要挑战在于其缺乏持久性，因为其有效性往往是短暂的。攻击者可以通过简单地收集受保护样本并重新训练他们的模型来绕过这些防御。这意味着静态防御在攻击者重新训练模型时不可避免地失败，这严重限制了实际使用。我们认为，有效的防御不仅扭曲伪造内容，还阻止模型适应的能力，这发生在攻击者在受保护图像上重新训练模型时。为此，我们提出了一种创新的双阶段防御框架（TSDF）。得益于本文设计的强度分离机制，该框架使用双功能对抗扰动执行两个角色。首先，它可以直接扭曲伪造结果。其次，它充当一种毒化载体，干扰攻击者重新训练流程所需的数据准备过程。通过毒化数据源，TSDF旨在防止攻击者的模型适应防御扰动，从而确保防御在长期内保持有效。综合实验表明，传统中断方法在遭受对抗性重新训练时性能急剧下降。然而，我们的框架显示出强大的双重防御能力，可以提高主动防御的持久性。我们的代码将发布在 https://github.com/vpsg-research/TSDF。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enhance the persistence of active defense strategies against deepfake technology, which are often rendered ineffective when attackers retrain their models using protected samples. The authors propose a Two-Stage Defense Framework (TSDF) that employs dual-function adversarial perturbations to both distort forged content and poison the data preparation process used by attackers. Experimental results demonstrate that while traditional interruption methods significantly lose effectiveness under adversarial retraining, the TSDF maintains strong dual defense capabilities, thereby improving the long-term effectiveness of active defenses against deepfakes.
本研究的动机是增强针对深度伪造技术的主动防御策略的持久性，因为攻击者通过使用受保护样本重新训练模型，往往使这些策略失效。作者提出了一种双阶段防御框架（TSDF），利用双功能对抗扰动来扭曲伪造内容并毒化攻击者的数据准备过程。实验结果表明，传统的中断方法在对抗性重新训练下显著失效，而TSDF表现出强大的双重防御能力，从而提高了针对深度伪造的主动防御的长期有效性。
IdentityGuard: Context-Aware Restriction and Provenance for Personalized Synthesis
Authors: Lingyun Zhang, Yu Xie, Ping Chen
Venue: ICASSP
First: 2026-03-14T08:38:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T08:38:47+00:00
Comments: 5 pages, 3 figures, Accepted to ICASSP
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The nature of personalized text-to-image models poses a unique safety challenge that generic context-blind methods are ill-equipped to handle. Such global filters create a dilemma: to prevent misuse, they are forced to damage the model's broader utility by erasing concepts entirely, causing unacceptable collateral damage.Our work presents a more precisely targeted approach, built on the principle that security should be as context-aware as the threat itself, intrinsically bound to the personalized concept. We present IDENTITYGUARD, which realizes this principle through a conditional restriction that blocks harmful content only when combined with the personalized identity, and a concept-specific watermark for precise traceability. Experiments show our approach prevents misuse while preserving the model's utility and enabling robust traceability. By moving beyond blunt, global filters, our work demonstrates a more effective and responsible path toward AI safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：身份保护：针对个性化合成的上下文感知限制和来源追踪
个性化文本到图像模型的特性带来了独特的安全挑战，通用的无上下文方法难以应对。这类全局过滤器造成了一个困境：为了防止滥用，它们被迫通过完全抹去概念来损害模型的更广泛效用，造成不可接受的附带损害。我们的工作提出了一种更精确的针对性方法，基于安全性应与威胁本身一样具备上下文感知的原则，内在地与个性化概念相绑定。我们提出了IDENTITYGUARD，通过条件限制实现这一原则，仅在与个性化身份结合时阻止有害内容，并使用概念特定的水印实现精确追踪。实验表明，我们的方法在保持模型效用和实现强大追踪能力的同时，防止了滥用。通过超越粗糙的全局过滤器，我们的工作展示了通向AI安全的更有效和负责任的路径。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the safety challenges posed by personalized text-to-image models, which are inadequately managed by generic context-blind methods that can compromise the model's utility. The authors propose IDENTITYGUARD, a method that employs conditional restrictions to block harmful content only when it is associated with a personalized identity, along with a concept-specific watermark for traceability. Experimental results indicate that this approach effectively prevents misuse while maintaining the model's utility and providing robust traceability, thus offering a more responsible solution for AI safety compared to traditional global filters.
本研究的动机在于解决个性化文本到图像模型所带来的安全挑战，而通用的无上下文方法无法有效应对，且可能损害模型的实用性。作者提出了一种名为IDENTITYGUARD的方法，该方法通过条件限制，仅在与个性化身份相关时阻止有害内容，并结合概念特定的水印以实现可追溯性。实验结果表明，该方法有效防止了模型的误用，同时保持了其整体实用性，并提供了强大的内容来源追踪机制。
ImagiNav: Scalable Embodied Navigation via Generative Visual Prediction and Inverse Dynamics
Authors: Jie Chen, Yuxin Cai, Yizhuo Wang, Ruofei Bai, Yuhong Cao, Jun Li, Yau Wei Yun, Guillaume Sartoretti
First: 2026-03-14T08:34:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T08:34:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Enabling robots to navigate open-world environments via natural language is critical for general-purpose autonomy. Yet, Vision-Language Navigation has relied on end-to-end policies trained on expensive, embodiment-specific robot data. While recent foundation models trained on vast simulation data show promise, the challenge of scaling and generalizing due to the limited scene diversity and visual fidelity in simulation persists. To address this gap, we propose ImagiNav, a novel modular paradigm that decouples visual planning from robot actuation, enabling the direct utilization of diverse in-the-wild navigation videos. Our framework operates as a hierarchy: a Vision-Language Model first decomposes instructions into textual subgoals; a finetuned generative video model then imagines the future video trajectory towards that subgoal; finally, an inverse dynamics model extracts the trajectory from the imagined video, which can then be tracked via a low-level controller. We additionally develop a scalable data pipeline of in-the-wild navigation videos auto-labeled via inverse dynamics and a pretrained Vision-Language Model. ImagiNav demonstrates strong zero-shot transfer to robot navigation without requiring robot demonstrations, paving the way for generalist robots that learn navigation directly from unlabeled, open-world data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ImagiNav：通过生成视觉预测和逆动力学实现可扩展的具身导航
使机器人能够通过自然语言在开放世界环境中导航对于通用自主性至关重要。然而，视觉-语言导航依赖于在昂贵的具身特定机器人数据上训练的端到端策略。尽管最近在大量仿真数据上训练的基础模型显示出潜力，但由于仿真中场景多样性和视觉保真度有限，扩展和泛化的挑战依然存在。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了ImagiNav，这是一种新颖的模块化范式，将视觉规划与机器人驱动解耦，能够直接利用多样的野外导航视频。我们的框架作为一个层次结构运行：视觉-语言模型首先将指令分解为文本子目标；经过微调的生成视频模型随后想象朝向该子目标的未来视频轨迹；最后，逆动力学模型从想象的视频中提取轨迹，然后可以通过低级控制器进行跟踪。我们还开发了一个可扩展的数据管道，通过逆动力学和预训练的视觉-语言模型自动标记野外导航视频。ImagiNav展示了强大的零-shot转移到机器人导航，无需机器人演示，为直接从未标记的开放世界数据中学习导航的通用机器人铺平了道路。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enable robots to navigate open-world environments using natural language, addressing the limitations of existing Vision-Language Navigation methods that depend on costly, specific robot data. The authors propose ImagiNav, a modular framework that separates visual planning from robot actuation, utilizing diverse navigation videos from real-world settings. Key experimental findings indicate that ImagiNav achieves effective zero-shot transfer for robot navigation, allowing robots to learn from unlabeled data without the need for prior demonstrations.
本研究的动机是使机器人能够通过自然语言在开放世界环境中导航，解决现有视觉-语言导航方法依赖昂贵特定机器人数据的局限性。作者提出了ImagiNav，一个模块化框架，分离视觉规划与机器人驱动，利用来自现实世界的多样化导航视频。主要实验结果表明，ImagiNav能够有效实现机器人导航的零-shot迁移，无需先前的机器人演示，展示了其开发能够从未标记数据中学习的通用机器人的潜力。
TableMark: A Multi-bit Watermark for Synthetic Tabular Data
Authors: Yuyang Xia, Yaoqiang Xu, Chen Qian, Yang Li, Guoliang Li, Jianhua Feng
First: 2026-03-14T03:01:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T03:01:00+00:00
Comments: 23 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Watermarking has emerged as an effective solution for copyright protection of synthetic data. However, applying watermarking techniques to synthetic tabular data presents challenges, as tabular data can easily lose their watermarks through shuffling or deletion operations. The major challenge is to provide traceability for tracking multiple users of the watermarked tabular data while maintaining high data utility and robustness (resistance to attacks). To address this, we design a multi-bit watermarking scheme TableMark that encodes watermarks into synthetic tabular data, ensuring superior traceability and robustness while maintaining high utility. We formulate the watermark encoding process as a constrained optimization problem, allowing the data owner to effectively trade off robustness and utility. Additionally, we propose effective optimization mechanisms to solve this problem to enhance the data utility. Experimental results on four widely used real-world datasets show that TableMark effectively traces a large number of users, is resilient to attacks, and preserves high utility. Moreover, TableMark significantly outperforms state-of-the-art tabular watermarking schemes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TableMark：一种用于合成表格数据的多比特水印
水印技术已成为合成数据版权保护的有效解决方案。然而，将水印技术应用于合成表格数据面临挑战，因为表格数据在洗牌或删除操作中容易丢失水印。主要挑战是提供可追溯性，以跟踪多个水印表格数据的用户，同时保持高数据效用和鲁棒性（抵抗攻击）。为此，我们设计了一种多比特水印方案TableMark，将水印编码到合成表格数据中，确保优越的可追溯性和鲁棒性，同时保持高效用。我们将水印编码过程形式化为一个约束优化问题，使数据所有者能够有效权衡鲁棒性和效用。此外，我们提出了有效的优化机制来解决此问题，以增强数据效用。在四个广泛使用的真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，TableMark有效追踪大量用户，具有抗攻击能力，并保持高效用。此外，TableMark显著优于最先进的表格水印方案。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to enhance copyright protection for synthetic tabular data through effective watermarking techniques, which face challenges due to the potential loss of watermarks during data manipulation. The authors propose a multi-bit watermarking scheme called TableMark, which encodes watermarks into synthetic tabular data while ensuring traceability and robustness without compromising data utility. Experimental results demonstrate that TableMark can effectively trace numerous users, withstand attacks, and maintain high utility, outperforming existing tabular watermarking methods across four widely used real-world datasets.
本研究的动机在于通过有效的水印技术增强合成表格数据的版权保护，但由于表格数据在洗牌或删除等操作中容易丢失水印，因此面临挑战。作者提出了一种名为TableMark的多比特水印方案，该方案将水印编码到合成表格数据中，同时确保高可追溯性和鲁棒性，并将其形式化为一个约束优化问题，以平衡鲁棒性和效用。实验结果表明，TableMark能够有效追踪大量用户，抵御攻击，并保持高数据效用，且在四个广泛使用的真实数据集上显著优于现有的表格水印方法。
REAEDP: Entropy-Calibrated Differentially Private Data Release with Formal Guarantees and Attack-Based Evaluation
Authors: Bo Ma, Jinsong Wu, Wei Qi Yan
First: 2026-03-14T02:23:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T02:23:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Sensitive data release is vulnerable to output-side privacy threats such as membership inference, attribute inference, and record linkage. This creates a practical need for release mechanisms that provide formal privacy guarantees while preserving utility in measurable ways. We propose REAEDP, a differential privacy framework that combines entropy-calibrated histogram release, a synthetic-data release mechanism, and attack-based evaluation. On the theory side, we derive an explicit sensitivity bound for Shannon entropy, together with an extension to Rényi entropy, for adjacent histogram datasets, enabling calibrated differentially private release of histogram statistics. We further study a synthetic-data mechanism $\mathcal{F}$ with a privacy-test structure and show that it satisfies a formal differential privacy guarantee under the stated parameter conditions. On multiple public tabular datasets, the empirical entropy change remains below the theoretical bound in the tested regime, standard Laplace and Gaussian baselines exhibit comparable trends, and both membership-inference and linkage-style attack performance move toward random-guess behavior as the privacy parameter decreases. These results support REAEDP as a practically usable privacy-preserving release pipeline in the tested settings. Source code: https://github.com/mabo1215/REAEDP.git
中文标题/摘要
标题：REAEDP：具有正式保证和基于攻击评估的熵校准差分隐私数据发布
敏感数据发布容易受到输出侧隐私威胁，如成员推断、属性推断和记录链接。这就需要提供正式隐私保证的发布机制，同时以可测量的方式保持效用。我们提出了REAEDP，一个结合熵校准直方图发布、合成数据发布机制和基于攻击评估的差分隐私框架。在理论方面，我们为香农熵推导了明确的敏感性界限，并扩展到邻近直方图数据集的雷尼熵，从而实现直方图统计的校准差分隐私发布。我们进一步研究了具有隐私测试结构的合成数据机制$\mathcal{F}$，并证明在所述参数条件下满足正式的差分隐私保证。在多个公共表格数据集上，经验熵变化保持在测试范围内的理论界限以下，标准拉普拉斯和高斯基线表现出可比的趋势，且随着隐私参数的降低，成员推断和链接式攻击性能趋向随机猜测行为。这些结果支持REAEDP作为在测试环境中可实际使用的隐私保护发布管道。源代码：https://github.com/mabo1215/REAEDP.git
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the vulnerabilities of sensitive data release to privacy threats such as membership inference and attribute inference, necessitating mechanisms that ensure formal privacy guarantees while maintaining data utility. The authors propose REAEDP, a differential privacy framework that integrates entropy-calibrated histogram release and a synthetic-data release mechanism, supported by attack-based evaluation. Experimental results on various public tabular datasets demonstrate that the empirical entropy change remains within theoretical bounds, standard Laplace and Gaussian methods show similar trends, and the performance of membership-inference and linkage-style attacks approaches random guessing as the privacy parameter decreases, indicating the practical applicability of REAEDP in privacy-preserving data release.
本研究的动机在于解决敏感数据发布面临的隐私威胁，如成员推断和属性推断，因此需要确保正式隐私保证的机制，同时保持数据的实用性。作者提出了REAEDP，这是一种差分隐私框架，结合了熵校准直方图发布和合成数据发布机制，以及基于攻击的评估方法。在多个公共表格数据集上的实验结果表明，经验熵变化保持在理论界限以下，标准的拉普拉斯和高斯基线显示出相似的趋势，并且随着隐私参数的降低，成员推断和链接式攻击的表现接近随机猜测行为，这表明REAEDP在隐私保护数据发布中的实用性。
Malicious Agent Skills in the Wild: A Large-Scale Security Empirical Study
Authors: Yi Liu, Zhihao Chen, Yanjun Zhang, Gelei Deng, Yuekang Li, Jianting Ning, Ying Zhang, Leo Yu Zhang
First: 2026-02-06T09:52:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T01:34:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Third-party agent skills extend LLM-based agents with instruction files and executable code that run on users' machines. Skills execute with user privileges and are distributed through community registries with minimal vetting, but no ground-truth dataset exists to characterize the resulting threats. We construct the first labeled dataset of malicious agent skills by behaviorally verifying 98,380 skills from two community registries, confirming 157 malicious skills with 632 vulnerabilities. These attacks are not incidental. Malicious skills average 4.03 vulnerabilities across a median of three kill chain phases, and the ecosystem has split into two archetypes: Data Thieves that exfiltrate credentials through supply chain techniques, and Agent Hijackers that subvert agent decision-making through instruction manipulation. A single actor accounts for 54.1\% of confirmed cases through templated brand impersonation. Shadow features, capabilities absent from public documentation, appear in 0\% of basic attacks but 100\% of advanced ones; several skills go further by exploiting the AI platform's own hook system and permission flags. Responsible disclosure led to 93.6\% removal within 30 days. We release the dataset and analysis pipeline to support future work on agent skill security.
中文标题/摘要
标题：恶意代理技能的实证研究：大规模安全研究
第三方代理技能通过指令文件和在用户机器上运行的可执行代码扩展基于LLM的代理。技能以用户权限执行，并通过社区注册表分发，审核最小，但没有真实数据集来表征由此产生的威胁。我们通过行为验证来自两个社区注册表的98,380个技能，构建了第一个标记的恶意代理技能数据集，确认了157个恶意技能和632个漏洞。这些攻击并非偶然。恶意技能在三个杀伤链阶段的中位数中平均有4.03个漏洞，生态系统分为两种原型：通过供应链技术窃取凭证的数据窃贼，以及通过指令操控颠覆代理决策的代理劫持者。一个单一的行为者占确认案例的54.1\%，通过模板化品牌冒充。阴影特征，即缺失于公共文档的能力，在基本攻击中出现0\%，但在高级攻击中出现100\%；一些技能进一步利用AI平台自身的钩子系统和权限标志。负责任的披露在30天内导致93.6\%的移除。我们发布数据集和分析管道，以支持未来的代理技能安全研究。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this study is to address the lack of a ground-truth dataset characterizing the threats posed by malicious agent skills that extend LLM-based agents. The researchers constructed the first labeled dataset by behaviorally verifying 98,380 skills from community registries, identifying 157 malicious skills with a total of 632 vulnerabilities. The findings reveal that malicious skills average 4.03 vulnerabilities across three kill chain phases, with two main archetypes identified: Data Thieves and Agent Hijackers. Notably, a single actor was responsible for over half of the confirmed malicious cases, and advanced attacks exhibited shadow features that were not documented publicly. The study also highlights the effectiveness of responsible disclosure, resulting in a high removal rate of malicious skills within 30 days, and the dataset along with the analysis pipeline has been made available for future research on agent skill security.
本研究的动机在于缺乏真实数据集来表征恶意代理技能对基于大型语言模型的代理所构成的威胁。作者通过行为验证来自两个社区注册表的98,380个技能，构建了第一个标记数据集，确认了157个恶意技能和632个漏洞。研究结果显示，恶意技能在三个攻击链阶段中平均存在4.03个漏洞，识别出两种主要类型：数据窃取者和代理劫持者，且一个单一行为者负责超过一半的确认案例。此外，先进攻击利用了影子特征，负责任的披露工作在30天内导致了高达93.6%的恶意技能被移除。数据集和分析管道已公开，以支持未来的代理技能安全研究。
TSDCRF: Balancing Privacy and Multi-Object Tracking via Time-Series CRF and Normalized Control Penalty
Authors: Bo Ma, Jinsong Wu, Weiqi Yan
First: 2026-03-14T00:27:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-14T00:27:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multi-object tracking in video often requires appearance or location cues that can reveal sensitive identity information, while adding privacy-preserving noise typically disrupts cross-frame association and causes ID switches or target loss. We propose TSDCRF, a plug-in refinement framework that balances privacy and tracking by combining three components: (i) $(\varepsilon,δ)$-differential privacy via calibrated Gaussian noise on sensitive regions under a configurable privacy budget; (ii) a Normalized Control Penalty (NCP) that down-weights unstable or conflicting class predictions before noise injection to stabilize association; and (iii) a time-series dynamic conditional random field (DCRF) that enforces temporal consistency and corrects trajectory deviation after noise, mitigating ID switches and resilience to trajectory hijacking. The pipeline is agnostic to the choice of detector and tracker (e.g., YOLOv4 and DeepSORT). We evaluate on MOT16, MOT17, Cityscapes, and KITTI. Results show that TSDCRF achieves a better privacy--utility trade-off than white noise and prior methods (NTPD, PPDTSA): lower KL-divergence shift, lower tracking RMSE, and improved robustness under trajectory hijacking while preserving privacy. Source code in https://github.com/mabo1215/TSDCRF.git
中文标题/摘要
标题：TSDCRF：通过时间序列条件随机场和归一化控制惩罚平衡隐私与多目标跟踪
视频中的多目标跟踪通常需要外观或位置线索，这可能会泄露敏感的身份信息，而添加保护隐私的噪声通常会干扰跨帧关联，导致身份切换或目标丢失。我们提出了TSDCRF，一个插件式的精细化框架，通过结合三个组件来平衡隐私和跟踪：（i）在可配置隐私预算下，通过对敏感区域施加校准的高斯噪声实现的$(\varepsilon,δ)$-差分隐私；（ii）在噪声注入之前，使用归一化控制惩罚（NCP）降低不稳定或冲突的类别预测权重，以稳定关联；（iii）一个时间序列动态条件随机场（DCRF），在噪声后强制执行时间一致性并纠正轨迹偏差，减轻身份切换并增强对轨迹劫持的抵抗力。该管道与检测器和跟踪器的选择无关（例如，YOLOv4和DeepSORT）。我们在MOT16、MOT17、Cityscapes和KITTI上进行了评估。结果表明，TSDCRF在隐私-效用权衡方面优于白噪声和先前的方法（NTPD，PPDTSA）：较低的KL散度偏移，较低的跟踪均方根误差，以及在轨迹劫持下的增强鲁棒性，同时保持隐私。源代码在https://github.com/mabo1215/TSDCRF.git
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this research is to address the challenge of multi-object tracking in video, which often compromises privacy by revealing sensitive identity information through appearance or location cues. The authors propose TSDCRF, a framework that integrates three key components: differential privacy through calibrated Gaussian noise, a Normalized Control Penalty to stabilize predictions, and a time-series dynamic conditional random field to ensure temporal consistency. Experimental results on datasets such as MOT16 and MOT17 demonstrate that TSDCRF provides a superior balance between privacy and tracking performance, achieving lower KL-divergence shift, reduced tracking RMSE, and enhanced resilience against trajectory hijacking compared to existing methods.
本研究的动机是提高视频中的多目标跟踪，同时保护敏感的身份信息，因为传统方法往往会妨碍隐私。作者提出了TSDCRF框架，该框架结合了通过校准高斯噪声实现的差分隐私、用于稳定预测的归一化控制惩罚，以及确保时间一致性的时间序列动态条件随机场。对MOT16和MOT17等数据集的实验结果表明，TSDCRF在隐私和跟踪性能之间提供了更优的平衡，相较于现有方法，达到了更低的KL散度偏移、更小的跟踪均方根误差，并提高了对轨迹劫持的抵抗力。
